## 上班
---
## to go to work
### shàngbān
---
- **definition:** to go to work
- **pinyin:** shàngbān
- **components:**
  - 上
    - shàng
    - to go upward; to attend
  - 班
    - bān
    - shift; duty
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 上 (shàng, "to go upward; to attend") + 班 (bān, "shift; duty") =
    - to go to work
  - **interpretation:** The word 上班 (shàngbān, "to go to work") combines the idea of attending, as in 上 (shàng, "to go upward; to attend"), with a work shift or duty, as indicated by 班 (bān, "shift; duty"). Thus, it literally means to attend one's duty or work shift, which is understood as going to work.
- **examples:**
  - 我早上九点(點)上班。
    - Wǒ zǎoshang jiǔ diǎn shàngbān.
    - I go to work at nine in the morning.
  - 他每天骑(騎)车(車)上班，充满(滿)热(熱)情工作。
    - Tā měitiān qíchē shàngbān, chōngmǎn rèqíng gōngzuò.
    - He rides his bike to work every day and works with great enthusiasm.
  - 她上班前喝杯咖啡。
    - Tā shàngbān qián hē bēi kāfēi.
    - She drinks a cup of coffee before going to work.
### 上班 → 上
- **definition:** to go upward; to attend
- **pinyin:** shàng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line above another line ->
    - indicates 'up'
  - **interpretation:** The character visually represents a line positioned above another, symbolizing upward direction or the concept of being 'on top.' This simplicity highlights its clear graphical indication of elevation or ascension.
- **examples:**
  - 鸟(鳥)儿(兒)飞(飛)上树(樹)梢。
    - Niǎo'ér fēi shàng shù shāo.
    - The birds fly to the treetops.
  - 他把梯子搭上，爬上屋顶(頂)。
    - Tā bǎ tīzi dā shàng, pá shàng wūdǐng.
    - He set the ladder up and climbed onto the roof.
  - 太阳(陽)从(從)东(東)方升上天边(邊)。
    - Tàiyáng cóng dōngfāng shēng shàng tiānbiān.
    - The sun rises from the east and ascends to the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 上](@media/glyph4e0a.png)
### 上班 → 班
- **definition:** shift; duty
- **pinyin:** bān
- **components:**
  - 玨
    - jué
    - pieces of jade
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 玨 (jué, "pieces of jade") + 刀 (dāo, "knife") ->
    - to cut jade into pieces with a knife ->
    - shift; work
  - **interpretation:** The character 班(bān, "shift; work") originally depicted the action of cutting a piece of jade into parts with a knife. Just as jade is divided into smaller parts, work or tasks are divided into shifts or segments, bridging the concept of dividing valuable items and dividing time or tasks.
- **examples:**
  - 我今天的班结(結)束后(後)我们(們)去喝饮(飲)料。
    - Wǒ jīntiān de bān jiéshù hòu wǒmen qù hē yǐnliào.
    - After my shift ends today, we will go for drinks.
  - 他新换(換)了一个(個)班，觉(覺)得很适(適)应(應)。
    - Tā xīn huànle yī gè bān, juéde hěn shìyìng.
    - He has switched to a new shift and feels very adapted to it.
  - 这(這)个(個)班的工作时(時)间(間)很长(長)，但是报(報)酬不错(錯)。
    - Zhège bān de gōngzuò shíjiān hěn cháng, dànshì bàochóu bùcuò.
    - This shift has long working hours, but the pay is good.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 班](@media/glyph73ed.png)
### 上班 → 班 → 玨
- **definition:** pieces of jade
- **pinyin:** jué
- **components:**
  - 玉
    - yù
    - jade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 玉 ('jade') + 玉 ('jade') =
    - duplication of jade ->
    - strings of jade
  - **interpretation:** The character 玨 is an ideogrammic compound formed by the repetition of 玉 (yù, 'jade'), with the two components signifying multiple pieces or strings of jade, representing abundance or multiplicity.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 玨](@media/glyph73a8.png)
### 上班 → 班 → 玨 → 玉
- **definition:** jade
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a picture of a cong (琮), a sort of ritual jade totem ->
    - dot added to differentiate from 王 (wáng, "king") ->
    - final form 玉 (yù, "jade")
  - **interpretation:** The character represents a picture of a jade cong, emphasizing its role in rituals and its cultural significance. The image eventually included a distinguishing dot to ensure clarity from similar characters like 王, underscoring the value jade held as a material in ancient contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 她收到了一个漂亮的玉手镯(鐲)。
    - Tā shōu dào le yī gè piàoliang de yù shǒuzhuó.
    - She received a beautiful jade bracelet.
  - 皇帝的王冠上镶(鑲)嵌着(著)闪(閃)耀的玉石。
    - Huángdì de wángguān shàng xiāngqiànzhe shǎnyào de yùshí.
    - The emperor's crown was inlaid with shining jade stones.
  - 古代的玉器常常被视(視)为(為)珍贵(貴)的艺(藝)术(術)品。
    - Gǔdài de yùqì chángcháng bèi shìwéi zhēnguì de yìshùpǐn.
    - Ancient jade artifacts are often regarded as precious works of art.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 玉](@media/glyph7389.png)
### 上班 → 班 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 刀](@media/glyph5200.png)

## 软(軟)件
---
## software
### ruǎnjiàn
---
- **traditional:** 軟件
- **definition:** software
- **pinyin:** ruǎnjiàn
- **components:**
  - 软(軟)
    - ruǎn
    - soft
  - 件
    - jiàn
    - item; component; piece; part
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 软(軟) (ruǎn, "soft") + 件 (jiàn, "item") =
    - software
  - **interpretation:** The term 软(軟)件 (ruǎnjiàn) is used to contrast the intangible nature of software with the tangible "hardware" of a computer. Here, 软(軟) (ruǎn) refers to the softness or flexibility of the software, in contrast to the solid, physical components of a computer, while 件 (jiàn) denotes an "item" or "component," indicating that it is a part of a larger system.
  - **simplification:** 软(軟) + 件
- **examples:**
  - 我安装(裝)了软(軟)件。
    - Wǒ ānzhuāng le ruǎnjiàn.
    - I installed the software.
  - 这(這)个(個)软(軟)件很实(實)用，帮(幫)助我提高效率。
    - Zhège ruǎnjiàn hěn shíyòng, bāngzhù wǒ tígāo xiàolǜ.
    - This software is very practical and helps me improve efficiency.
  - 使用开(開)源软(軟)件，促进(進)了技术(術)创(創)新。
    - Shǐyòng kāiyuán ruǎnjiàn, cùjìn le jìshù chuàngxīn.
    - Using open source software fosters technological innovation.
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟)
- **traditional:** 軟
- **definition:** soft
- **pinyin:** ruǎn
- **components:**
  - 車
    - chē
    - carriage
  - 耎
    - nuǎn
    - soft; weak
  - 欠
    - qiàn
    - yawn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 車 (carriage) semantic + 耎 (phonetic, sounds like "njon") ->
    - variant with 欠 replaces 耎 ->
    - soft
  - **interpretation:** This character's association with softness may come from the use of wood in carriage construction that is soft enough to be shaped, or the exhaustion associated with operating a heavy carriage. The phonetic component 耎 was replaced with 欠, which depicts exhaustion (a man breathing heavily), fitting the idea of softness as lacking hardness or rigidity.
  - **simplification:** 軟 was simplified to 软(軟) by replacing 車 (chē, "carriage") with 车, a simpler form representing the same meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)张(張)床很软(軟)。
    - Zhè zhāng chuáng hěn ruǎn.
    - This bed is very soft.
  - 她的声(聲)音很柔软(軟)。
    - Tā de shēngyīn hěn róuruǎn.
    - Her voice is very soft.
  - 这(這)种(種)面(麵)包很软(軟)，非常好吃。
    - Zhè zhǒng miànbāo hěn ruǎn, fēicháng hǎochī.
    - This type of bread is very soft and delicious.
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 車
- **definition:** carriage
- **pinyin:** chē
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a carriage viewed from above; wheels on both sides + sun shade on top ->
    - depicted vertically with wheels as strokes and loading area marked by 田 (tián, "field") ->
    - 車
  - **interpretation:** The character 車(chē, "vehicle") originally depicts a carriage from an overhead perspective. The transformation into the vertical form involved simplifying the depiction of wheels and emphasizing the loading area, marked by a field symbol, creating a streamlined pictographic representation.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 車 was simplified to 车 by reducing the number of strokes, maintaining the overall shape of the vehicle but removing intricate details.
- **examples:**
  - 我坐车(車)去上班。
    - Wǒ zuò chē qù shàngbān.
    - I take a car to go to work.
  - 这(這)辆(輛)车(車)很快。
    - Zhè liàng chē hěn kuài.
    - This car is very fast.
  - 我想买(買)一辆(輛)新车(車)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I want to buy a new car.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 車](@media/glyph8eca.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 車 → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民在田里(裡)耕作。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那边(邊)的田长(長)满(滿)了庄(莊)稼，农(農)民收获(穫)忙碌。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋收时(時)节(節)，人们(們)忙于(於)收割田里(裡)的稻谷。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 田](@media/glyph7530.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎
- **definition:** soft; weak
- **pinyin:** nuǎn
- **components:**
  - 需
    - xū
    - need
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Originally the same character as 需 (xū, 'need') during the Han dynasty; diverged into a distinct form for 'soft; weak' ->
    - phono-semantic development
  - **interpretation:** 耎 (ruǎn, 'soft; weak') is a phono-semantic compound that diverged from 需 (xū, 'need') during the Han dynasty, differentiating to express the notion of 'softness' or 'weakness'. It was specifically modified to convey a different meaning while retaining phonetic similarity.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 耎](@media/glyph800e.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需
- **definition:** need
- **pinyin:** xū
- **components:**
  - 天
    - tiān
    - person
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 而
    - ér
    - then
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 天 (tiān, "person") + 雨 (yǔ, "rain") =
    - person getting wet in the rain ->
    - 天 corrupted to 而 (ér) ->
    - final form is 需
  - **interpretation:** The character 需 originally depicted a person getting wet in the rain, showing a need or requirement to stay dry. Over time, 天 (tiān, "person") was replaced by a corrupted form 而 (ér) during the Han dynasty, leading to the modern character.
- **examples:**
  - 学(學)生需努力学(學)习(習)。
    - Xuéshēng xū nǔlì xuéxí.
    - Students must study diligently.
  - 工程师(師)需解决(決)问(問)题(題)，团(團)队(隊)需协(協)同合作。
    - Gōngchéngshī xū jiějué wèntí, tuánduì xū xiétóng hézuò.
    - Engineers need to solve problems, and the team needs to cooperate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 需](@media/glyph9700.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需 → 天
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜幕降临(臨)，天边(邊)星光闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈求天佑众(眾)生。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 天](@media/glyph5929.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需 → 雨
- **definition:** rain
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cloud with drops of rain falling from it ->
    - horizontal stroke added later ->
    - rain
  - **interpretation:** 雨 (yǔ, "rain") visually represents rain falling from a cloud, capturing its essential form.
- **examples:**
  - 今天雨下得很大。
    - Jīntiān yǔ xià de hěn dà.
    - It rained hard today.
  - 他忘记(記)带(帶)伞(傘)，雨却(卻)毫不留情。
    - Tā wàngjì dài sǎn, yǔ què háobù liúqíng.
    - He forgot to bring an umbrella, and the rain showed no mercy.
  - 细(細)雨如丝(絲)，轻(輕)拂着(著)花瓣。
    - Xì yǔ rú sī, qīng fú zhe huā bàn.
    - The fine rain falls like silk, gently brushing the petals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雨](@media/glyph96e8.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需 → 而
- **definition:** then
- **pinyin:** ér
- **components:**
  - 耏
    - ér
    - beard
  - 髵
    - ér
    - beard
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a beard ->
    - original form of 耏 or 髵
  - **interpretation:** The character 而 initially depicted a beard, which shares visual similarities to the concept of 'and then' due to the flow and continuity implied by hair, thus connecting to transitional ideas.
- **examples:**
  - 他努力工作，而他的老板(闆)却(卻)不满(滿)意他的表现(現)。
    - Tā nǔlì gōngzuò, ér tā de lǎobǎn què bù mǎnyì tā de biǎoxiàn.
    - He works hard, yet his boss is not satisfied with his performance.
  - 我很想去旅行，而这(這)次疫情使我无(無)法成行。
    - Wǒ hěn xiǎng qù lǚxíng, ér zhè cì yìqíng shǐ wǒ wúfǎ chéng xíng.
    - I really want to travel, but the pandemic has made it impossible for me.
  - 猫(貓)抓住了小鸟(鳥)，而它却(卻)没(沒)有伤(傷)害它。
    - Māo zhuā zhù le xiǎo niǎo, ér tā què méiyǒu shānghài tā.
    - The cat caught the bird, but it did not harm it.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 而](@media/glyph800c.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需 → 而 → 耏
- **definition:** beard
- **pinyin:** ér
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a person with a stylized beard ->
    - original meaning: beard
  - **interpretation:** The character 耏 (něi) originally depicted the head of a person with a stylized representation of a beard, directly reflecting its meaning related to 'beard'. The pictogram visually conveys the image of facial hair.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 耏](@media/glyph800f.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 耎 → 需 → 而 → 髵
- **definition:** beard
- **pinyin:** ér
- **components:**
  - 髟
    - biāo
    - long hair
  - 兒
    - ér
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 髟 (biāo, "long hair") + phonetic 兒 (ér) ->
    - hair, beard
  - **interpretation:** The character 髵 combines the semantic 髟 (biāo, "long hair"), which conveys the connection to hair or beard, with the phonetic element 兒 (ér), which provides the sound. The combination effectively describes hair or beard, both recurring concepts linked to long hair.
### 软(軟)件 → 软(軟) → 欠
- **definition:** yawn
- **pinyin:** qiàn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person in a bent posture with an open mouth, suggesting the act of yawning or slackening
  - **interpretation:** The character 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") visually represents a person with their mouth open, capturing the physical gesture associated with yawning. It symbolizes a relaxed or tired state.
- **examples:**
  - 他打哈欠。
    - tā dǎ hāqiàn
    - He yawns.
  - 上课(課)时(時)他总(總)是打哈欠，让(讓)老师(師)分心。
    - shàngkè shí tā zǒng shì dǎ hāqiàn, ràng lǎoshī fēnxīn
    - He keeps yawning during class, distracting the teacher.
  - 会(會)议(議)中，他不自觉(覺)地打哈欠。
    - huìyì zhōng, tā bù zìjué dì dǎ hāqiàn
    - During the meeting, he involuntarily yawns.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 欠](@media/glyph6b20.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 件
- **definition:** item; component; piece; part
- **pinyin:** jiàn
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 牛
    - niú
    - cow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 牛 (niú, "cow") =
    - items or parts related to or involving work with animals ->
    - item; component; piece; part
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 人 (rén, "person") and 牛 (niú, "cow") suggests activities or tasks a person might perform with cattle, illustrating the idea of a task or work unit, and thus extending to mean an 'item' or 'component' as a distinct piece of work or object.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)是一件漂亮的衬(襯)衫。
    - Zhè shì yī jiàn piàoliang de chènshān.
    - This is a beautiful shirt.
  - 他每周(週)都会(會)买(買)一件新衣服。
    - Tā měi zhōu dōu huì mǎi yī jiàn xīn yīfú.
    - He buys a new piece of clothing every week.
  - 那是一个(個)重要的项(項)目的一部分。
    - Nà shì yīgè zhòngyào de xiàngmù de yī bùfèn.
    - That is a part of an important project.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 件](@media/glyph4ef6.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 件 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 软(軟)件 → 件 → 牛
- **definition:** cow
- **pinyin:** niú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the head and horns of an ox
  - **interpretation:** The character 牛 (niú, "ox") is a pictogram representing the head and horns of an ox, reflecting its importance in agriculture and daily life in ancient China.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民牵(牽)着(著)牛，去市场(場)买(買)东(東)西。
    - Nóngmín qiānzhe niú，qù shìchǎng mǎi dōngxī。
    - The farmer leads the ox and goes to the market to buy things.
  - 农(農)家养(養)牛，生活更加富足。
    - Nóngjiā yǎng niú，shēnghuó gèngjiā fùzú。
    - Rural families raise oxen, making their lives more prosperous.
  - 这(這)个(個)牛非常听(聽)话(話)。
    - Zhège niú fēicháng tīnghuà。
    - This ox is very obedient.

## 工程师(師)
---
## engineer
### gōngchéngshī
---
- **traditional:** 工程師
- **definition:** engineer
- **pinyin:** gōngchéngshī
- **components:**
  - 工
    - gōng
    - work; craft
  - 程
    - chéng
    - process; journey
  - 师(師)
    - shī
    - teacher; master; expert
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 工 (gōng, "work") + 程 (chéng, "process") + 师(師) (shī, "expert") =
    - engineer
  - **interpretation:** An engineer is someone who is an expert 师(師) (shī, "expert") in the process 程 (chéng, "process") of work 工 (gōng, "work").
- **examples:**
  - 他是一名优(優)秀的工程师(師)。
    - Tā shì yī míng yōuxiù de gōngchéngshī.
    - He is an excellent engineer.
  - 工程师(師)设(設)计(計)建筑(築)，创(創)造未来(來)。
    - Gōngchéngshī shèjì jiànzhú, chuàngzào wèilái.
    - Engineers design buildings, creating the future.
  - 许(許)多人梦(夢)想成为(為)工程师(師)。
    - Xǔduō rén mèngxiǎng chéngwéi gōngchéngshī.
    - Many people dream of becoming an engineer.
### 工程师(師) → 工
- **definition:** work; craft
- **pinyin:** gōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bladed tool to plow the ground and to mark a border, or a carpenter's square
  - **interpretation:** 工 (gōng, "work") represents either a tool used in agriculture for marking or a carpenter's square, reflecting its connection to traditional manual labor and craftsmanship.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天下午去做工。
    - Tā měitiān xiàwǔ qù zuò gōng.
    - He goes to work every afternoon.
  - 工厂(廠)里(裡)的机(機)器不停地运(運)转(轉)。
    - Gōng chǎng lǐ de jīqì bù tíng de yùnzhuǎn.
    - The machines in the factory run nonstop.
  - 这(這)位工人技艺(藝)精湛。
    - Zhè wèi gōngrén jìyì jīngzhàn.
    - This worker is highly skilled.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 工](@media/glyph5de5.png)
### 工程师(師) → 程
- **definition:** process; journey
- **pinyin:** chéng
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 呈
    - chéng
    - to present
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 禾 (grain) + phonetic 呈 (chéng) ->
    - measurements
  - **interpretation:** 禾 (hé, 'grain') is a semantic component related to agriculture and growth, suggesting an ongoing process or series of actions. 呈 (chéng, 'to present') provides the pronunciation. In historical usage, 'measurements' were a necessary part of managing agricultural processes, which is how the concept of 'process' is tied to 程 (chéng, 'process; journey'). The 'grain' implies a progression or journey of growth leading to a final result.
- **examples:**
  - 学(學)习(習)是一段持续(續)的过(過)程。
    - Xuéxí shì yī duàn chíxù de guòchéng.
    - Learning is a continuous process.
  - 我们(們)经(經)过(過)了一段漫长(長)的旅程。
    - Wǒmen jīngguòle yī duàn màncháng de lǚchéng.
    - We went through a long journey.
  - 这(這)次旅行的行程安排得非常紧(緊)凑(湊)。
    - Zhè cì lǚxíng de xíngchéng ānpái dé fēicháng jǐncòu.
    - The itinerary for this trip is very compactly arranged.
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着(著)丰(豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈
- **definition:** to present
- **pinyin:** chéng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 𡈼
    - lǐ
    - unknown
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 𡈼 ->
    - to present
  - **interpretation:** 口 (kǒu, "mouth") suggests speaking or presenting, while 𡈼 provides the pronunciation. The character implies presenting something orally or making it known through speech.
- **examples:**
  - 他在会(會)议(議)上呈交了报(報)告。
    - Tā zài huìyì shàng chéngjiāo le bàogào.
    - He presented the report at the meeting.
  - 天空呈现(現)出晚霞的颜(顏)色。
    - Tiānkōng chéngxiàn chū wǎnxiá de yánsè.
    - The sky presented the colors of the evening glow.
  - 这(這)幅画(畫)呈现(現)出了一种(種)宁(寧)静(靜)的气(氣)氛。
    - Zhè fú huà chéngxiàn chūle yī zhǒng níngjìng de qìfēn.
    - This painting presented a tranquil atmosphere.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 呈](@media/glyph5448.png)
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈 → 𡈼
- **definition:** unknown
- **pinyin:** lǐ
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - soil
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** 亻(human) standing on 土(soil)
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a human figure represented by 亻 standing upon the ground or soil, represented by 土, reflecting the concept of a person in relation to the earth.
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈 → 𡈼 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座城市里(裡)住着(著)很多优(優)秀的人。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.

  - 每个(個)人都有梦(夢)想。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈 → 𡈼 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**

    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.

### 工程师(師) → 程 → 呈 → 𡈼 → 土

- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.

### 工程师(師) → 师(師)
- **traditional:** 師
- **definition:** teacher; master; expert
- **pinyin:** shī
- **components:**
  - 𠂤
    - -
    - mound, hill
  - 帀
    - zā
    - to surround
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠂤 (mound, hill) + 帀 (to surround) =
    - ancient troops stationed at a hill ->
    - leader, master
  - **interpretation:** The character 師 (shī, 'master') combines a depiction of a mound or hill and the idea of surrounding, representing troops stationed around a hill, symbolizing command and leadership. This naturally extends to the concept of a 'master' or 'teacher'.
  - **simplification:** 师(師) simplified by removing additional strokes, preserving phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一位优(優)秀的师(師)。
    - Tā shì yī wèi yōuxiù de shī.
    - He is an excellent master.
  - 学(學)生敬重师(師)，认(認)真求学(學)。
    - Xuéshēng jìngzhòng shī, rènzhēn qiúxué.
    - Students respect their teacher and study diligently.
  - 他拜访(訪)名师(師)，虚(虛)心求教。
    - Tā bàifǎng míng shī, xūxīn qiújiào.
    - He visits a renowned master and earnestly seeks advice.
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 𠂤
- **definition:** mound, hill
- **pinyin:** -
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts hills ->
    - interpreted also as representing buttocks ->
    - in 官, represents multiple rooms under a roof
  - **interpretation:** Depicts hills, a series of mounds or elevations which naturally convey the idea of terrain differences -> metaphorically extended to represent buttocks due to similar curvatures -> further utilized in characters like 官 (guān, 'official') to represent multiple rooms sheltered under a roof.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 𠂤](@media/glyph200a4.png)
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀
- **definition:** to surround
- **pinyin:** zā
- **components:**
  - 之
    - zhī
    - footprint
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 帀 (zā, "to surround") ->
    - inverted 之 (footprint) representing 'surround' sense
  - **interpretation:** The character 帀 (zā, "to surround") is a phono-semantic compound where the component 之, originally written as 㞢, represents a footprint. This indicates the idea of surrounding or encircling with connected steps or pathways, as if forming a boundary or enclosure. This imagery may also allude to the convergence of paths or borders, thus reinforcing the meaning 'to surround.'
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之
- **definition:** footprint
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; the beginning place
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 ('foot') + 一 ('beginning place') ->
    - originally 㞢 ('to go') ->
    - simplified to a point
  - **interpretation:** The original compound 㞢 depicted a foot 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') stepping on a line 一 (yī, 'one; the beginning place'), indicating the concept of 'to go'. The footprint evolving into a point symbolized direction or movement, ultimately abstracted into 之 (zhī, 'of; possessive particle'), representing directionality or connection, as in 'of'.
- **examples:**
  - 天空之蓝(藍)让(讓)人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Tiānkōng zhī lán ràng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the sky makes people feel relaxed and happy.
  - 树(樹)之影在湖面上摇(搖)曳。
    - Shù zhī yǐng zài húmiàn shàng yáoyè.
    - The shadow of the tree sways on the surface of the lake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 之](@media/glyph4e4b.png)
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 工程师(師) → 师(師) → 帀 → 之 → 一
- **definition:** one; the beginning place
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)

## 新

## new
### xīn
---
- **definition:** new
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **components:**
  - 辛
    - xīn
    - bitter
  - 斤
    - jīn
    - axe
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 薪
    - xīn
    - firewood
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 辛 (xīn) + semantic 斤 (jīn, "axe") ->
    - originally "to chop wood"; semantic 木 (mù, "wood") later added ->
    - borrowed for "new"
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted actions associated with chopping wood, with 斤 (jīn, "axe") indicating the semantic idea and 辛 (xīn, "bitter") providing the sound. Over time, the semantic element 木 (mù, "wood") was incorporated in the bronze inscriptions, closely merging with 辛 (xīn, "bitter"). The character later served as a phonetic loan to express the concept of "new," borrowing its sound from 辛 (xīn), as new growth or change often marks the unfamiliar or novel.
- **examples:**
  - 我买(買)了一辆(輛)新车(車)。
    - Wǒ mǎi le yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I bought a new car.
  - 他们(們)搬进(進)了新家。
    - Tāmen bān jìnle xīn jiā.
    - They moved into a new home.
  - 新政策实(實)施后(後)，公司开(開)始发(發)展得更快。
    - Xīn zhèngcè shíshī hòu, gōngsī kāishǐ fāzhǎn de gèng kuài.
    - After the new policy was implemented, the company began to develop faster.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 新](@media/glyph65b0.png)
### 新 → 辛
- **definition:** bitter
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool—chisel or awl—used to mark slaves and criminals ->
    - 辛
  - **interpretation:** The character 辛 (xīn) originally depicted a tool such as a chisel, used for marking or branding. The association with a sharp tool helps explain its extended meaning of 'spice,' as spices can have a pungent, sharp quality reminiscent of a tool's point or effect.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)菜有一种(種)辛辣的味道。
    - Zhège cài yǒu yī zhǒng xīnlà de wèidào.
    - This dish has a spicy taste.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在食物里(裡)添加辛香料。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài shíwù lǐ tiānjiā xīn xiāngliào.
    - He likes to add spices to the food.
  - 这(這)种(種)辛口的调(調)料非常受欢(歡)迎。
    - Zhè zhǒng xīnkǒu de tiáoliào fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of spicy seasoning is very popular.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辛](@media/glyph8f9b.png)
### 新 → 斤
- **definition:** axe
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an axe
  - **interpretation:** The character 斤 (jīn, 'axe') is a pictogram that visually represents an axe. Its shape resembles the tool's blade and handle.
- **examples:**
  - 他拿起一把斤，熟练(練)地劈开(開)木头(頭)。
    - Tā ná qǐ yī bǎ jīn, shú liàn de pī kāi mù tóu.
    - He picked up an axe and skillfully split the firewood.
  - 古人制(製)造精巧的斤，以制(製)作雕刻工具。
    - Gǔ rén zhì zào jīng qiǎo de jīn, yǐ zhì zuò diāo kè gōng jù.
    - In ancient times, people crafted exquisite axes for carving tools.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 斤](@media/glyph65a4.png)
### 新 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 新 → 薪
- **definition:** firewood
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass; vegetation
  - 新
    - xīn
    - new
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, 'grass; vegetation') + phonetic 新 (xīn, 'new') ->
    - firewood
  - **interpretation:** 薪 (xīn, 'firewood') combines the semantic component 艹 (cǎo, 'grass; vegetation'), indicating a plant-related material, with the phonetic 新 (xīn, 'new'), which suggests the pronunciation. This form intuitively links the cutting of fresh plants or wood to create firewood.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)夫每天收集柴薪。
    - Nóngfū měitiān shōují chái xīn.
    - The farmer collects firewood every day.
  - 冬天来(來)临(臨)时(時)，人们(們)需要更多的薪。
    - Dōngtiān láilín shí, rénmen xūyào gèng duō de xīn.
    - When winter arrives, people need more firewood.
  - 他在山上砍了很多薪。
    - Tā zài shānshàng kǎnle hěn duō xīn.
    - He chopped a lot of firewood on the mountain.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 薪](@media/glyph85aa.png)
### 新 → 薪 → 艹
- **definition:** grass; vegetation
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来(來)时(時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.

## 创(創)业(業)公司
---
## startup
### chuàngyè gōngsī
---
- **traditional:** 創業公司
- **definition:** startup
- **pinyin:** chuàngyè gōngsī
- **components:**
  - 创(創)
    - chuàng
    - create
  - 业(業)
    - yè
    - business; industry; work; enterprise
  - 公
    - gōng
    - public; common; official
  - 司
    - sī
    - company; manage; control; conduct
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 創業 combines 創 (chuàng, 'create') and 業 (yè, 'business'), literally forming 'create business'. 公司 combines 公 (gōng, 'public; common') and 司 (sī, 'company; manage'), meaning 'corporation' or 'company'. Together, it refers to a 'startup', emphasizing the act of creating a new business.
  - **interpretation:** 創 (chuàng, 'create') suggests initiating something new, while 業 (yè, 'business') reflects enterprise or undertaking, directly leading to 'entrepreneurship'. The marriage of these concepts underscores the action of founding a business. 公 (gōng, 'public; common') with 司 (sī, 'company; manage') indicates a structured entity concerned with economic activities, thus forming a 'company'. The complete phrase represents a 'startup', a company at its inception stage focusing on innovative and new ventures.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)家创(創)业(業)公司专(專)注于(於)人工智能领(領)域。
    - Zhè jiā chuàngyè gōngsī zhuānzhù yú réngōng zhìnéng lǐngyù.
    - This startup focuses on the field of artificial intelligence.
  - 他决(決)定加入一个(個)创(創)业(業)公司，以积(積)累更多经(經)验(驗)。
    - Tā juédìng jiārù yīgè chuàngyè gōngsī, yǐ jīlěi gèng duō jīngyàn.
    - He decided to join a startup to gain more experience.
  - 许(許)多创(創)业(業)公司都在快速增长(長)。
    - Xǔduō chuàngyè gōngsī dōu zài kuàisù zēngzhǎng.
    - Many startups are experiencing rapid growth.
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創)
- **traditional:** 創
- **definition:** create
- **pinyin:** chuàng
- **components:**
  - 倉
    - cāng
    - granary
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic: 倉 (cāng) + semantic: 刀 (dāo, "knife") =
    - initiate with a knife ->
    - wound or create
  - **interpretation:** The character 创(創) originally signified to initiate something with a knife, symbolizing the act of creating or making a first cut, which is metaphorically extended to mean initiating or starting a new venture.
  - **simplification:** 创 is the simplified form of 創, where the top component '倉' is simplified by removing strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他创(創)办(辦)了一家公司。
    - Tā chuàngbàn le yī jiā gōngsī.
    - He founded a company.
  - 她创(創)意无(無)限，解决(決)了难(難)题(題)。
    - Tā chuàngyì wúxiàn, jiějué le nántí.
    - She has boundless creativity, and she solved a difficult problem.
  - 我们(們)创(創)下了新的记(記)录(錄)。
    - Wǒmen chuàng xià le xīn de jìlù.
    - We set new records.
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉
- **definition:** granary
- **pinyin:** cāng
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - roof
  - 戶
    - hù
    - door
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - pit for storing grain
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (roof) + 戶 (hù, 'door') + 口 (kǒu, 'pit for storing grain') ->
    - depicts a granary
  - **interpretation:** The character 倉 (cāng, 'granary') visually represents a storage structure with a roof, door, and grain pit, illustrating its function as a place for storing grain.
  - **simplification:** The variant 仓(倉) simplified the components and was listed as an 'odd character' in historical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕种(種)，把粮(糧)食存进(進)倉。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzhòng, bǎ liángshí cún jìn cāng.
    - The farmer works hard in the fields, storing the grain in the granary.
  - 君王下令建造倉，储(儲)存战(戰)利品。
    - Jūnwáng xiàlìng jiànzào cāng, chúcún zhànlìpǐn.
    - The king ordered the construction of a granary to store the spoils of war.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 倉](@media/glyph5009.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 亼
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** jī
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入座。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生走入校园(園)，开(開)始新学(學)期。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客走入古城，探索历(歷)史。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 戶
- **definition:** door
- **pinyin:** hù
- **components:**
  - 門
    - mén
    - gate
  - 𠁣
    - unknown
    - unknown
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts one-half of 門 (mén, "gate") ->
    - stylized as 𠁣 ->
    - final form 戶 (hù, "door")
  - **interpretation:** The character 戶 (hù, "door") represents a single door panel, derived from the depiction of half a gate, symbolizing entry or a threshold.
  - **simplification:** 户 is a simplified and variant traditional form of 戶, streamlining the pictorial elements to a more abstract representation, but retaining the symbolic essence of a door or entrance.
- **examples:**
  - 他推开(開)了戶。
    - Tā tuī kāi le hù.
    - He pushed open the door.

    - Yè wǎn jiàng lín shí, gǔ zhái de hù huǎn huǎn kāi qǐ.

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 创(創) → 倉 → 口
- **definition:** pit for storing grain
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.

  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.

    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 业(業)
- **traditional:** 業
- **definition:** business; industry; work; enterprise
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 丵
    - zhuó
    - chisel
  - 大
    - dà
    - person; big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 丵 (chisel) + 大 (person; big) =
    - to launch a great attack
  - **interpretation:** The traditional character 業 represents a large undertaking, depicted by a combination of a chisel and a large person, indicating the effort or work involved in starting a significant task or endeavor.
  - **simplification:** 业 is a simplified form of 業, where the complex structure of 丵 and 大 was replaced with a simpler outline that still suggests structure and action.
- **examples:**
  - 他的事业(業)很成功。
    - Tā de shìyè hěn chénggōng.
    - His career is very successful.
  - 工业(業)发(發)展迅速。
    - Gōngyè fāzhǎn xùnsù.
    - The industrial development is rapid.
  - 她在法律行业(業)工作。
    - Tā zài fǎlǜ hángyè gōngzuò.
    - She works in the legal industry.
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 业(業) → 丵
- **definition:** chisel
- **pinyin:** zhuó
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Derived from 辛 (chisel tool) ->
    - tool for digging
  - **interpretation:** The character 丵 is a pictogram derived from 辛 (xīn, "chisel tool"), representing a tool used for digging. This visual depiction captures the essence of a tool employed for carving or gouging, reflecting its specific association with digging tasks.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 丵](@media/glyph4e35.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 业(業) → 大
- **definition:** person; big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 业(業) → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 公
- **definition:** public; common; official
- **pinyin:** gōng
- **components:**
  - 八
    - bā
    - divide
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - object
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 八 (divide) + 口 (object) =
    - equally dividing objects ->
    - public resources
  - **interpretation:** The character 公(gōng, 'public') is traditionally thought of as representing the opposite of 'private'. While some suggest that 八 represents deviation, this modern interpretation sees 八 as division and 口 as a generic object, together symbolizing the distribution of resources into communal or public property.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)尊重公共设(設)施。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi zūnzhòng gōnggòng shèshī.
    - We should respect public facilities.
  - 这(這)个(個)公园(園)很受当(當)地人的欢(歡)迎。
    - Zhège gōngyuán hěn shòu dāngdì rén de huānyíng.
    - This park is very popular among locals.
  - 她在一家公共图(圖)书(書)馆(館)工作。
    - Tā zài yījiā gōnggòng túshūguǎn gōngzuò.
    - She works at a public library.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 公](@media/glyph516c.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 公 → 八
- **definition:** divide
- **pinyin:** bā
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two bent lines ->
    - originally meant 'to divide' ->
    - borrowed for phonetic similarity to mean 'eight'
  - **interpretation:** The character 八(bā,
- **examples:**
  - 他有八个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Tā yǒu bā gè píngguǒ.
    - He has eight apples.
  - 这(這)只(隻)猫(貓)已经(經)八岁(歲)了。
    - Zhè zhī māo yǐjīng bā suì le.
    - This cat is already eight years old.
  - 我上午八点(點)上班。
    - Wǒ shàngwǔ bā diǎn shàngbān.
    - I start work at eight in the morning.
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 公 → 口
- **definition:** object
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 司
- **definition:** company; manage; control; conduct
- **pinyin:** sī
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth

  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 一 (yī, "one") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - overseeing one's speech or words ->
    - manage
  - **interpretation:** The character 司 (sī, "manage") combines 一 (yī, "one") and 口 (kǒu, "mouth") suggesting the idea of control or direction over speech, symbolizing management or supervision.
- **examples:**
  - 他司图(圖)书(書)馆(館)，井井有条(條)。
    - Tā sī lǐ túshūguǎn, jǐng jǐng yǒu tiáo.
    - He manages the library, keeping it in perfect order.
  - 他亲(親)自司掌全局。
    - Tā qīnzì sī zhǎng quán jú.
    - He personally takes charge of the overall situation.

### 创(創)业(業)公司 → 司 → 一

  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.

    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

## 时(時)间(間)
---
## time
### shíjiān
---
- **traditional:** 時間
- **definition:** time
- **pinyin:** shíjiān
- **components:**
  - 时(時)
    - shí
    - time; season; hour; era
  - 间(間)
    - jiān
    - between; space; room; interval
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The word 時間 (shíjiān, "time") is composed of two morphemes: 時 (shí, "time; season; hour; era") and 間 (jiān, "between; space; room; interval"). In combination, it designates the abstract concept of time as a continuum by which events are sequenced.
  - **interpretation:** 時 (shí, "time; season; hour; era") indicates the specific or cyclical nature of time, like hours or seasons; 間 (jiān, "between; space; room; interval") introduces the concept of a measured span or interval. Together, 時間 (shíjiān) embraces the perception of time as segmented and measurable, like intervals between events, which is essential to understanding history and planning for the future.
- **examples:**
  - 时(時)间(間)过(過)得真快。
    - Shíjiān guò de zhēn kuài.
    - Time passes really quickly.
  - 我们(們)需要更多的时(時)间(間)，才能完成任务(務)。
    - Wǒmen xūyào gèng duō de shíjiān, cái néng wánchéng rènwù.
    - We need more time to complete the task.
  - 现(現)在是时(時)候喝茶了。
    - Xiànzài shì shíhòu hē chá le.
    - Now it's time to drink tea.
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時)
- **traditional:** 時
- **definition:** time; season; hour; era
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun; day
  - 寺
    - sì
    - temple
  - 之
    - zhī
    - governing
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, 'sun; day') as semantic + 寺 as phonetic ->
    - associated with time; ancient form 旹 with 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing'), referring to the passing of time ->
    - over time, 寸 (cùn, 'inch') added to form current 時
  - **interpretation:** The character 時 (shí, 'time; season') stems from the interplay between 日 (rì, 'sun; day'), which signifies the passage of time marked by the sun, and 寺 as the phonetic component capturing the sound. The historical forms show an evolution from 旹, merging 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing') to imply governance over time, to its modern form, where 寸 ('inch') likely emphasizes precision or measurement in the concept of time.
  - **simplification:** In 时 (shí), the component 寺 was retained for phonetic purposes, while 日 (rì, 'sun; day') was simplified to resemble 日 with fewer strokes, streamlining the character.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)相识(識)时(時)，天已经(經)暗了。
    - Wǒmen xiāngshí shí, tiān yǐjīng àn le.
    - When we met, the sky was already dark.
  - 在这(這)样(樣)的时(時)刻，我们(們)需要团(團)结(結)。
    - Zài zhèyàng de shíkè, wǒmen xūyào tuánjié.
    - At such a time, we need to unite.
  - 时(時)光流逝，童年的回忆(憶)依然鲜(鮮)活。
    - Shíguāng liúshì, tóngnián de huíyì yīrán xiānhuó.
    - As time passes, childhood memories remain vivid.
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 日
- **definition:** sun; day
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺
- **definition:** temple
- **pinyin:** sì
- **components:**
  - 𡳿
    - zhī
    - to go; footprint
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 𡳿 ->
    - 之; 士 + semantic 又 (hand) ->
    - 寸 in Small Seal Script ->
    - 寺
  - **interpretation:** 寺(sì, 'temple') combines the semantic element 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), originally from 又 (yòu, 'hand'), to imply precision or holding, with the phonetic element that evolved into 士 (shì, 'scholar'). The phonetic component originally represented going or movement but later took on a more abstract form. This combination suggests a place of order and ritual, characteristic of temples.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天早晨去寺庙(廟)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎochén qù sìmiào.
    - He goes to the temple every morning.
  - 寺庙(廟)里(裡)的钟(鐘)声(聲)非常悠扬(揚)。
    - Sìmiào lǐ de zhōngshēng fēicháng yōuyáng.
    - The bell sounds in the temple are very melodious.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了京都的古老寺庙(廟)，觉(覺)得很平静(靜)。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle Jīngdū de gǔlǎo sìmiào, juéde hěn píngjìng.
    - We visited an ancient temple in Kyoto and felt very peaceful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寺](@media/glyph5bfa.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿
- **definition:** to go; footprint
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - the beginning place
  - 之
    - zhī
    - to go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止(“foot”) + 一(“the beginning place”) ->
    - originally 㞢 ->
    - similar to 出 ->
    - evolved as a variant of 之
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡳿 is a variant of 之 (zhī, "to go") and conveys the idea of movement or direction. The original form 㞢 combines 止 (zhǐ, "foot") representing a footprint with 一 (yī, "the beginning place"), symbolizing the commencement of movement or journey, leading to the meaning of 'to go'. Over time, components such as the footprint evolved into different forms, leading to variants such as 𡳿.
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 一
- **definition:** the beginning place
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 之
- **definition:** to go
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; the beginning place
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 ('foot') + 一 ('beginning place') ->
    - originally 㞢 ('to go') ->
    - simplified to a point
  - **interpretation:** The original compound 㞢 depicted a foot 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') stepping on a line 一 (yī, 'one; the beginning place'), indicating the concept of 'to go'. The footprint evolving into a point symbolized direction or movement, ultimately abstracted into 之 (zhī, 'of; possessive particle'), representing directionality or connection, as in 'of'.
- **examples:**
  - 天空之蓝(藍)让(讓)人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Tiānkōng zhī lán ràng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the sky makes people feel relaxed and happy.
  - 树(樹)之影在湖面上摇(搖)曳。
    - Shù zhī yǐng zài húmiàn shàng yáoyè.
    - The shadow of the tree sways on the surface of the lake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 之](@media/glyph4e4b.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 时(時) → 寺 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数(數)据(據)都准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)
### 时(時)间(間) → 间(間)
- **traditional:** 間
- **definition:** between; space; room; interval
- **pinyin:** jiān
- **components:**
  - 门(門)
    - mén
    - gate
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 門 (mén, "gate") + 日 (rì, "sun") =
    - light peeking through a gate ->
    - space/interval
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 門 (mén, "gate") as the semantic component, suggesting separation or division, with 日 (rì, "sun") as the phonetic component, invoking the image of sunlight streaming through a gap. This evokes the idea of a 'space' or 'interval' as it is visible between two gates or within an enclosure.
  - **simplification:** The simplification reduced the strokes in 日 (rì, "sun") for easier writing, but retained the overall structure.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房间(間)很宽(寬)敞。
    - Zhège fángjiān hěn kuānchǎng.
    - This room is very spacious.
  - 两(兩)间(間)公寓，中间(間)隔着(著)花园(園)。
    - Liǎng jiān gōngyù, zhōngjiān gézhe huāyuán.
    - There are two apartments, with a garden in between.
  - 窗户(戶)和门(門)之间(間)，有个(個)狭(狹)小的空间(間)。
    - Chuānghù hé mén zhījiān, yǒu gè xiáxiǎo de kōngjiān.
    - Between the window and the door, there is a narrow space.
### 时(時)间(間) → 间(間) → 门(門)
- **traditional:** 門
- **definition:** gate
- **pinyin:** mén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 門 (mén, "gate") depicts a gate ->
    - simplified to 门 (mén, "gate")
  - **interpretation:** The character 门(門) (mén, "gate") represents the image of a double-sided gate. It simplifies to 门 but retains the depiction of an entrance or gateway.
  - **simplification:** The character 门 is a simplified form of 門, where the complex structure is replaced by a more straightforward representation while preserving the overall image of a gate.
- **examples:**
  - 学(學)校门(門)前站着(著)一位老师(師)。
    - Xuéxiào mén qián zhànzhe yī wèi lǎoshī(學校門前站著一位老師)。
    - A teacher stands at the school gate.
  - 请(請)你从(從)这(這)扇门(門)进(進)来(來)，把鞋子脱(脫)掉。
    - Qǐng nǐ cóng zhè shàn mén(請你從這扇門) jìnlái(進來)，bǎ xiézi(把鞋子) tuōdiào(脫掉)。
    - Please come in through this door and take off your shoes.
  - 夜深了，只有微弱的光从(從)门(門)缝(縫)里(裡)泄(洩)出。
    - Yè shēn le(夜深了)，zhǐ yǒu wēiruò de guāng cóng mén fèng lǐ xiè chū(只有微弱的光從門縫裡洩出)。
    - It's late at night, and only a faint light seeps through the gap in the door.
### 时(時)间(間) → 间(間) → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)

## 时(時)间(間)
### shíjiān

## time

## 医(醫)生
---
## doctor
### yīshēng
---
- **traditional:** 醫生
- **definition:** doctor
- **pinyin:** yīshēng
- **components:**
  - 医(醫)
    - yī
    - to heal; doctor; medicine
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life; birth; grow; raw
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 醫 (yī, "to heal") + 生 (shēng, "life; birth; grow; raw") =
    - a person who heals life ->
    - doctor
  - **interpretation:** 醫 (yī, "to heal") combines the idea of treating and curing illnesses. 生 (shēng, "life; birth; grow; raw") refers to life and the act of giving life or allowing life to continue. Together, 醫生 (yīshēng, "doctor") conveys the role of a person who heals and restores life, emphasizing the doctor's function to maintain and improve health, thus 'doctor'.
- **examples:**
  - 我想成为(為)一名医(醫)生。
    - Wǒ xiǎng chéngwéi yī míng yīshēng.
    - I want to become a doctor.
  - 医(醫)生给(給)我开(開)了药(藥)。
    - Yīshēng gěi wǒ kāi le yào.
    - The doctor prescribed medicine for me.
  - 这(這)个(個)医(醫)生很有经(經)验(驗)。
    - Zhège yīshēng hěn yǒu jīngyàn.
    - This doctor is very experienced.
### 医(醫)生 → 医(醫)
- **traditional:** 醫
- **definition:** to heal; doctor; medicine
- **pinyin:** yī
- **components:**
  - 匸
    - xì
    - that which hides; that which stores
  - 矢
    - shǐ
    - arrow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 匸 (that which hides) + 矢 (arrow) =
    - a hidden arrow ->
    - metaphor for treating (hidden dangers addressed by medicine)
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the concepts of 'hide' with 'arrow', suggesting the idea of dealing with hidden threats or illnesses, akin to specialized knowledge required for healing.
  - **simplification:** 醫 was simplified by using the right side 耂 (lǎo), an abbreviated structure representing the character.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一名优(優)秀的医(醫)生。
    - Tā shì yì míng yōuxiù de yīshēng.
    - He is an excellent doctor.
  - 我感冒了，需要去医(醫)院。
    - Wǒ gǎnmào le, xūyào qù yīyuàn.
    - I caught a cold and need to go to the hospital.
  - 这(這)家医(醫)院以先进(進)的医(醫)疗(療)技术(術)闻(聞)名。
    - Zhè jiā yīyuàn yǐ xiānjìn de yīliáo jìshù wénmíng.
    - This hospital is famous for its advanced medical technology.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 医](@media/glyph533b.png)
### 医(醫)生 → 医(醫) → 匸
- **definition:** that which hides; that which stores
- **pinyin:** xì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 𠃊 (symbolic graphic) ->
    - depicts an enclosure hiding something or someone ->
    - evolved to represent a concealed space or item
  - **interpretation:** The character 匸(xì, 'box') is a pictogram representing a concealed or enclosed space. Its graphical form suggests something contained or hidden, which aligns with its meaning as a 'box' or an enclosure. Unlike other related pictograms that depict physical containers, 匸 emphasizes the aspect of concealment or secrecy.
- **examples:**
  - 他把匸搬到了房间(間)角落。
    - Tā bǎ xì bān dào le fángjiān jiǎoluò.
    - He moved the box to the corner of the room.
  - 我们(們)在仓(倉)库(庫)找到了匸，里(裡)面装(裝)有秘密文件。
    - Wǒmen zài cāngkù zhǎodào le xì, lǐmiàn zhuāng yǒu mìmì wénjiàn.
    - We found the box in the warehouse, and it contained secret documents.
  - 工厂(廠)工人把旧(舊)匸清理了，然后(後)再利用。
    - Gōngchǎng gōngrén bǎ jiù xì qīnglǐ le, ránhòu zài lìyòng.
    - Factory workers cleaned the old box and then reused it.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 匸](@media/glyph5338.png)
### 医(醫)生 → 医(醫) → 矢
- **definition:** arrow
- **pinyin:** shǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow
  - **interpretation:** The character 矢(shǐ, 'arrow') is a pictogram representing an arrow. Its resemblance to arrows was more evident in ancient script forms.
- **examples:**
  - 他拉开(開)弓，射出一支矢。
    - Tā lā kāi gōng, shè chū yī zhī shǐ.
    - He drew his bow and released an arrow.
  - 古代战(戰)士用矢，攻破敌(敵)阵(陣)。
    - Gǔdài zhànshì yòng shǐ, gōng pò dí zhèn.
    - Ancient warriors used arrows to breach enemy formations.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 矢](@media/glyph77e2.png)
### 医(醫)生 → 生
- **definition:** life; birth; grow; raw
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生命是一场(場)美丽(麗)的旅程。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他在战(戰)场(場)上奋(奮)力生存。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)的生鱼(魚)片非常新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 生](@media/glyph751f.png)
### 医(醫)生 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)

## 医(醫)生
### yīshēng

## doctor
