## 告诉(訴)
---
## to tell
### gàosu
---
- **traditional:** 告訴
- **definition:** to tell
- **pinyin:** gàosu
- **components:**
  - 告
    - gào
    - inform; announce; report
  - 诉(訴)
    - sù
    - complain; tell; relate; express
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 告 (gào, "inform") and 诉(訴) (sù, "complain"). 告 (gào, "inform") refers to conveying information, while 诉(訴) (sù, "complain") involves speaking out or expressing something.
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 告 (gào, "inform") and 诉(訴) (sù, "complain") forms the word for 'tell' by emphasizing the act of communicating something verbally. In this context, 诉(訴) (sù) does not primarily mean to complain but rather to express or communicate, making 告诉(訴) (gàosu) mean 'to tell.'
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)告诉(訴)我。
    - Qǐng gàosu wǒ。
    - Please tell me.
  - 他告诉(訴)我，明天会(會)来(來)。
    - Tā gàosu wǒ, míngtiān huì lái。
    - He told me that he will come tomorrow.
  - 老师(師)告诉(訴)我们(們)，读(讀)书(書)使人进(進)步。
    - Lǎoshī gàosu wǒmen, dúshū shǐ rén jìnbù。
    - The teacher told us that reading makes people progress.
### 告诉(訴) → 告
- **definition:** inform; announce; report
- **pinyin:** gào
- **components:**
  - 壴
    - zhù
    - drum
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 初 (chū, 'initial') depiction unclear ->
    - later interpretations consider abbreviated 壴 (zhù, 'drum') + 口 (kǒu, 'mouth') =
    - drum with open mouth ->
    - 'announce, tell'
  - **interpretation:** The character 告 (gào, 'inform; announce; tell') likely evolved from a depiction related to announcing or informing others using a combination of sound (drum) and speech (mouth). The interpretation of 告 as a drum and mouth aligns with its meaning of announcing or speaking out loud.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)告学(學)生，考试(試)规(規)则(則)已更新。
    - Lǎoshī gào xuéshēng, kǎoshì guīzé yǐ gēngxīn.
    - The teacher informed the students that the exam rules have been updated.
  - 父亲(親)告我，晚上早點回家。
    - Fùqīn gào wǒ, wǎnshàng zǎodiǎn huí jiā.
    - My father informed me to come home early tonight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 告](@media/glyph544a.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 告 → 壴
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** zhù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a drum 壴, with a base and feathers 土 on top ->
    - stylized in the Kangxi radical 鼓
  - **interpretation:** The character 壴 (zhù, "drum") visually represents a drum with two ends, with elements contributing to its structure, such as a base and feathers. It was later incorporated into characters like 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") by adding elements that illustrate additional actions like hands holding a drumstick.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)面壴声(聲)震天动(動)地。
    - Zhè miàn zhù shēng zhèn tiān dòng dì.
    - The sound of this drum shakes the heavens and the earth.
  - 战(戰)士敲响(響)壴，示警敌(敵)人。
    - Zhànshì qiāo xiǎng zhù, shì jǐng dírén.
    - The soldier beats the drum to warn the enemy.
  - 庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式上，祭司击(擊)打壴，宣告传(傳)统(統)。
    - Zhuāngyán yíshì shàng, jìsī jī dǎ zhù, xuānguò chuántǒng.
    - At the solemn ceremony, the priest beats the drum to proclaim tradition.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 壴](@media/glyph58f4.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 告 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴)
- **traditional:** 訴
- **definition:** complain; tell; relate; express
- **pinyin:** sù
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - word, speak
  - 斥
    - chì
    - accuse, blame
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 言 (yán, "word, speak") + 斥 (chì, "accuse, blame") =
    - to accuse verbally ->
    - complain/tell
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 言 (yán, "word, speak") to denote verbal action with 斥 (chì, "accuse, blame") to imply making a complaint or expressing discontent. This reflects the character's meaning of expressing or communicating grievances.
  - **simplification:** Simplified by replacing 訁 (one of the forms of 言) with 讠, which is a more cursive and simplified form.
- **examples:**
  - 她向朋友诉(訴)说(說)烦(煩)恼(惱)。
    - Tā xiàng péngyǒu sùshuō fánnǎo.
    - She confided her troubles to her friend.
  - 他向官员(員)诉(訴)苦，希望得到公正。
    - Tā xiàng guānyuán sùkǔ, xīwàng dédào gōngzhèng.
    - He complained to the officials, hoping to obtain justice.
  - 村民纷(紛)纷(紛)向官府诉(訴)冤。
    - Cūnmín fēnfēn xiàng guānfǔ sùyuān.
    - Villagers urgently appealed to the government to redress their grievances.
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 言
- **definition:** word, speak
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他的言语(語)充满(滿)智慧。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)以行动(動)证(證)明我们(們)的言词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他说(說)话(話)的方式显(顯)示了他的修养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他的舌非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品尝(嚐)美食时(時)，他的舌细(細)品滋味。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他长(長)舌无(無)忌，经(經)常泄露秘密。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥
- **definition:** accuse, blame
- **pinyin:** chì
- **components:**
  - 广(廣)
    - guǎng
    - building
  - 屰
    - nì
    - contrary
  - 干(幹)
    - gān
    - to offend
  - 厂(廣)
    - hǎn
    - cliff
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Originally 㡿: semantic 广 ('building') + phonetic 屰 ('nì') ->
    - 广 simplified to 厂 + 屰 became 干 ->
    - 斥
  - **interpretation:** The original form 㡿 combined 广 (guǎng, 'building') for its meaning with 屰 (nì) for its sound. Over time, 广 was simplified to 厂 (hǎn, 'cliff'), and the character 屰 was replaced by 干 (gān, 'to offend'), leading to the modern form 斥 traditionally associated with openness or exposure, which aligns with the senses of accusing or blaming as an act of openly calling attention to someone's faults.
- **examples:**
  - 他被老板(闆)斥责(責)。
    - Tā bèi lǎobǎn chìzé.
    - He was reprimanded by the boss.
  - 父母常常斥责(責)他不努力。
    - Fùmǔ chángcháng chìzé tā bù nǔlì.
    - His parents often reprimand him for not working hard.
  - 老师(師)斥责(責)学(學)生不遵守纪(紀)律。
    - Lǎoshī chìzé xuéshēng bù zūnshǒu jìlǜ.
    - The teacher reprimanded the students for not following the rules.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 斥](@media/glyph65a5.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** building
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广(廣) (guǎng, "broad") + phonetic 黃 (huáng, "yellow") ->
    - broad
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, "broad") combines the semantic element 广(廣), depicting a broad area or structure, with the phonetic element 黃 (huáng), which lends its sound. This combination signifies the idea of something wide or expansive.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by removing the 黃 (huáng, "yellow") phonetic component, leaving only the semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)河非常广(廣)阔(闊)。
    - Zhè tiáo hé fēicháng guǎngkuò.
    - This river is very broad.
  - 他的知识(識)面很广(廣)，总(總)是能解决(決)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā de zhīshì miàn hěn guǎng, zǒng shì néng jiějué wèntí.
    - His knowledge is broad, and he is always able to solve problems.
  - 在学(學)校里(裡)，他参(參)加了许(許)多广(廣)泛的活动(動)。
    - Zài xuéxiào lǐ, tā cānjiāle xǔduō guǎngfàn de huódòng.
    - At school, he participated in many broad activities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 广](@media/glyph5e7f.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 广(廣) → 廣
- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by retaining the roof radical but removing 黃, simplifying the structure considerably.
- **examples:**
  - 我们正在寻找一个可以提供广(廣)的地方。
    - Wǒmen zhèngzài xúnzhǎo yī gè kěyǐ tígōng guǎng de dìfāng.
    - We are looking for a place that can provide shelter.
  - 那里的广(廣)设施非常完善，适合长时间停留。
    - Nàlǐ de guǎng shèshī fēicháng wánshàn, shìhé cháng shíjiān tíngliú.
    - The shelter facilities there are very complete, suitable for long stays.
  - 如果有恶劣天气，我们需要一个广(廣)来保护自己。
    - Rúguǒ yǒu èliè tiānqì, wǒmen xūyào yī gè guǎng lái bǎohù zìjǐ.
    - If there is bad weather, we need a shelter to protect ourselves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廣](@media/glyph5ee3.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 广(廣) → 廣 → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵花是黄(黃)色的。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋天来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成金黄(黃)色。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.
  - 他穿了一件黄(黃)色的外套。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黃](@media/glyph9ec3.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 屰
- **definition:** contrary
- **pinyin:** nì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an inverted 大 (dà, "big" or "person") ->
    - person upside down ->
    - opposite, backwards, opposing ->
    - original form of 逆 (nì, "go against")
  - **interpretation:** 屰 (nì, "disobedient") originally depicted a person upside down, representing the idea of being opposite or backwards. This inversion symbolizes opposition or non-compliance, aligning with the meaning of disobedience. It served as the original form of 逆 (nì, "go against").
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屰](@media/glyph5c70.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 干
- **definition:** to offend
- **pinyin:** gān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a simple representation of a shield
  - **interpretation:** The character 干(gān, "shield") originally represented a simple depiction of a shield used in ancient Chinese warfare. It visually resembles a shield with a handle in its structure.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士举(舉)起干。
    - Zhànshì jǔ qǐ gān.
    - The warrior raises his shield.
  - 在夜幕降临(臨)时(時)他紧(緊)握干，抵抗敌(敵)人的侵袭(襲)。
    - Zài yèmù jiànglín shí tā jǐnwò gān, dǐkàng dírén de qīn xí.
    - As night falls, he tightly grasps his shield to fend off the enemy's attack.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 干](@media/glyph5e72.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 厂(廠)
- **traditional:** 廠
- **definition:** cliff
- **pinyin:** hǎn
- **components:**
  - 广(廣)
    - guǎng
    - shelter
  - 敞
    - chǎng
    - open; spacious
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (guǎng, "shelter") + phonetic 敞 (chǎng, "open; spacious") ->
    - factory
  - **interpretation:** The character 廠 (chǎng, "factory") combines the semantic element 广 (guǎng, "shelter") with the phonetic element 敞 (chǎng, "open; spacious"), suggesting a large, open building used for production, akin to a factory.
  - **simplification:** 厂 is a simplified form by removing the phonetic component 敞 while retaining the basic shelter concept from 广, streamlining it to represent 'cliff' or 'factory'.
- **examples:**
  - 在高高的山顶(頂)，有一个(個)陡峭的厂(廠)。
    - Zài gāo gāo de shāndǐng, yǒu yī gè dǒu qiào de chǎng.
    - At the top of the tall mountain, there is a steep cliff.
  - 那座厂(廠)看起来(來)很壮(壯)观(觀)。
    - Nà zuò chǎng kàn qǐ lái hěn zhuàng guān.
    - That cliff looks very spectacular.
  - 悬(懸)崖下有一片辽(遼)阔(闊)的海洋。
    - Xuányá xià yǒu yī piàn liáokuò de hǎiyáng.
    - Below the cliff lies a vast ocean.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 厂](@media/glyph5382.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 厂(廠) → 敞
- **definition:** open; spacious
- **pinyin:** chǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - wide, extensive
  - 尚
    - shàng
    - esteem
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (wide, extensive) + phonetic 尚 (shàng) ->
    - open
  - **interpretation:** The character 敞(chǎng, 'open') combines the semantic element 广(廣) (guǎng, 'wide, extensive'), which conveys the idea of an expansive area, with the phonetic component 尚 (shàng), which contributes the sound. The semantic component suggests opening or widening a space, leading to the meaning of 'open'.
- **examples:**
  - 房门(門)敞开(開)着(著)。
    - Fángmén chǎng kāizhe.
    - The door is wide open.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在敞亮的空间(間)工作。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài chǎngliàng de kōngjiān gōngzuò.
    - He likes working in bright, open spaces.
  - 天气(氣)晴朗时(時)，我们(們)在沙滩(灘)上敞开(開)心扉。
    - Tiānqì qínglǎng shí, wǒmen zài shātān shàng chǎngkāi xīnfēi.
    - When the weather is clear, we open our hearts on the beach.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 敞](@media/glyph655e.png)
### 告诉(訴) → 诉(訴) → 斥 → 厂(廠) → 敞 → 尚
- **definition:** esteem
- **pinyin:** shàng
- **components:**
  - 八
    - bā
    - eight
  - 向
    - xiàng
    - face; towards
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 八 (bā, "eight") + phonetic 向 (xiàng, "face; towards") ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 尚(shàng, "esteem") combines 八 (bā, "eight"), which acts as the semantic component, with 向 (xiàng, "face; towards"), which provides the phonetic sound. The sense of moving towards something in 向 supports ideas of ascending or elevating, hence developing into the sense of 'esteem' associated with elevating status or regard.
- **examples:**
  - 他的作风(風)很时(時)尚。
    - Tā de zuòfēng hěn shíshàng.
    - His style is very fashionable.
  - 她总(總)是追求高尚的理想。
    - Tā zǒng shì zhuīqiú gāoshàng de lǐxiǎng.
    - She always pursues noble ideals.
  - 他是一个(個)很有思想的人，大家都很敬仰他。
    - Tā shì yīgè hěn yǒu sīxiǎng de rén, dàjiā dōu hěn jìngyǎng tā.
    - He is a person with great ideas, and everyone esteems him.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 尚](@media/glyph5c1a.png)

## 睡
---
## to sleep
### shuì
---
- **definition:** to sleep
- **pinyin:** shuì
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 垂
    - chuí
    - hang down
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, "eye") + 垂 (chuí, "hang down") =
    - indicative of eyes closed or drooping when sleeping ->
    - sleep
  - **interpretation:** The character 睡(shuì, "to sleep") combines the semantic element 目 (mù, "eye") which is associated with vision, with the phonetic component 垂 (chuí, "hang down"). This suggests an intuitive depiction of eyes closing or drooping as one enters sleep.
- **examples:**
  - 我睡得很好。
    - Wǒ shuì dé hěn hǎo.
    - I sleep well.
  - 夜深了，我迫不及待地想睡觉(覺)。
    - Yè shēn le, wǒ pò bù jí dài de xiǎng shuì jiào.
    - When the night deepens, I can’t wait to go to sleep.
  - 春夜静(靜)谧(謐)时(時)，人们(們)多喜欢(歡)美美地睡上一觉(覺)。
    - Chūn yè jìng mì shí, rénmen duō xǐ huān měi měi de shuì shàng yī jiào.
    - On serene spring nights, people often like to have a good sleep.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 睡](@media/glyph7761.png)
### 睡 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 睡 → 垂
- **definition:** hang down
- **pinyin:** chuí
- **components:**
  - 𠂹
    - n/a
    - depicts hanging flowers
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 𠂹 (depicts hanging flowers) + 土 (tǔ, "earth") ->
    - depicts flowers hanging from a plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 垂 originally illustrated the image of flowers or foliage hanging down from a plant and touching the earth, capturing the concept of 'hang down.'
- **examples:**
  - 晚风(風)拂过(過)树(樹)梢，柳条(條)轻(輕)轻(輕)垂落。
    - Wǎn fēng fú guò shù shāo, liǔ tiáo qīngqīng chuí luò.
    - The evening breeze brushes the treetops, and the willow branches hang down softly.
  - 玉带(帶)般的青藤垂挂(掛)。
    - Yù dài bān de qīng téng chuí guà.
    - The liana, like a jade belt, hangs down.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 垂](@media/glyph5782.png)
### 睡 → 垂 → 𠂹
- **definition:** depicts hanging flowers
- **pinyin:** n/a
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts 𠂹 (hanging element) + 土 (earth) =
    - flowers hanging from a plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠂹 is an ancient form of 垂 (chuí, "hang down") and depicts the image of flowers hanging from a plant. This visualization is directly related to the idea of something drooping or hanging downward, typically from the earth or ground as part of a plant. The incorporation of 土 (tǔ, "earth") suggests the grounding context of the flowers.
### 睡 → 垂 → 𠂹 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 土](@media/glyph571f.png)

## 说(說)
---
## to speak
### shuō
---
- **traditional:** 說
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** shuō
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - speech
  - 兌(兑)
    - duì
    - exchange
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 言 (yán, "speech") + phonetic 兌(兑) (duì, "exchange") =
    - speak or explain through speech ->
    - final meaning "speak"
  - **interpretation:** The character 說 (shuō, "speak") combines the speech radical 言 (yán, "speech") with the phonetic component 兌(兑) (duì, "exchange"), emphasizing verbal communication or the exchange of spoken words.
  - **simplification:** 說 was simplified to 说(說) by replacing the full 言(言, "speech") component with its simplified form 讠(讠, "speech") to streamline writing while maintaining phonetic similarity.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是说(說)诚(誠)实(實)的话(話)。
    - Tā zǒngshì shuō chéngshí de huà.
    - He always speaks honestly.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)说(說)，请(請)你安静(靜)。
    - Māma shuō, qǐng nǐ ānjìng.
    - Mom said, please be quiet.
  - 朋友说(說)，我们(們)该(該)努力工作。
    - Péngyǒu shuō, wǒmen gāi nǔlì gōngzuò.
    - A friend said, we should work hard.
### 说(說) → 言
- **definition:** speech
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他的言语(語)充满(滿)智慧。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)以行动(動)证(證)明我们(們)的言词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他说(說)话(話)的方式显(顯)示了他的修养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 说(說) → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他的舌非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品尝(嚐)美食时(時)，他的舌细(細)品滋味。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他长(長)舌无(無)忌，经(經)常泄露秘密。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 说(說) → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 说(說) → 兌
- **definition:** exchange
- **pinyin:** duì
- **components:**
  - 兄
    - xiōng
    - elder brother
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 卩 (jié, 'kneeling person') + phonetic 兄 (xiōng, 'elder brother') ->
    - standing elder brother ->
    - phonetic element
  - **interpretation:** The character 兌 originally depicts a person with an open mouth and an extended hand, symbolizing an elder brother who speaks or declares. It evolved to a phonetic role in other characters, such as 悅 (yuè, 'delight'), where it also retains the suggestion of expression or declaration, fitting the emotional context.
- **examples:**
  - 他在银(銀)行兌钱(錢)。
    - Tā zài yínháng duì qián.
    - He exchanged money at the bank.
  - 我们(們)可以在这(這)里(裡)兌外币(幣)。
    - Wǒmen kěyǐ zài zhèlǐ duì wàibì.
    - We can exchange foreign currency here.
  - 你需要先去柜(櫃)台(檯)兌票。
    - Nǐ xūyào xiān qù guìtái duì piào.
    - You need to first go to the counter to exchange your ticket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 兌](@media/glyph514c.png)
### 说(說) → 兌 → 兄
- **definition:** elder brother
- **pinyin:** xiōng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 儿
    - ér
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + 儿 (ér, "child") =
    - giving orders ->
    - elder brother
  - **interpretation:** The character 兄 (xiōng, "brother") combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with 儿 (ér, "child") to depict an elder brother who gives orders. This conveys the traditional family role of the elder brother as a figure of authority, similar to other characters like 令 (lìng, "order") that emphasize the act of speaking or commanding.
- **examples:**
  - 我兄从(從)小向我传(傳)授智慧，使我终(終)生受益。
    - wǒ xiōng cóng xiǎo xiàng wǒ chuánshòu zhìhuì, shǐ wǒ zhōngshēng shòuyì.
    - My brother taught me wisdom from childhood, which has benefited me all my life.
  - 贤(賢)兄常助我困境。
    - xián xiōng cháng zhù wǒ kùn jìng.
    - My worthy brother often helps me overcome difficulties.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 兄](@media/glyph5144.png)
### 说(說) → 兌 → 兄 → 儿(兒)
- **traditional:** 兒
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** ér
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an infant with an imperfect cranium (fontanelle)
  - **interpretation:** The character 兒 (ér, "child") is a pictogram representing a child with a distinctive fontanelle, highlighting the child's young age and the characteristic soft spot on the head. This reflects the character's meaning as 'child.'
  - **simplification:** 儿 is a simplified and cursive form of 兒, representing a stylistic reduction of strokes while still retaining the essence of a child's figure.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小女孩喜欢(歡)唱歌。
    - Zhè gè xiǎo nǚhái xǐhuān chànggē.
    - This little girl likes to sing.
  - 他有一个(個)聪(聰)明的儿(兒)子。
    - Tā yǒu yī gè cōngmíng de érzi.
    - He has a smart son.
  - 每个(個)父母都希望自己的孩子健康快乐(樂)。
    - Měi gè fùmǔ dōu xīwàng zìjǐ de háizi jiànkāng kuàilè.
    - Every parent hopes their child is healthy and happy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 儿](@media/glyph513f.png)
### 说(說) → 兌 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)

## 穿
---
## to wear
### chuān
---
- **definition:** to wear
- **pinyin:** chuān
- **components:**
  - 穴
    - xué
    - cave
  - 牙
    - yá
    - tooth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 穴 (xué, "cave") + 牙 (yá, "tooth") =
    - something boring or piercing through a cave ->
    - to penetrate ->
    - to wear
  - **interpretation:** The character 穿(chuān, "to wear") combines a cave 穴 (xué, "cave") and a tooth 牙 (yá, "tooth"), suggesting the action of piercing or boring through a surface, akin to a tooth digging into material, leading to the concept of passing through or penetrating. This imagery extends to the act of wearing, penetrating clothing.
- **examples:**
  - 今天我穿了一件新衣服。
    - Jīntiān wǒ chuānle yī jiàn xīn yīfú.
    - Today, I wore a new piece of clothing.
  - 他每次上班都穿西装(裝)。
    - Tā měicì shàngbān dōu chuān xīzhuāng.
    - He wears a suit every time he goes to work.
  - 小孩子喜欢(歡)穿鲜(鮮)艳(豔)的颜(顏)色。
    - Xiǎo háizi xǐhuān chuān xiānyàn de yánsè.
    - Children like to wear bright colors.
### 穿 → 穴
- **definition:** cave
- **pinyin:** xué
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a cave or hole, resembling a small dwelling or opening
  - **interpretation:** The character 穴 (xué, "cave") visually represents a hole or cave with an open entry, suggesting a sheltered space similar to a primitive dwelling or burrow.
- **examples:**
  - 山里(裡)隐(隱)匿着(著)一个(個)深深的穴。
    - Shān lǐ yǐn nì zhe yí gè shēn shēn de xué.
    - A deep cave is hidden in the mountains.
  - 探险(險)家在悬(懸)崖下发(發)现(現)了一个(個)幽静(靜)的穴，据(據)说(說)里(裡)面住着(著)古老的精灵(靈)。
    - Tàn xiǎnjiā zài xuán yá xià fāxiàn le yí gè yōu jìng de xué, jù shuō lǐmiàn zhùzhe gǔlǎo de jīng líng.
    - The explorer discovered a quiet cave beneath the cliff, and it is said that ancient spirits dwell inside.
  - 河岸边(邊)的岩石上有一个(個)小穴。
    - Hé àn biān de yán shí shàng yǒu yí gè xiǎo xué.
    - There is a small cave on the rock by the riverbank.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 穴](@media/glyph7a74.png)
### 穿 → 牙
- **definition:** tooth
- **pinyin:** yá
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a pair of elephant tusks ->
    - used to indicate human molars
  - **interpretation:** The character 牙 (yá, 'tooth') originated as a pictogram representing elephant tusks, which resemble human molars in shape. This specific imagery was chosen to signify back teeth rather than incisors.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天刷牙。
    - Wǒ měitiān shuā yá.
    - I brush my teeth every day.
  - 医(醫)生检(檢)查牙齿(齒)，建议(議)定期看牙。
    - Yīshēng jiǎnchá yá chǐ, jiànyì dìngqī kàn yá.
    - The doctor examines the teeth and advises regular dental check-ups.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 牙](@media/glyph7259.png)

## 一样(樣)
---
## same
### yīyàng
---
- **traditional:** 一樣
- **definition:** same
- **pinyin:** yīyàng
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single
  - 样(樣)
    - yàng
    - appearance; kind
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 一 (yī, "one; single") + 样(樣) (yàng, "appearance; kind") =
    - having the same appearance or kind, thus 'same' or 'alike'.
  - **interpretation:** It makes sense to use 一 (yī, "one") to imply singularity or uniformity, combined with 样(樣) (yàng, "appearance") to denote having a unified appearance or type, thereby meaning 'same'.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)的衣服一样(樣)。
    - Wǒmen de yīfu yīyàng.
    - Our clothes are the same.
  - 这(這)件衬(襯)衫和那件衬(襯)衫一样(樣)。
    - Zhè jiàn chènshān hé nà jiàn chènshān yīyàng.
    - This shirt and that shirt are the same.
  - 我们(們)的观(觀)点(點)一样(樣)，追求的目标(標)相同。
    - Wǒmen de guāndiǎn yīyàng, zhuīqiú de mùbiāo xiāngtóng.
    - Our perspectives are the same, and the goals we pursue are identical.
### 一样(樣) → 一
- **definition:** one; single
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 一样(樣) → 样(樣)
- **traditional:** 樣
- **definition:** appearance; kind
- **pinyin:** yàng
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 羕
    - yàng
    - a place in ancient Shu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, 'wood') + phonetic 羕 (yàng) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 樣 (yàng, 'appearance; shape; manner') combines the semantic component 木 (mù, 'wood') to suggest a tangible or physical form, with the phonetic 羕 to provide the sound. The concept of 'appearance; shape; manner' relates to understanding form or style as if referring to forms made of or carved in wood.
  - **simplification:** 样(樣): 羊 (yáng, 'sheep') replaced 羕 (yàng) for a simpler phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 他的样(樣)子看起来(來)很疲惫(憊)。
    - Tā de yàngzi kàn qǐlái hěn pí bèi.
    - His appearance looks very tired.
  - 这(這)件衣服的款式和样(樣)式很流行。
    - Zhè jiàn yīfú de kuǎnshì hé yàngshì hěn liúxíng.
    - The style and appearance of this clothing are very popular.
  - 你应(應)该(該)学(學)学(學)他的工作样(樣)。
    - Nǐ yīnggāi xué xué tā de gōngzuò yàng.
    - You should learn his manner of working.
### 一样(樣) → 样(樣) → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 一样(樣) → 样(樣) → 羕
- **definition:** a place in ancient Shu
- **pinyin:** yàng
- **components:**
  - 羊
    - yáng
    - sheep
  - 永
    - yǒng
    - forever
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 羊 + semantic 永 ->
    - river
  - **interpretation:** The character 羕 (yàng, 'river') combines 羊 (yáng, 'sheep') as the phonetic component, which provides the sound, with 永 (yǒng, 'forever'), meaning 'perpetual' or 'endless', as the semantic component. The idea of a river is suggested through the continuous and flowing nature associated with 'forever'.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 羕](@media/glyph7f95.png)
### 一样(樣) → 样(樣) → 羕 → 羊
- **definition:** sheep
- **pinyin:** yáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a ram's head
  - **interpretation:** The character 羊(yáng, 'sheep') visually represents the head of a sheep or ram, capturing the animal's distinctive features. It serves as a straightforward pictogram, portraying one of the common animals in ancient agrarian societies.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)场(場)里(裡)有羊。
    - Nóngchǎng lǐ yǒu yáng.
    - There are sheep on the farm.
  - 春天来(來)了，羊群在草地上吃草。
    - Chūntiān lái le, yángqún zài cǎodì shàng chī cǎo.
    - In spring, the flock of sheep grazes on the meadow.
  - 那只(隻)羊看起来(來)很温(溫)顺(順)。
    - Nà zhī yáng kàn qǐlái hěn wēnshùn.
    - That sheep looks very gentle.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 羊](@media/glyph7f8a.png)
### 一样(樣) → 样(樣) → 羕 → 永
- **definition:** forever
- **pinyin:** yǒng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a long river with tributaries ->
    - original form of 泳 (yǒng, "swim")
  - **interpretation:** The character 永 depicts a long river, which visually represents its tributaries joining together. This imagery of an expansive and enduring water body conveys the sense of 'long-lasting' or 'perpetual' by suggesting continuity and flow. Additionally, the original association with water makes 永 also relate to 泳 (yǒng, "swim"), highlighting its aquatic connections.
- **examples:**
  - 友情是永恒(恆)的。
    - Yǒuqíng shì yǒnghéng de.
    - Friendship is eternal.
  - 她对(對)音乐(樂)的热(熱)爱(愛)永不会(會)改变(變)。
    - Tā duì yīnyuè de rè'ài yǒng bù huì gǎibiàn.
    - Her love for music will never change.
  - 他们(們)的故事将(將)在历(歷)史中永存。
    - Tāmen de gùshì jiāng zài lìshǐ zhōng yǒngcún.
    - Their story will endure in history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 永](@media/glyph6c38.png)

## 星期六
---
## Saturday
### xīngqīliù
---
- **definition:** Saturday
- **pinyin:** xīngqīliù
- **components:**
  - 星
    - xīng
    - star
  - 期
    - qī
    - period; time
  - 六
    - liù
    - six
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 星 (xīng, "star") + 期 (qī, "period; time") + 六 (liù, "six") combine to denote the sixth day of the week, Saturday. The naming convention for days of the week in Chinese is based on a numerical sequence starting from Sunday.
  - **interpretation:** 星期六(xīngqīliù, "Saturday") follows the sequential naming pattern used for days of the week in Chinese, with 六 (liù, "six") indicating it is the sixth day.
- **examples:**
  - 星期六，我不上班。
    - Xīngqīliù, wǒ bù shàngbān.
    - I don't work on Saturday.
  - 星期六，我和朋友一起去郊游(遊)。
    - Xīngqīliù, wǒ hé péngyǒu yīqǐ qù jiāoyóu.
    - On Saturday, I go for a picnic with my friends.
  - 星期六，我喜欢(歡)睡到自然醒。
    - Xīngqīliù, wǒ xǐhuān shuì dào zìrán xǐng.
    - On Saturday, I like to sleep in.
### 星期六 → 星
- **definition:** star
- **pinyin:** xīng
- **components:**
  - 晶
    - jīng
    - twinkling stars
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life; birth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 晶 (jīng, 'twinkling stars') + phonetic 生 (shēng) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted twinkling stars with 晶 (jīng, 'twinkling stars') indicating the twinkling or shining quality. The phonetic component 生 (shēng) was added to support the pronunciation but ultimately did not carry a separate semantic load. This compounded form solidified the modern representation of 'star'.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空中有许(許)多闪(閃)烁(爍)的星星。
    - Yèkōng zhōng yǒu xǔduō shǎnshuò de xīngxing.
    - There are many twinkling stars in the night sky.
  - 她的眼睛像星星一样(樣)明亮。
    - Tā de yǎnjing xiàng xīngxing yīyàng míngliàng.
    - Her eyes are as bright as stars.
  - 孩子们(們)在数(數)星星。
    - Háizimen zài shǔ xīngxing.
    - The children are counting stars.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 星](@media/glyph661f.png)
### 星期六 → 星 → 晶
- **definition:** twinkling stars
- **pinyin:** jīng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") x 3 =
    - multiple suns shining brightly ->
    - bright; sparkle; crystal
  - **interpretation:** The character 晶(jīng, "sparkle; crystal; bright") is formed by three 日 (rì, "sun") characters combined to visually represent multiple suns. This suggests an intense brilliance or sparkle, much like how multiple suns would create a radiant or crystal-like shine.
- **examples:**
  - 她的眼睛像晶石一样(樣)明亮。
    - Tā de yǎnjīng xiàng jīngshí yīyàng míngliàng.
    - Her eyes are as bright as crystals.
  - 窗户(戶)上结(結)了许(許)多冰晶。
    - Chuānghù shàng jié le xǔduō bīngjīng.
    - Many ice crystals have formed on the window.
  - 这(這)个(個)城市的夜景闪(閃)烁(爍)着(著)晶光。
    - Zhège chéngshì de yèjǐng shǎnshuò zhe jīngguāng.
    - The night view of the city sparkles brightly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 晶](@media/glyph6676.png)
### 星期六 → 星 → 晶 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 星期六 → 星 → 生
- **definition:** life; birth
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生命是一场(場)美丽(麗)的旅程。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他在战(戰)场(場)上奋(奮)力生存。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)的生鱼(魚)片非常新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

### 星期六 → 星 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)
### 星期六 → 期
- **definition:** period; time
- **pinyin:** qī
- **components:**
  - 其
    - qí
    - his
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 其 (qí) + semantic 月 (yuè, "moon") ->
    - changing moon marks passage of time ->
    - period of time
  - **interpretation:** The character 期(qī, "period") combines the phonetic 其 (qí, "his") with the semantic 月 (yuè, "moon") to signify the phases of the moon, which naturally represent cycles and periods of time. The moon's regular changes provide a clear, cyclical marker of time's passage.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)项(項)目需要完成的时(時)间(間)是三个(個)月。
    - Zhège xiàngmù xūyào wánchéng de shíjiān shì sān gè yuè.
    - The period required to complete this project is three months.
  - 在考试(試)期间(間)，请(請)保持安静(靜)。
    - Zài kǎoshì qījiān, qǐng bǎochí ānjìng.
    - During the exam period, please remain quiet.
  - 我们(們)在下一个(個)阶(階)段继(繼)续(續)努力。
    - Wǒmen zài xià yī gè jiēduàn jìxù nǔlì.
    - We will continue to work hard in the next phase.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 期](@media/glyph671f.png)
### 星期六 → 期 → 其
- **definition:** his
- **pinyin:** qí
- **components:**
  - 丌
    - qí
    - stand
  - 箕
    - jī
    - basket
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 𠀠 (basket) ->
    - 𠔝 with added 丌 (stand, phonetic) ->
    - borrowed as pronoun
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a basket (𠀠), which later included a stand (丌) beneath it to stabilize the image on bronze inscriptions, forming 𠔝. This combination was later borrowed for its sound to represent the pronoun 'his, her, its', and the basket meaning was reassigned to 箕 (jī, 'basket').
- **examples:**
  - 他把其思绪(緒)整理了一遍。
    - Tā bǎ qí sīxù zhěnglǐ le yī biàn.
    - He organized his thoughts once.
  - 其琴声(聲)如水般柔软(軟)。
    - Qí qín shēng rú shuǐ bān róuruǎn.
    - His playing is as soft as water.
  - 其计(計)划(劃)得到了同事们(們)的支持。
    - Qí jìhuà dédào le tóngshìmen de zhīchí.
    - His plan received the support of his colleagues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 其](@media/glyph5176.png)
### 星期六 → 期 → 其 → 丌
- **definition:** stand
- **pinyin:** qí
- **components:**
  - 其
    - qí
    - his
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a support or stand for a basket ->
    - later representation of a table
  - **interpretation:** The character 丌 (jī, "table") originally represents a stand or support and was used as a component under 其 (qí, "his") to depict a basket on a stand. This association serves as its link to the meaning of 'table', conceptualizing a flat-topped support structure. This character was an ancient form of 其 and primarily served as a physical depiction of a supporting stand.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 丌](@media/glyph4e0c.png)
### 星期六 → 期 → 其 → 箕
- **definition:** basket
- **pinyin:** jī
- **components:**
  - 竹
    - zhú
    - bamboo
  - 其
    - qí
    - his
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 竹 (zhú, "bamboo") + phonetic 其 (qí, "his") ->
    - basket made of bamboo
  - **interpretation:** The character 箕(jī, "basket") combines 竹 (zhú, "bamboo") as the semantic component, indicating that the item is made of bamboo, with 其 (qí, "his") serving as the phonetic component to provide the sound. Originally, 其 (qí, "his") depicted a basket or container shape, and accordingly, 箕 specializes in the meaning related to a bamboo basket.
- **examples:**
  - 他用箕收集落下的叶(葉)子。
    - Tā yòng jī shōují luòxià de yèzi.
    - He uses a basket to collect fallen leaves.
  - 箕的大小非常适(適)合装(裝)米。
    - Jī de dàxiǎo fēicháng shìhé zhuāng mǐ.
    - The size of the basket is perfect for holding rice.
  - 那个(個)老人总(總)在集市上卖(賣)他编(編)的箕。
    - Nàge lǎorén zǒng zài jíshì shàng mài tā biān de jī.
    - That old man always sells the baskets he weaves at the market.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 箕](@media/glyph7b95.png)
### 星期六 → 期 → 其 → 箕 → 竹
- **definition:** bamboo
- **pinyin:** zhú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts bamboo stalks with leaves
  - **interpretation:** The character 竹 (zhú, "bamboo") visually represents two stalks of bamboo with leaves at the top, illustrating the appearance of bamboo plants traditionally found in nature.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)根竹坚(堅)韧(韌)且美丽(麗)。
    - Zhè gēn zhú jiān rèn qiě měi lì.
    - This bamboo is strong and beautiful.
  - 竹子在风(風)中摇(搖)曳，发(發)出沙沙的声(聲)音。
    - Zhúzi zài fēng zhōng yáo yè, fā chū shā shā de shēng yīn.
    - The bamboo sways in the wind, making a rustling sound.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 竹](@media/glyph7af9.png)
### 星期六 → 期 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 星期六 → 六
- **definition:** six
- **pinyin:** liù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Ancient counting symbol ->
    - character for 'six'
  - **interpretation:** 六 (liù, 'six') is a pictogram that may originally have depicted a shed, but was primarily used as an ancient counting symbol. The form resembles primitive tally markings used for numerical purposes.
- **examples:**
  - 我有六个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu liù gè píngguǒ.
    - I have six apples.
  - 这(這)个(個)盒子可以放六瓶水。
    - Zhè gè hézi kěyǐ fàng liù píng shuǐ.
    - This box can hold six bottles of water.
  - 六只(隻)猫(貓)在花园(園)里(裡)玩耍。
    - Liù zhī māo zài huāyuán lǐ wánshuǎ.
    - Six cats are playing in the garden.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 六](@media/glyph516d.png)

## 星期六

## Saturday

## 多
---
## many
### duō
---
- **definition:** many
- **pinyin:** duō
- **components:**
  - 肉
    - ròu
    - meat
  - 夕
    - xī
    - evening
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 肉 (ròu, 'meat') corrupted to 夕 (xī) ->
    - duplicated 夕 =
    - many
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted two pieces of meat 肉 (ròu, 'meat'), suggesting abundance or 'many'. Over time, 肉 was corrupted to 夕 (xī), and the character became a duplication of 夕, signifying multiplicity or 'many'. This aligns with other duplicative characters like 林 (lín, 'forest').
- **examples:**
  - 书(書)架上有很多书(書)。
    - Shūjià shàng yǒu hěn duō shū.
    - There are many books on the shelf.
  - 他工作得比我多。
    - Tā gōngzuò de bǐ wǒ duō.
    - He works more than I do.
  - 多喝水有益健康。
    - Duō hē shuǐ yǒuyì jiànkāng.
    - Drinking more water is beneficial to health.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 多](@media/glyph591a.png)
### 多 → 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of flesh or meat with stripes representing texture.
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉(ròu, "flesh") depicts a piece of meat, meant to evoke the concept of flesh through its visual resemblance to a striped or sectioned piece of meat.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃肉。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like eating meat.
  - 这(這)块(塊)肉很鲜(鮮)美，营(營)养(養)丰(豐)富。
    - Zhè kuài ròu hěn xiānměi, yíngyǎng fēngfù.
    - This piece of meat is very fresh and delicious, and it is nutritious.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 肉](@media/glyph8089.png)
### 多 → 夕
- **definition:** evening
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a moon crescent
  - **interpretation:** The character 夕 (xī, 'evening') is a pictogram that represents a crescent moon, capturing the image of the moon in the evening sky. The comparison to 月 (yuè, 'moon') underscores its depiction of the moon phase commonly associated with evening.
- **examples:**
  - 夕阳(陽)西下。
    - xī yáng xīxià.
    - The setting sun descends.
  - 夕阳(陽)西下，晚风(風)徐徐。
    - xī yáng xīxià, wǎn fēng xúxú.
    - The sun sets as the gentle evening breeze blows.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夕](@media/glyph5915.png)
### 多 → 夕 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)

## 少
---
## few
### shǎo
---
- **definition:** few
- **pinyin:** shǎo
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts four dots, perhaps three grains of sand ->
    - indicates "a few, a little" ->
    - phonetically borrowed from 小 (xiǎo, "small")
  - **interpretation:** The character 少 (shǎo, "few") originally depicted four dots, possibly representing grains of sand, conveying the impression of a small quantity. It was phonetically borrowed from 小 (xiǎo, "small"), which uses three dots to signify smallness, reinforcing the sense of 'few' through the idea of minimal amounts.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)有很少的字。
    - Zhè běn shū yǒu hěn shǎo de zì.
    - This book has very few words.
  - 来(來)参(參)加演出的人很少。
    - Lái cānjiā yǎnchū de rén hěn shǎo.
    - Few people came to attend the performance.
  - 这(這)个(個)季节(節)雨水很少。
    - Zhège jìjié yǔshuǐ hěn shǎo.
    - There is very little rain this season.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 少](@media/glyph5c11.png)
### 少 → 小
- **definition:** small
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小猫(貓)很可爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座小桥(橋)横(橫)跨河流，连(連)接两(兩)岸。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我一小杯水。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 小](@media/glyph5c0f.png)

## 少
### shǎo
---
## few
%%%
## 多少
---
## how many
### duōshao
---
- **definition:** how many
- **pinyin:** duōshao
- **components:**
  - 多
    - duō
    - many; much
  - 少
    - shǎo
    - few; little
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 多 (duō, "many") refers to a large quantity, while 少 (shǎo, "few") refers to a small quantity or lack. Together, 多少 (duōshao, "how many") asks about the number of items, functioning as an interrogative phrase inquiring about quantity.
  - **interpretation:** The character 多 (duō, "many") suggests an abundance or a large number, while 少 (shǎo, "few") signifies a small number or scarcity. Combining these contrasting notions forms a question about numerical quantity, 'how many,' blending the concepts of more and less.
- **examples:**
  - 你想买(買)多少苹(蘋)果？
    - Nǐ xiǎng mǎi duōshao píngguǒ?
    - How many apples do you want to buy?
  - 这(這)里(裡)有多少人？
    - Zhèlǐ yǒu duōshao rén?
    - How many people are here?
  - 你们(們)学(學)校有多少老师(師)？
    - Nǐmen xuéxiào yǒu duōshao lǎoshī?
    - How many teachers are at your school?

    - many

    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.

  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 多少 → 少
- **definition:** few; little
- **pinyin:** shǎo
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts four dots, perhaps three grains of sand ->
    - indicates "a few, a little" ->
    - phonetically borrowed from 小 (xiǎo, "small")
  - **interpretation:** The character 少 (shǎo, "few") originally depicted four dots, possibly representing grains of sand, conveying the impression of a small quantity. It was phonetically borrowed from 小 (xiǎo, "small"), which uses three dots to signify smallness, reinforcing the sense of 'few' through the idea of minimal amounts.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)有很少的字。
    - Zhè běn shū yǒu hěn shǎo de zì.
    - This book has very few words.
  - 来(來)参(參)加演出的人很少。
    - Lái cānjiā yǎnchū de rén hěn shǎo.
    - Few people came to attend the performance.
  - 这(這)个(個)季节(節)雨水很少。
    - Zhège jìjié yǔshuǐ hěn shǎo.
    - There is very little rain this season.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 少](@media/glyph5c11.png)
### 多少 → 少 → 小
- **definition:** small
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小猫(貓)很可爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座小桥(橋)横(橫)跨河流，连(連)接两(兩)岸。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我一小杯水。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.

## 汉(漢)堡
---
## hamburger
### hànbǎo
---
- **traditional:** 漢堡
- **definition:** hamburger
- **pinyin:** hànbǎo
- **components:**
  - 汉(漢)
    - hàn
    - Han
  - 堡
    - bǎo
    - fort; castle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 漢 (hàn, "Han"); 堡 (bǎo, "fort; castle")
  - **interpretation:** 漢 (hàn, "Han") often represents the ethnic group or language but here is used phonetically. 堡 (bǎo, "fort; castle") is a phonetic component capturing the pronunciation of the word. When combined, 漢堡 (hànbǎo, "hamburger") represents the borrowed term for 'hamburger', utilizing both characters for their phonetic similarity to the English term rather than semantic meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 我今天中午吃了一个(個)汉(漢)堡。
    - Wǒ jīntiān zhōngwǔ chīle yī gè hànbǎo.
    - I had a hamburger for lunch today.
  - 这(這)家店的汉(漢)堡非常美味。
    - Zhè jiā diàn de hànbǎo fēicháng měiwèi.
    - The hamburgers at this place are very delicious.
  - 小明买(買)了两(兩)个(個)汉(漢)堡，还(還)买(買)了一瓶可乐(樂)。
    - Xiǎo Míng mǎile liǎng gè hànbǎo, hái mǎile yī píng kělè.
    - Xiao Ming bought two hamburgers and also bought a bottle of cola.
### 汉(漢)堡 → 汉(漢)
- **traditional:** 漢
- **definition:** Han
- **pinyin:** hàn
- **components:**
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 又
    - yòu
    - again
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 水 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic component 暵 or 熯 ->
    - refers to river in China 漢江/漢水 ->
    - simplified by removing components to form 又 (yòu, "again")
  - **interpretation:** The character 漢 initially depicts the Han River with water radical 水 (shuǐ, "water") and a phonetic element. Its simplification to 汉 involved reducing complexity by retaining the 又 (yòu, "again") shape, reflecting modern streamlining efforts.
  - **simplification:** 汉(漢) was simplified by eliminating components, retaining the shape 又 (yòu, "again"), a common simplification strategy to reduce strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他是汉(漢)人。
    - Tā shì hànrén.
    - He is Han Chinese.
  - 汉(漢)语(語)很美。
    - Hànyǔ hěn měi.
    - The Chinese language is beautiful.
  - 他学(學)习(習)汉(漢)字，了解汉(漢)文化。
    - Tā xuéxí hànzì, liǎojiě hàn wénhuà.
    - He studies Chinese characters and learns about Chinese culture.
### 汉(漢)堡 → 汉(漢) → 水
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水是一种(種)生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì yī zhǒng shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 夏天很热(熱)，喝水能解暑。
    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿岸绿(綠)树(樹)成荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.
    - The river flows babbling, and green trees along the bank provide shade.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 水](@media/glyph6c34.png)
### 汉(漢)堡 → 汉(漢) → 又
- **definition:** again
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 汉(漢)堡 → 堡
- **definition:** fort; castle
- **pinyin:** bǎo
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 保
    - bǎo
    - protect; safeguard
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "earth") + phonetic 保 (bǎo) ->
    - fort; castle
  - **interpretation:** 堡(bǎo) uses 土 (tǔ, "earth") to emphasize its connection to earthworks or constructions made of earth, such as a fort or castle. 保 (bǎo) provides the pronunciation. The character thus evokes the idea of a fortified structure built upon or within the earth.
- **examples:**
  - 那座城堡非常壮(壯)观(觀)。
    - Nà zuò chéngbǎo fēicháng zhuàngguān.
    - That castle is very magnificent.
  - 我们(們)在山顶(頂)建了一个(個)堡垒(壘)。
    - Wǒmen zài shāndǐng jiàn le yī gè bǎolěi.
    - We built a fort on the mountaintop.
  - 堡上的旗帜(幟)随(隨)风(風)飘(飄)扬(揚)。
    - Bǎo shàng de qízhì suí fēng piāoyáng.
    - The flag on the fort is waving in the wind.
### 汉(漢)堡 → 堡 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.

### 汉(漢)堡 → 堡 → 保
- **definition:** protect; safeguard
- **pinyin:** bǎo
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
  - 爪
    - zhuǎ
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 子 (zǐ, "child") ->
    - person carrying a child ->
    - to carry (a child) ->
    - 爪 (zhuǎ, "hand") added to emphasize carrying ->
    - simplified to enhance meaning ->
    - current form with two strokes for hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 保 (bǎo, "protect") originates from the image of a person carrying a child, representing protection and caregiving. The addition of 爪 (zhuǎ, "hand") in early forms highlights the act of carrying with hands, reinforcing the protective role of the person. The modern form retains the strokes that symbolize hands, maintaining the theme of protection through physical support and care, which follows from the basic image of human protection of offspring.
  - **simplification:** 徤 replaced with a simpler form for ease of writing without changing pronunciation or meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 警察负(負)责(責)保护(護)市民的安全。
    - Jǐngchá fùzé bǎohù shìmín de ānquán.
    - The police are responsible for protecting the safety of the citizens.
  - 请(請)保管好你的贵(貴)重物品。
    - Qǐng bǎoguǎn hǎo nǐ de guìzhòng wùpǐn.
    - Please keep your valuable items safe.
  - 我们(們)要保证(證)食物的质(質)量。
    - Wǒmen yào bǎozhèng shíwù de zhìliàng.
    - We need to ensure the quality of the food.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 保](@media/glyph4fdd.png)

## 店
---
## shop
### diàn
---
- **definition:** shop
- **pinyin:** diàn
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - house built to depend on a cliff
  - 占
    - zhān
    - divine; observe
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 ("house built to depend on a cliff") + phonetic 占 ->
    - shop
  - **interpretation:** The character 店 (diàn, "shop") combines the semantic element 广, representing a building or structure, with the phonetic element 占, providing the sound. The idea is of a structure where goods are stationed, forming a place to sell or trade items, hence a 'shop'.
- **examples:**
  - 我在书(書)店买(買)了一本书(書)。
    - Wǒ zài shūdiàn mǎi le yī běn shū.
    - I bought a book at the bookstore.
  - 这(這)个(個)小村庄(莊)只有一家小杂(雜)货(貨)店。
    - Zhège xiǎo cūnzhuāng zhǐ yǒu yī jiā xiǎo záhuòdiàn.
    - This small village has only one small grocery shop.
  - 每当(當)我路过(過)那家甜品店，我都会(會)停下来(來)买(買)些东(東)西。
    - Měidāng wǒ lùguò nà jiā tiánpǐndiàn, wǒ dūhuì tíng xiàlái mǎi xiē dōngxi.
    - Whenever I pass by that dessert shop, I always stop to buy something.
### 店 → 廣
- **definition:** house built to depend on a cliff
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by retaining the roof radical but removing 黃, simplifying the structure considerably.
- **examples:**
  - 我们正在寻找一个可以提供广(廣)的地方。
    - Wǒmen zhèngzài xúnzhǎo yī gè kěyǐ tígōng guǎng de dìfāng.
    - We are looking for a place that can provide shelter.
  - 那里的广(廣)设施非常完善，适合长时间停留。
    - Nàlǐ de guǎng shèshī fēicháng wánshàn, shìhé cháng shíjiān tíngliú.
    - The shelter facilities there are very complete, suitable for long stays.
  - 如果有恶劣天气，我们需要一个广(廣)来保护自己。
    - Rúguǒ yǒu èliè tiānqì, wǒmen xūyào yī gè guǎng lái bǎohù zìjǐ.
    - If there is bad weather, we need a shelter to protect ourselves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廣](@media/glyph5ee3.png)
### 店 → 廣 → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** roof; shelter
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广(廣) (guǎng, "broad") + phonetic 黃 (huáng, "yellow") ->
    - broad
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, "broad") combines the semantic element 广(廣), depicting a broad area or structure, with the phonetic element 黃 (huáng), which lends its sound. This combination signifies the idea of something wide or expansive.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by removing the 黃 (huáng, "yellow") phonetic component, leaving only the semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)河非常广(廣)阔(闊)。
    - Zhè tiáo hé fēicháng guǎngkuò.
    - This river is very broad.
  - 他的知识(識)面很广(廣)，总(總)是能解决(決)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā de zhīshì miàn hěn guǎng, zǒng shì néng jiějué wèntí.
    - His knowledge is broad, and he is always able to solve problems.
  - 在学(學)校里(裡)，他参(參)加了许(許)多广(廣)泛的活动(動)。
    - Zài xuéxiào lǐ, tā cānjiāle xǔduō guǎngfàn de huódòng.
    - At school, he participated in many broad activities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 广](@media/glyph5e7f.png)
### 店 → 廣 → 广(廣) → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵花是黄(黃)色的。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋天来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成金黄(黃)色。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.
  - 他穿了一件黄(黃)色的外套。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黃](@media/glyph9ec3.png)
### 店 → 占
- **definition:** divine; observe
- **pinyin:** zhān
- **components:**
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divination
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 卜 (bǔ, "divination") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - speaking about divination ->
    - divination
  - **interpretation:** The character 占 (zhān, "divination") represents the act of divination, combining the symbol for divination itself with the mouth, which may imply speaking or chanting during the divinatory practice.
- **examples:**
  - 古人借占，测(測)定吉凶。
    - Gǔ rén jiè zhān, cè dìng jí xiōng.
    - Ancient people used divination to determine auspiciousness and inauspiciousness.
  - 他占了一卦。
    - Tā zhānle yī guà.
    - He performed a divination.
  - 他运(運)用占，预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Tā yùnyòng zhān, yùcè wèilái.
    - He relied on divination to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 占](@media/glyph5360.png)
### 店 → 占 → 卜
- **definition:** divination
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)
### 店 → 占 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)

## 得
