### 过(過) → 咼 → 冎
- **definition:** a type of ancient vessel
- **pinyin:** guā
- **components:**
  - 骨
    - gǔ
    - bone
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts bones ->
    - original form of 骨 (gǔ, "bone")
  - **interpretation:** The character 冎 is a pictogram representing bones and serves as the original form of 骨 (gǔ, "bone"). Its depiction captures the outline of bones, highlighting its usage in ancient scripts. It also appears in other characters as a component, maintaining its essence related to structure and form.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)汉(漢)字由偏旁和冎构(構)成，其中冎提供了语(語)音线(線)索。
    - Zhège hànzì yóu piānpáng hé guǒ gòuchéng, qízhōng guǒ tígōng le yǔyīn xiànsuǒ.
    - This character is composed of radicals and guǒ, wherein guǒ provides a phonetic clue.
  - 在古代造字过(過)程中，冎常作为(為)声(聲)旁使用。
    - Zài gǔdài zàozì guòchéng zhōng, guǒ cháng zuòwéi shēngpáng shǐyòng.
    - In the process of character creation in ancient times, guǒ was often used as a phonetic component.
  - 冎是一种(種)发(發)音提示符。
    - Guǒ shì yī zhǒng fāyīn tíshì fú.
    - Guǒ is a phonetic indicator.
- **historical forms:**

## 学(學)校
---
## school
### xuéxiào
---
- **traditional:** 學校
- **definition:** school
- **pinyin:** xuéxiào
- **components:**
  - 学(學)
    - xué
    - to learn; to study
  - 校
    - xiào
    - school; comparison; military field officer
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 學 (xué, "to learn") + 校 (xiào, "school") =
    - place of learning ->
    - school
  - **interpretation:** 學 (xué, "to learn") depicts a child under a roof, symbolizing receiving knowledge or education. 校 (xiào, "school") originally referred to a place of examination or comparison, where standards are upheld. Together, they create the concept of a structured environment or institution dedicated to learning and education.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)每天早上八点(點)去学(學)校。
    - Wǒmen měitiān zǎoshang bā diǎn qù xuéxiào.
    - We go to school at eight every morning.
  - 学(學)校的图(圖)书(書)馆(館)很大。
    - Xuéxiào de túshūguǎn hěn dà.
    - The school's library is very big.
  - 放学(學)后(後)，我通常和朋友打篮(籃)球。
    - Fàngxué hòu, wǒ tōngcháng hé péngyǒu dǎ lánqiú.
    - After school, I usually play basketball with friends.
### 学(學)校 → 学(學)
- **traditional:** 學
- **definition:** to learn; to study
- **pinyin:** xué
- **components:**
  - 爻
    - yáo
    - double cross
  - 六
    - liù
    - six
  - 𦥑
    - kuk
    - hands around
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 爻 + phonetic 六 ->
    - 𦥑 added ->
    - semantic 子 added ->
    - simplified 六 ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** The character 學 (xué, "study") originally combined two phonetic components, 爻 (yáo, "double cross") and 六 (liù, "six"), to represent its sound. Over time, the character evolved with the addition of 𦥑 (components positioned like hands around 爻) and the semantic 子 (zǐ, "child") to specify a child learning or studying, under a cover (冖). In its modern form, 六 is simplified to resemble 冖, which visually merges with the hands around 爻, reflecting the learning process enclosed as children gather to study.
  - **simplification:** "学" is the simplified form of "學." The transformation occurred by merging the visual elements into a compact form, where 冖 serves as a common phonetic and visual element, while the complex structure of 學 was streamlined.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天都努力学(學)习(習)。
    - Tā měitiān dōu nǔlì xuéxí.
    - He studies diligently every day.
  - 我在北京大学(學)学(學)习(習)中文。
    - Wǒ zài Běijīng Dàxué xuéxí zhōngwén.
    - I am studying Chinese at Peking University.
  - 这(這)个(個)学(學)校有很多优(優)秀的老师(師)。
    - Zhège xuéxiào yǒu hěnduō yōuxiù de lǎoshī.
    - This school has many excellent teachers.
### 学(學)校 → 学(學) → 爻
- **definition:** double cross
- **pinyin:** yáo
- **components:**
  - 乂
    - yì
    - to govern
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 乂 (yì, "to govern") + 乂 =
    - two stacked 'X' marks representing divination lines
  - **interpretation:** The character 爻(yáo, "divination lines") depicts two crossing lines, resembling 'X' marks, symbolizing the divination lines used in traditional methods. These marks can be interpreted as representing either pairs of yarrow stalks used for divination or bamboo slips used for calculations. Though it might visually resemble 交 (jiāo, "cross") or 駁 (bó, "contradict"), its primary function is depicting the meaningful crossing patterns in divination.
- **examples:**
  - 易经(經)卜卦时(時)，观(觀)察爻的变(變)化。
    - Yì jīng bǔ guà shí, guānchá yáo de biànhuà.
    - When consulting the I Ching, one observes the changes of the divination lines.
  - 卦中的每一个(個)爻都蕴(蘊)含宇宙奥(奧)秘。
    - Guà zhōng de měi yīgè yáo dōu yùnhán yǔzhòu àomì.
    - Every divination line in the hexagram contains the mysteries of the universe.
  - 大师(師)解读(讀)时(時)，详(詳)细(細)说(說)明爻的象征(徵)意义(義)。
    - Dàshī jiědú shí, xiángxì shuōmíng yáo de xiàngzhēng yìyì.
    - When the master interprets, he elaborates on the symbolic meaning of the divination lines.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爻](@media/glyph723b.png)
### 学(學)校 → 学(學) → 爻 → 乂
- **definition:** to govern
- **pinyin:** yì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool (similar to a sickle or a pair of scissors) for mowing or weeding ->
    - used for governing ->
    - final form 乂
  - **interpretation:** The character 乂 originally depicted a tool used for cutting, and by extension, it was associated with governing due to the notion of cutting or managing weeds as a metaphor for ruling effectively. This sense of order is crucial in governance.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)些年，他致力于(於)地方的治理。
    - Zhèxiē nián, tā zhìlì yú dìfāng de zhìlǐ.
    - Over the years, he has dedicated himself to local governance.
  - 为(為)民者，先自齐(齊)以治家。
    - Wèi mín zhě, xiān zì qí yǐ zhì jiā.
    - Those who govern for the people, first manage their own households.
  - 长(長)者都希望后(後)代能好好治理天下。
    - Zhǎng zhě dōu xīwàng hòudài néng hǎohǎo zhìlǐ tiānxià.
    - The elders hope that future generations can govern the world well.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 乂](@media/glyph4e42.png)
### 学(學)校 → 学(學) → 六
- **definition:** six
- **pinyin:** liù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Ancient counting symbol ->
    - character for 'six'
  - **interpretation:** 六 (liù, 'six') is a pictogram that may originally have depicted a shed, but was primarily used as an ancient counting symbol. The form resembles primitive tally markings used for numerical purposes.
- **examples:**
  - 我有六个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu liù gè píngguǒ.
    - I have six apples.
  - 这(這)个(個)盒子可以放六瓶水。
    - Zhè gè hézi kěyǐ fàng liù píng shuǐ.
    - This box can hold six bottles of water.
  - 六只(隻)猫(貓)在花园(園)里(裡)玩耍。
    - Liù zhī māo zài huāyuán lǐ wánshuǎ.
    - Six cats are playing in the garden.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 六](@media/glyph516d.png)
### 学(學)校 → 学(學) → 𦥑
- **definition:** hands around
- **pinyin:** kuk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a pair of hands
  - **interpretation:** The character 𦥑 (kù, "hands") directly represents the image of two hands, embodying the concept through visual depiction. It is a straightforward pictogram, intended to convey the physical form and function of hands.
### 学(學)校 → 学(學) → 子
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.
- **historical forms:**

### 学(學)校 → 校
- **definition:** school; comparison; military field officer
- **pinyin:** xiào
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 交
    - xiāo
    - to mix
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, 'tree') providing the semantic element of a place or structure + 交 (xiāo, 'to mix') as the phonetic component ->
    - signifies a place where teachings mix, originally for schooling or correction
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 木 (mù, 'tree'), representing buildings or institutions made of wood, and 交 (xiāo, 'to mix'), signifying the mixing or interaction of knowledge, reflecting a place of education or correction like a school.
- **examples:**
  - 他早上到校，参(參)加考试(試)。
    - Tā zǎoshang dào xiào, cānjiā kǎoshì.
    - He goes to school in the morning, and takes an exam.
  - 他认(認)真校对(對)，确(確)保答案正确(確)。
    - Tā rènzhēn xiàoduì, quèbǎo dá'àn zhèngquè.
    - He carefully proofs his work, ensuring the answers are correct.
  - 她在校期间(間)，结(結)识(識)了许(許)多好友。
    - Tā zài xiào qíjiān, jiéshí le xǔduō hǎoyǒu.
    - During her time at school, she made many friends.
- **historical forms:**

### 学(學)校 → 校 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.

### 学(學)校 → 校 → 交
- **definition:** to mix
- **pinyin:** xiāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human with crossed legs ->
    - today's form shows upper part similar to 立 (lì, 'stand')
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a human figure with crossed legs, visually suggesting the notion of crossing or mixing, as legs are intertwined. This cross-legged posture naturally extended to meanings associated with mixing or crossing paths.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)必须(須)把材料交在一起。
    - Wǒmen bìxū bǎ cáiliào xiāo zài yīqǐ.

    - Zài pēngrèn kè shàng, lǎoshī jiāo wǒmen rúhé xiāo bùtóng de pèiliào.
    - In the cooking class, the teacher taught us how to mix different ingredients.
  - 把这(這)两(兩)种(種)颜(顏)料交在一起，可以得到一种(種)新的颜(顏)色。
    - Bǎ zhè liǎng zhǒng yánliào xiāo zài yīqǐ, kěyǐ dédào yī zhǒng xīn de yánsè.
    - By mixing these two paints together, you can get a new color.

## 员(員)工
---
## employee
### yuángōng
---
- **traditional:** 員工
- **definition:** employee
- **pinyin:** yuángōng
- **components:**
  - 员(員)
    - yuán
    - person
  - 工
    - gōng
    - work; worker; craft
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 员(員) (yuán, "person") + 工 (gōng, "work") =
    - person who works ->
    - employee
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 员(員) (yuán, "person") and 工 (gōng, "work") logically denotes an "employee," someone who is employed to perform work. The term succinctly captures the role of an individual in a workplace setting.
- **examples:**
  - 我是公司的员(員)工。
    - Wǒ shì gōngsī de yuángōng.
    - I’m an employee of the company.
  - 这(這)个(個)公司有很多员(員)工。
    - Zhège gōngsī yǒu hěn duō yuángōng.
    - The company has many employees.
### 员(員)工 → 员(員)
- **traditional:** 員
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** yuán
- **components:**
  - 鼎
    - dǐng
    - ding
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 〇 representing top edge of 鼎 (dǐng, "ding") ->
    - roundness ->
    - member
  - **interpretation:** 〇 indicates the top edge of a 鼎 (dǐng, "ding") representing roundness, which metaphorically connects to the idea of a group of members forming a unified whole.
  - **simplification:** 員: 貝 (bèi, "cowry") was simplified to 贝(貝) in the character 員 to form the simplified character 员, which visually reduces the strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一名团(團)队(隊)成员(員)。
    - Tā shì yī míng tuánduì chéngyuán.
    - He is a member of the team.
  - 公司需要招募新员(員)工。
    - Gōngsī xūyào zhāomù xīn yuángōng.
    - The company needs to recruit new members of staff.
  - 俱乐(樂)部的所有成员(員)都喜欢(歡)运(運)动(動)。
    - Jùlèbù de suǒyǒu chéngyuán dōu xǐhuān yùndòng.
    - All the members of the club like sports.
### 员(員)工 → 员(員) → 鼎
- **definition:** ding
- **pinyin:** dǐng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a three-legged bronze vessel ->
    - later used for divination
  - **interpretation:** The character 鼎(dǐng, 'tripod') is a pictogram that depicts a tripod vessel with three legs, symbolizing its use in cooking and ritual sacrifices. Over time, it was also borrowed phonetically to represent the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 商朝的青铜(銅)鼎象征(徵)着(著)权(權)力。
    - Shāng cháo de qīngtóng dǐng xiàngzhēng zhe quánlì.
    - The bronze tripod from the Shang Dynasty symbolizes power.
  - 在古代，鼎是用来(來)烹饪(飪)食物的器具。
    - Zài gǔdài, dǐng shì yòng lái pēngrèn shíwù de qìjù.
    - In ancient times, the tripod was a utensil used for cooking food.
  - 这(這)个(個)博物馆(館)里(裏)展示了一尊精美的铜(銅)鼎。
    - Zhège bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnshì le yī zūn jīngměi de tóngdǐng.
    - This museum exhibits an exquisite bronze tripod.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 鼎](@media/glyph9f0e.png)
### 员(員)工 → 工
- **definition:** work; worker; craft
- **pinyin:** gōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bladed tool to plow the ground and to mark a border, or a carpenter's square
  - **interpretation:** 工 (gōng, "work") represents either a tool used in agriculture for marking or a carpenter's square, reflecting its connection to traditional manual labor and craftsmanship.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天下午去做工。
    - Tā měitiān xiàwǔ qù zuò gōng.
    - He goes to work every afternoon.
  - 工厂(廠)里(裡)的机(機)器不停地运(運)转(轉)。
    - Gōng chǎng lǐ de jīqì bù tíng de yùnzhuǎn.
    - The machines in the factory run nonstop.
  - 这(這)位工人技艺(藝)精湛。
    - Zhè wèi gōngrén jìyì jīngzhàn.
    - This worker is highly skilled.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 工](@media/glyph5de5.png)

## 服务(務)员(員)
---
## waiter/waitress
### fúwùyuán
---
- **traditional:** 服務員
- **definition:** waiter/waitress
- **pinyin:** fúwùyuán
- **components:**
  - 服
    - fú
    - serve; clothes; obey
  - 務
    - wù
    - duties; affairs; business
  - 員
    - yuán
    - member; person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 服 (fú, "serve") + 務 (wù, "duties; affairs") + 員 (yuán, "member; person") =
    - a person (員) who serves (服) duties (務) ->
    - waiter/waitress
  - **interpretation:** 服 (fú, "serve") implies attending to others' needs. 務 (wù, "duties; affairs") emphasizes the responsibilities or tasks involved. 員 (yuán, "member; person") specifies someone engaged in a particular role or job. Together, 服務員 (fúwùyuán) represents a person tasked with serving others by performing specific duties, hence a waiter or waitress, focusing on the service aspect in hospitality.
- **examples:**
  - 服务(務)员(員)正在为(為)我们(們)上菜。
    - Fúwùyuán zhèngzài wèi wǒmen shàng cài.
    - The waiter is serving us dishes.
  - 我叫服务(務)员(員)过(過)来(來)，然后(後)点(點)了饮(飲)料。
    - Wǒ jiào fúwùyuán guòlái, ránhòu diǎnle yǐnliào.
    - I called the waiter over and then ordered drinks.
  - 服务(務)员(員)给(給)了我们(們)很好的建议(議)。
    - Fúwùyuán gěile wǒmen hěn hǎo de jiànyì.
    - The waiter gave us great advice.
### 服务(務)员(員) → 服
- **definition:** serve; clothes; obey
- **pinyin:** fú
- **components:**
  - 凡
    - fán
    - tray
  - 𠬝
    - [not standardized]
    - to subdue
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 凡 ('tray') + phonetic 𠬝 ('to subdue') ->
    - to serve; 凡 corrupted to 月
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a tray, 凡 (fán, 'tray'), as a symbol for offering or serving, combined with 𠬝 (a pictogram for 'to subdue') to convey the act of serving or obeying. Over time, the component 凡 (fán) became corrupted into a form resembling 月 (yuè, 'moon'), which is retained in the final character. The concept of clothing is related to serving in ancient contexts where clothing represented a person's role or duty.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是服从(從)命令。
    - Tā zǒng shì fúcóng mìnglìng.
    - He always obeys orders.
  - 这(這)件衣服很漂亮。
    - Zhè jiàn yīfú hěn piàoliang.
    - This piece of clothing is very beautiful.
  - 我对(對)他的回答感到心服口服。
    - Wǒ duì tā de huídá gǎndào xīnfú kǒufú.
    - I am completely convinced by his answer.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 服](@media/glyph670d.png)
### 服务(務)员(員) → 服 → 凡
- **definition:** tray
- **pinyin:** fán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plate or flat dish ->
    - borrowed for abstract meanings ->
    - unrelated to 几(幾) (jī, 'small table')
  - **interpretation:** 凡 (fán, 'ordinary') originally depicted a flat dish or plate. Over time, it expanded to encompass broader abstract meanings and is unrelated to the character 几(幾) which represents a small table.
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)平凡的人。
    - tā shì gè píngfán de rén.
    - He is an ordinary person.
  - 凡人都可能犯错(錯)，从(從)错(錯)误(誤)中成长(長)。
    - fán rén dōu kěnéng fàncuò, cóng cuòwù zhōng chéngzhǎng.
    - Ordinary people may make mistakes, and grow from them.
  - 他凡去旅行，总(總)能发(發)现(現)新的风(風)景。
    - tā fán qù lǚxíng, zǒng néng fāxiàn xīn de fēngjǐng.
    - Whenever he travels, he always discovers new sceneries.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 凡](@media/glyph51e1.png)
### 服务(務)员(員) → 服 → 𠬝
- **definition:** to subdue
- **pinyin:** [not standardized]
- **components:**
  - 凡
    - fán
    - tray
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠬝 (original pictogram for serving) ->
    - 凡 (fán, 'tray') added as semantic + 𠬝 (fú, 'to subdue') as phonetic ->
    - 服
  - **interpretation:** 𠬝 originally depicted the concept of serving or subduing. When 凡 (fán, 'tray') was added, it contributed to the meaning of serving or submitting, while 𠬝 provided the phonetic component. This later evolved into the character 服.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 𠬝](@media/glyph20b1d.png)
### 服务(務)员(員) → 服 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 服务(務)员(員) → 務
- **definition:** duties; affairs; business
- **pinyin:** wù
- **components:**
  - 敄
    - wù
    - choose, select
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 敄 + semantic 力 ('strength') ->
    - affairs; duties; to attend to
  - **interpretation:** Phonetic 敄 lends the sound, while the semantic component 力 (lì, 'strength') suggests the exertion of effort needed to manage 'affairs' or 'duties.' Essentially, it embodies attending to affairs with effort or strength, linking to the sense of 'to attend to.'
  - **simplification:** 務 (wù) was simplified by removing the component 矛 (máo, 'spear') while keeping the 力 component combined with a simplified form of the phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 小王总(總)是认(認)真负(負)责(責)地处(處)理各项(項)业(業)务(務)。
    - Xiǎo Wáng zǒng shì rènzhēn fùzé de chǔlǐ gè xiàng yèwù.
    - Xiao Wang always handles various tasks diligently and responsibly.
  - 他应(應)对(對)紧(緊)急事务(務)时(時)，表现(現)得很镇(鎮)定。
    - Tā yìngduì jǐnjí shìwù shí, biǎoxiàn de hěn zhèndìng.
    - He remained very calm when dealing with urgent matters.
  - 务(務)必按时(時)完成这(這)个(個)项(項)目。
    - Wùbì ànshí wánchéng zhège xiàngmù.
    - Make sure to complete this project on time.
- **historical forms:**

### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 敄
- **definition:** choose, select
- **pinyin:** wù
- **components:**
  - 矛
    - máo
    - spear
  - 攵
    - pū
    - action
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 矛 (máo, "spear") + semantic 攵 (pū, "action") ->
    - choose, select
  - **interpretation:** The character 敄 combines the phonetic element 矛 (máo, "spear") suggesting the sound, with the semantic element 攵 (pū, "action") indicating an action, leading to the meaning "choose" or "select". The sense of selecting or choosing can be linked to the deliberate action suggested by the semantic component.
- **historical forms:**

### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 敄 → 矛
- **definition:** spear
- **pinyin:** máo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bamboo spear with a ring in the middle ->
    - spear
  - **interpretation:** The character 矛(máo, 'spear') is a pictogram, directly illustrating the shape of a bamboo spear. The design reflects the basic components of the object it represents.
- **examples:**
  - 士兵举(舉)起矛。
    - Shìbīng jǔ qǐ máo.
    - The soldier raised his spear.
  - 古代战(戰)士用矛，冲(衝)锋(鋒)陷阵(陣)。

### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 敄 → 攵
- **definition:** action
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divination
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand 又 (yòu, "hand") holding a tool, stylized as 卜 (bǔ, "divination") ->
    - meaning "to hit"
  - **interpretation:** 攵 is a stylized pictogram originally depicting a hand holding a tool or weapon, representing action or hitting. The hand component evolved into a more uniform stylistic form using 卜 while preserving the core meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 他埋怨我的方式总(總)是冲(衝)动(動)而不经(經)过(過)思考。
    - Tā mányuàn wǒ de fāngshì zǒng shì chōngdòng ér bù jīngguò sīkǎo.
    - He complains that my actions are always impulsive and thoughtless.
  - 需要的不是空谈(談)，而是切实(實)的行动(動)。
    - Xūyào de bù shì kōngtán, ér shì qiēshí de xíngdòng.
    - What is needed is not empty talk, but concrete action.
### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 敄 → 攵 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 敄 → 攵 → 卜
- **definition:** divination
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.

### 服务(務)员(員) → 務 → 力

  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough

- **examples:**

### 服务(務)员(員) → 員
- **definition:** member; person
- **pinyin:** yuán
- **components:**
  - 鼎
    - dǐng
    - ding
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 〇 (round) indicating the top edge of a 鼎 (dǐng, "ding") ->
    - round
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted the top view of a 鼎 (dǐng, "ding"), which is a round ancient cooking vessel, capturing its round shape to convey the concept of 'member' or 'person', as in a complete or rounded group.
  - **simplification:** To simplify 員, 貝 (bèi, "cowry") was reduced to 贝(貝), maintaining the concept while reducing stroke count.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一名优(優)秀的员(員)工。
    - Tā shì yī míng yōuxiù de yuángōng.
    - He is an outstanding employee.
  - 我们(們)团(團)队(隊)需要更多成员(員)。
    - Wǒmen tuánduì xūyào gèng duō chéngyuán.
    - Our team needs more members.
  - 退休后(後)，他不再是公司的职(職)员(員)。
    - Tuìxiū hòu, tā bùzài shì gōngsī de zhíyuán.
    - After retiring, he is no longer an employee of the company.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 員](@media/glyph54e1.png)
### 服务(務)员(員) → 員 → 鼎
- **definition:** ding
- **pinyin:** dǐng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a three-legged bronze vessel ->
    - later used for divination
  - **interpretation:** The character 鼎(dǐng, 'tripod') is a pictogram that depicts a tripod vessel with three legs, symbolizing its use in cooking and ritual sacrifices. Over time, it was also borrowed phonetically to represent the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 商朝的青铜(銅)鼎象征(徵)着(著)权(權)力。
    - Shāng cháo de qīngtóng dǐng xiàngzhēng zhe quánlì.
    - The bronze tripod from the Shang Dynasty symbolizes power.
  - 在古代，鼎是用来(來)烹饪(飪)食物的器具。
    - Zài gǔdài, dǐng shì yòng lái pēngrèn shíwù de qìjù.
    - In ancient times, the tripod was a utensil used for cooking food.
  - 这(這)个(個)博物馆(館)里(裏)展示了一尊精美的铜(銅)鼎。
    - Zhège bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnshì le yī zūn jīngměi de tóngdǐng.
    - This museum exhibits an exquisite bronze tripod.
- **historical forms:**

## 饭(飯)馆(館)
---
## restaurant
### fànguǎn
---
- **traditional:** 飯館
- **definition:** restaurant
- **pinyin:** fànguǎn
- **components:**
  - 饭(飯)
    - fàn
    - meal; cooked rice
  - 馆(館)
    - guǎn
    - building
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 饭(飯) (fàn, "meal; cooked rice") + 馆(館) (guǎn, "building") =
    - a place where meals are served ->
    - restaurant
  - **interpretation:** The term combines 饭(飯) (fàn, "meal; cooked rice"), a fundamental part of Chinese diet, with 馆(館) (guǎn, "building"), indicating a place where meals are prepared and served to guests, which perfectly describes a restaurant.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)去饭(飯)馆(館)吃饭(飯)。
    - Wǒmen qù fànguǎn chī fàn.
    - Let's go eat at a restaurant.
  - 这(這)个(個)饭(飯)馆(館)很热(熱)闹(鬧)，服务(務)态(態)度好。
    - Zhège fànguǎn hěn rènào, fúwù tàidù hǎo.
    - This restaurant is very lively, and the service is good.
  - 小李梦(夢)想着(著)有一天开(開)自己的饭(飯)馆(館)。
    - Xiǎo Lǐ mèngxiǎngzhe yǒu yītiān kāi zìjǐ de fànguǎn.
    - Little Li dreams of one day owning his own restaurant.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯)
- **traditional:** 飯
- **definition:** meal; cooked rice
- **pinyin:** fàn
- **components:**
  - 食
    - shí
    - food
  - 反
    - fǎn
    - return
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 食 (food) + phonetic 反 ->
    - meal
  - **interpretation:** 食 (shí, "food") provides the semantic element indicating the character's relation to food, while 反 (fǎn, "return") provides the sound. The association of 食 with the sound of 反 conveys the concept of 'meal' or 'food to return to'.
  - **simplification:** Simplified by replacing 食 (shí, "food") with 饣, a reduced form.
- **examples:**
  - 每天我都和家人一起吃饭(飯)。
    - Měitiān wǒ dōu hé jiārén yīqǐ chī fàn.
    - Every day, I eat a meal with my family.
  - 他做的晚餐很美味，我吃了两(兩)碗饭(飯)。
    - Tā zuò de wǎncān hěn měiwèi, wǒ chīle liǎng wǎn fàn.
    - The dinner he made was very delicious, I ate two bowls of rice.
  - 饭(飯)后(後)我们(們)去散步。
    - Fàn hòu wǒmen qù sànbù.
    - We go for a walk after the meal.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食
- **definition:** food
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - assemble
  - 𠊊
    - jí
    - bowl with stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:** 亼 (jí, "assemble") over a pictographic bowl of rice on a stand, symbolized by 𠊊 (jí, "bowl with stand")
  - **interpretation:** Initially, the character 食 (shí, "eat") visually represented a mouth over a bowl of rice, conveying the act of eating or a meal intuitively through this imagery.
- **examples:**
  - 他食得很快。
    - Tā shí dé hěn kuài.
    - He eats very quickly.
  - 我准(準)备(備)午食，与(與)朋友共享佳肴(餚)。
    - Wǒ zhǔnbèi wǔ shí, yǔ péngyǒu gòngxiǎng jiāyáo.
    - I am preparing lunch to share a delicious meal with my friends.
  - 民以食为(為)天。
    - Mín yǐ shí wéi tiān.
    - Food is regarded as the most important element for the people.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 亼
- **definition:** assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入座。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生走入校园(園)，开(開)始新学(學)期。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客走入古城，探索历(歷)史。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 入](@media/glyph5165.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 曰](@media/glyph66f0.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 𠊊
- **definition:** bowl with stand
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - mouth
  - 皀
    - jí
    - bowl of rice on a stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (mouth) over 皀 (bowl of rice on a stand) ->
    - depicts a bowl with a stand
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠊊 visually represents a mouth above a bowl of rice on a stand, indicating a utensil or vessel used for holding food. This image directly links to the idea of a 'bowl with stand.' The component 皀 specifically conveys the idea of a container or bowl elevated, which situates its primary meaning in the context of serving or holding food.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 食 → 𠊊 → 皀
- **definition:** bowl of rice on a stand
- **pinyin:** jí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bowl of rice on a stand ->
    - part of the radical 食 (shí, "food")
  - **interpretation:** The character 皀(bá, "acorn") depicts a bowl of rice on a stand, aligning it with food-related imagery.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 皀](@media/glyph7680.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 饭(飯) → 反
- **definition:** return
- **pinyin:** fǎn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand turning or flipping over something ->
    - idea of 'opposite', 'reverse'
  - **interpretation:** The character 反 (fǎn, 'opposite') visually represents the concept of turning something over, which is a physical action associated with reversal or opposites. This intuitive representation connects the physical flip to the abstract idea of opposition.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是反着(著)说(說)话(話)。
    - Tā zǒng shì fǎn zhe shuō huà.
    - He always speaks in the opposite way.
  - 正面思考问(問)题(題)，反面寻(尋)找答案。
    - Zhèngmiàn sīkǎo wèntí, fǎnmiàn xúnzhǎo dá'àn.
    - Consider the problem from a positive perspective; seek solutions from the opposite side.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 反](@media/glyph53cd.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館)
- **traditional:** 館
- **definition:** building
- **pinyin:** guǎn
- **components:**
  - 艮
    - gèn
    - stopping
  - 食
    - shí
    - food
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 艮 (gèn, "stopping") + semantic: 食 (shí, "food") =
    - place associated with food ->
    - building, hall
  - **interpretation:** In 馆(館), the component 艮 (gèn, "stopping") acts as the phonetic element, while 食 (shí, "food") is the semantic component symbolizing a place related to food, thus forming the meaning of a building or hall, particularly one related to eating or gathering.
  - **simplification:** 馆(館): Radicals simplified with 夂 (zhǐ, "go") replacing 食(飠) for visual simplicity while keeping the overall meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 我在图(圖)书(書)馆(館)借阅(閱)书(書)籍。
    - Wǒ zài túshūguǎn jièyuè shūjí.
    - I borrow books at the library.
  - 故宫(宮)博物馆(館)收藏珍贵(貴)文物。
    - Gùgōng bówùguǎn shōucáng zhēnguì wénwù.
    - The Palace Museum collects precious cultural relics.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 艮
- **definition:** stopping
- **pinyin:** gèn
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, 'eye') + 人 (rén, 'person') =
    - a person looking back ->
    - concept of disobedience or limit
  - **interpretation:** The character 艮(gěn) depicts a person turning around to look back, symbolizing hesitation or obstruction. The association with stopping or limiting arises from the act of looking back as a check on forward movement.
- **examples:**
  - 火车(車)在车(車)站艮停。
    - huǒchē zài chēzhàn gěn tíng.
    - The train is stopping at the station.
  - 他前行至半途便艮住。
    - tā qiánxíng zhì bàntú biàn gěn zhù.
    - He stopped halfway through his journey.
  - 研究易经(經)时(時)，学(學)者发(發)现(現)艮象寓意着(著)停止。
    - yánjiū yìjīng shí, xuézhě fāxiàn gěn xiàng yùyì zhe tíngzhǐ.
    - While studying the I Ching, scholars discovered that the image of Gèn implies stopping.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 艮](@media/glyph826e.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 艮 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.

- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.

### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食
- **definition:** food
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - assemble
  - 𠊊
    - jí
    - bowl with stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:** 亼 (jí, "assemble") over a pictographic bowl of rice on a stand, symbolized by 𠊊 (jí, "bowl with stand")
  - **interpretation:** Initially, the character 食 (shí, "eat") visually represented a mouth over a bowl of rice, conveying the act of eating or a meal intuitively through this imagery.
- **examples:**
  - 他食得很快。
    - Tā shí dé hěn kuài.
    - He eats very quickly.
  - 我准(準)备(備)午食，与(與)朋友共享佳肴(餚)。
    - Wǒ zhǔnbèi wǔ shí, yǔ péngyǒu gòngxiǎng jiāyáo.
    - I am preparing lunch to share a delicious meal with my friends.
  - 民以食为(為)天。
    - Mín yǐ shí wéi tiān.
    - Food is regarded as the most important element for the people.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 亼
- **definition:** assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入座。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生走入校园(園)，开(開)始新学(學)期。

### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 亼 → 一

- **pinyin:** yī

  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.

    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'
- **historical forms:**

    - depicts a bowl with a stand
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠊊 visually represents a mouth above a bowl of rice on a stand, indicating a utensil or vessel used for holding food. This image directly links to the idea of a 'bowl with stand.' The component 皀 specifically conveys the idea of a container or bowl elevated, which situates its primary meaning in the context of serving or holding food.
### 饭(飯)馆(館) → 馆(館) → 食 → 𠊊 → 皀

## 多音字
---
## polyphonic character
### duōyīnzì
---
- **definition:** polyphonic character
- **pinyin:** duōyīnzì
- **components:**
  - 多
    - duō
    - many; much
  - 音
    - yīn
    - sound; tone; pitch; pronunciation
  - 字
    - zì
    - character; word; letter; symbol
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 多 (duō, "many") + 音 (yīn, "sound") + 字 (zì, "character"; "word")
  - **interpretation:** The term 多音字 (duōyīnzì) refers to a character that can be pronounced in multiple ways, each possibly with a different meaning. The combination of 多 (duō, "many"), 音 (yīn, "sound"), and 字 (zì, "character") effectively describes a character with multiple pronunciations.
- **examples:**
  - ‘数(數)’是一个(個)多音字。
    - ‘Shù’ shì yīgè duōyīn zì.
    - ‘Shu’ is a polyphonic character.
  - 读(讀)出一个(個)多音字时(時)，需要根据(據)不同的语(語)境。
    - Dú chū yīgè duōyīn zì shí, xūyào gēnjù bùtóng de yǔjìng.
    - When pronouncing a polyphonic character, one needs to consider the different contexts.
### 多音字 → 多
- **definition:** many; much
- **pinyin:** duō
- **components:**
  - 肉
    - ròu
    - meat
  - 夕
    - xī
    - evening
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 肉 (ròu, 'meat') corrupted to 夕 (xī) ->
    - duplicated 夕 =
    - many
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted two pieces of meat 肉 (ròu, 'meat'), suggesting abundance or 'many'. Over time, 肉 was corrupted to 夕 (xī), and the character became a duplication of 夕, signifying multiplicity or 'many'. This aligns with other duplicative characters like 林 (lín, 'forest').
- **examples:**
  - 书(書)架上有很多书(書)。
    - Shūjià shàng yǒu hěn duō shū.
    - There are many books on the shelf.
  - 他工作得比我多。
    - Tā gōngzuò de bǐ wǒ duō.
    - He works more than I do.
  - 多喝水有益健康。
    - Duō hē shuǐ yǒuyì jiànkāng.
    - Drinking more water is beneficial to health.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 多](@media/glyph591a.png)
### 多音字 → 多 → 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of flesh or meat with stripes representing texture.
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉(ròu, "flesh") depicts a piece of meat, meant to evoke the concept of flesh through its visual resemblance to a striped or sectioned piece of meat.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃肉。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like eating meat.
  - 这(這)块(塊)肉很鲜(鮮)美，营(營)养(養)丰(豐)富。
    - Zhè kuài ròu hěn xiānměi, yíngyǎng fēngfù.
    - This piece of meat is very fresh and delicious, and it is nutritious.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 肉](@media/glyph8089.png)
### 多音字 → 多 → 夕
- **definition:** evening
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a moon crescent
  - **interpretation:** The character 夕 (xī, 'evening') is a pictogram that represents a crescent moon, capturing the image of the moon in the evening sky. The comparison to 月 (yuè, 'moon') underscores its depiction of the moon phase commonly associated with evening.
- **examples:**
  - 夕阳(陽)西下。
    - xī yáng xīxià.
    - The setting sun descends.
  - 夕阳(陽)西下，晚风(風)徐徐。
    - xī yáng xīxià, wǎn fēng xúxú.
    - The sun sets as the gentle evening breeze blows.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夕](@media/glyph5915.png)
### 多音字 → 多 → 夕 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 多音字 → 音
- **definition:** sound; tone; pitch; pronunciation
- **pinyin:** yīn
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - word
  - 甘
    - gān
    - sweet
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to say
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 言 (yán, "word") with 甘 (gān, "sweet") ->
    - a depiction of sound emanating from the mouth ->
    - 甘 stylized as 曰 (yuē) ->
    - final form 音
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a word or sound (言) coming from the mouth, initially represented by 甘 as the body of the tongue, which transforms into 曰. This evolution symbolizes the emergence of sound from the mouth, capturing the essence of 'sound' and 'tone.'
- **examples:**
  - 我最喜欢(歡)听(聽)大提琴的声(聲)音。
    - Wǒ zuì xǐhuān tīng dàtíqín de shēngyīn.
    - I love the sound of the cello the most.
  - 她的声(聲)音很悦(悅)耳。
    - Tā de shēngyīn hěn yuè'ěr.
    - Her voice is very pleasant.
  - 音乐(樂)可以抚(撫)慰人心，给(給)生活增添色彩。
    - Yīnyuè kěyǐ fǔwèi rénxīn, gěi shēnghuó zēngtiān sècǎi.
    - Music can soothe the soul and add color to life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 音](@media/glyph97f3.png)
### 多音字 → 音 → 言
- **definition:** word
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他的言语(語)充满(滿)智慧。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)以行动(動)证(證)明我们(們)的言词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他说(說)话(話)的方式显(顯)示了他的修养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 多音字 → 音 → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他的舌非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品尝(嚐)美食时(時)，他的舌细(細)品滋味。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他长(長)舌无(無)忌，经(經)常泄露秘密。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 多音字 → 音 → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 多音字 → 音 → 甘
- **definition:** sweet
- **pinyin:** gān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 𠁿 ->
    - something sweet in an open mouth ->
    - 甘
  - **interpretation:** 甘 (gān, "sweet") is an ideogram depicting something sweet inside an open mouth. This visualization of taste illustrates the core concept of sweetness as directly related to the act of consuming something pleasant. This visual representation connects the sensory experience of sweetness with its meaning in the character.
- **examples:**
  - 蜂蜜很甘。
    - Fēngmì hěn gān.
    - Honey is very sweet.
  - 他的话(話)如甘露滋润(潤)了我的心。
    - Tā de huà rú gānlù zīrùnle wǒ de xīn.
    - His words nourished my heart like sweet dew.
  - 这(這)种(種)水果味道甘美。
    - Zhè zhǒng shuǐguǒ wèidào gān měi.
    - The taste of this fruit is sweet and delicious.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 甘](@media/glyph7518.png)
### 多音字 → 音 → 曰
- **definition:** to say
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 曰](@media/glyph66f0.png)
### 多音字 → 字
- **definition:** character; word; letter; symbol
- **pinyin:** zì
- **components:**
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
  - 宀
    - mián
    - roof
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 子 (zǐ, "child") + 宀 (mián, "roof") =
    - child under a roof ->
    - representation of how children would learn to write characters inside a house ->
    - character
  - **interpretation:** The character 字(zì, "character") combines 子(zǐ, "child") and 宀(mián, "roof") to depict a child learning to write under the protection of a roof. This makes intuitive sense as learning and education traditionally took place at home.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)字很漂亮。
    - Zhège zì hěn piàoliang.
    - This character is very beautiful.
  - 每个(個)字都有故事，蕴(蘊)含着(著)历(歷)史智慧。
    - Měi gè zì dōu yǒu gùshì, yùnhán zhe lìshǐ zhìhuì.
    - Every character has a story, containing the wisdom of history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 字](@media/glyph5b57.png)
### 多音字 → 字 → 子
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 子](@media/glyph5b50.png)
### 多音字 → 字 → 宀
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含有宀的汉(漢)字代表家的温(溫)暖。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋顶(頂)遮风(風)挡(擋)雨，家园(園)散发(發)温(溫)馨。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 宀](@media/glyph5b80.png)

## polyphonic character

## 数(數)
---
## to count
### shǔ
---
- **traditional:** 數
- **definition:** to count
- **pinyin:** shǔ
- **components:**
  - 婁
    - lóu
    - bundle
  - 攴
    - pū
    - tap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic: 婁 (lóu, "bundle") + semantic: 攴 (pū, "tap") =
    - calculating by tapping or marking numbers ->
    - number; count
  - **interpretation:** The character 数(數) (shù, "number; count") combines 婁 (lóu, "bundle") as a phonetic component with 攴 (pū, "tap") as the semantic component, reflecting the action of physically counting or tallying numbers.
- **examples:**
  - 我会(會)数(數)。
    - Wǒ huì shù.
    - I can count.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)教我数(數)，像一、二、三那样(樣)。
    - Māmā jiào wǒ shù, xiàng yī, èr, sān nàyàng.
    - Mom teaches me how to count, like one, two, three.
  - 这(這)个(個)数(數)很大，使人难(難)以计(計)算。
    - Zhège shù hěn dà, shǐ rén nán yǐ jìsuàn.
    - This number is huge, making it hard to calculate.
### 数(數) → 婁
- **definition:** bundle
- **pinyin:** lóu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 数(數) → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爪](@media/glyph722a.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 角
- **definition:** horn
- **pinyin:** jiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an animal horn
  - **interpretation:** The character 角 (jiǎo, "horn") visually represents the distinctive shape of an animal's horn.
- **examples:**
  - 牛角是一种(種)坚(堅)固的天然武器。
    - niú jiǎo shì yī zhǒng jiān gù de tiān rán wǔ qì。
    - Cow horns are sturdy natural weapons.
  - 鹿角丰(豐)富了森林的传(傳)说(說)，象征(徵)着(著)自由与(與)力量。
    - lù jiǎo fēng fù le sēn lín de chuán shuō, xiàng zhēng zhe zì yóu yǔ lì liàng。
    - Deer antlers enrich the legends of the forest and symbolize freedom and strength.
  - 犀牛角在古代被视(視)作珍贵(貴)药(藥)材。
    - xī niú jiǎo zài gǔ dài bèi shì zuò zhēn guì yào cái。
    - Rhinoceros horns were regarded as precious medicinal materials in ancient times.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 角](@media/glyph89d2.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 数(數) → 攴
- **definition:** tap
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)

## 数(數)

## to count
%%%
## 晚上
---
## evening
### wǎnshang
---
- **definition:** evening
- **pinyin:** wǎnshang
- **components:**
  - 晚
    - wǎn
    - evening; late
  - 上
    - shàng
    - up; above; on
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 晚 (wǎn, "evening; late") and 上 (shàng, "up; above; on") combine to depict the concept of evening.
  - **interpretation:** 晚 (wǎn, "evening; late") denotes the time of day after sunset, when activities typically slow down. 上 (shàng, "up; above; on") can give the sense of something being on or upon, here suggesting the time that follows the day being 'upon' us, in the sense of happening now. Together, 晚上 ('evening') describes the period of transition from day to night when it becomes late.
- **examples:**
  - 晚上，我们(們)常常去散步。
    - Wǎnshang, wǒmen chángcháng qù sànbù.
    - In the evening, we often go for a walk.
  - 晚上，星星在天上闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Wǎnshang, xīngxing zài tiān shàng shǎnshuò.
    - In the evening, the stars twinkle in the sky.
  - 我喜欢(歡)晚上喝热(熱)茶。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān wǎnshang hē rè chá.
    - I like drinking hot tea in the evening.
### 晚上 → 晚
- **definition:** evening; late
- **pinyin:** wǎn
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 免
    - miǎn
    - avoid
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic: 日 (rì, "sun") + Phonetic: 免 (miǎn, "avoid") ->
    - time after sunset ->
    - evening
  - **interpretation:** 晚 (wǎn, "evening; late") combines 日 (rì, "sun") to indicate the time of day, and 免 (miǎn, "avoid") as the phonetic component, suggesting the period when the sun is no longer visible.
- **examples:**
  - 现(現)在很晚。
    - Xiànzài hěn wǎn。
    - It is late now.
  - 太阳(陽)下山了，夜幕降临(臨)。
    - Tàiyáng xiàshān le, yèmù jiànglín。
    - The sun has set, and the night has fallen.
### 晚上 → 晚 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免
- **definition:** avoid
- **pinyin:** miǎn
- **components:**
  - 冕
    - miǎn
    - crown
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a man wearing a ceremonial hat ->
    - borrowed for sound and abstract meanings (e.g., 'exempt', 'dismiss', 'avoid') ->
    - 冕 (miǎn, 'crown') confirms original ceremonial context
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a man with a ceremonial hat, which over time became associated with the idea of exemption or dismissal like one being ceremonially released or avoided from obligations. This ceremonial context still lingers in the derived character 冕 (miǎn, 'crown'), reinforcing the visual origin.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)可以免去会(會)议(議)。
    - Wǒmen kěyǐ miǎn qù huìyì.
    - We can dismiss the meeting.
  - 为(為)避免误(誤)解，我们(們)要仔细(細)沟(溝)通。
    - Wèi bìmiǎn wùjiě, wǒmen yào zǐxì gōutōng.
    - To avoid misunderstanding, we need to communicate carefully.
  - 他被免除了责(責)任。
    - Tā bèi miǎnchúle zérèn.
    - He was exempted from responsibility.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 免](@media/glyph514d.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕
- **definition:** crown
- **pinyin:** miǎn
- **components:**
  - 冃
    - mào
    - crown
  - 頁(页)
    - yè
    - head
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 冃 (mào, "crown") + 頁(页) (yè, "head") =
    - crown on a head ->
    - crown
  - **interpretation:** The character 冕(miǎn, "crown") combines 冃 (mào, "crown"), depicting the shape of a crown, with 頁(页) (yè, "head"), representing the positioning on a head. This composition effectively illustrates the concept of a crown being worn on one's head.
- **examples:**
  - 国(國)王戴冕，威仪(儀)四射。
    - Guówáng dài miǎn, wēiyí sìshè.
    - The king wears a crown, exuding majestic authority.
  - 古代帝王的冕象征(徵)着(著)无(無)上的荣(榮)耀。
    - Gǔdài dìwáng de miǎn xiàngzhēngzhe wúshàng de róngyào.
    - The crown of ancient emperors symbolizes supreme glory.
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕 → 冃
- **definition:** crown
- **pinyin:** mào
- **components:**
  - 帽
    - mào
    - hat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hat ->
    - original form of 帽
  - **interpretation:** The character 冃 (mào, "crown") is a pictogram depicting a hat, which serves as the original form for 帽 (mào, "hat") where 冃 appears as the component ⺜. The simplicity of its design reflects its function, representing a crown or cap. Over time, as the meaning became more specific, 帽 incorporated additional components like 巾 (jīn, "cloth") to emphasize its connection to headwear.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 冃](@media/glyph5183.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕 → 冃 → 帽
- **definition:** hat
- **pinyin:** mào
- **components:**
  - 冒
    - mào
    - to risk; to face
  - 巾
    - jīn
    - cloth
  - 冃
    - mào
    - covering
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 冃 ('covering') ->
    - phonetic 冒 + semantic 巾 ('cloth') added ->
    - 帽
  - **interpretation:** The character 帽 originally depicted a covering with the element 冃. By adding 冒 (mào), the phonetic element, and 巾 (jīn, 'cloth'), the semantic component, it specified something that covers the head made of cloth, which logically leads to the meaning 'hat'.
- **examples:**
  - 他戴了一顶(頂)红(紅)色的帽子。
    - Tā dài le yī dǐng hóngsè de màozi.
    - He wore a red hat.
  - 这(這)顶(頂)帽子是我去年买(買)的。
    - Zhè dǐng màozi shì wǒ qùnián mǎi de.
    - This hat is the one I bought last year.
  - 她在商店看见(見)了一顶(頂)漂亮的帽子。
    - Tā zài shāngdiàn kànjiàn le yī dǐng piàoliang de màozi.
    - She saw a beautiful hat at the store.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 帽](@media/glyph5e3d.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕 → 頁
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head; first
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (head/face) + 卩 (kneeling person) ->
    - depicts a person's head and body
  - **interpretation:** Originally represented a head and its body in a kneeling posture, emphasizing “head”. The depiction was extended semantically to represent a 'page', as pages bear leading information like a head does for a body. The concept of 'head' is also reflected in its modern usage as a radical in characters related to parts of the head or face.
  - **simplification:** 页 is a cursive shorthand of the traditional 頁, simplifying the structure while maintaining the core shape of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)打开(開)书(書)的第十页(頁)。
    - Qǐng dǎkāi shū de dì shí yè.
    - Please open to page ten of the book.
  - 这(這)本书(書)每一页(頁)都有插图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū měi yī yè dōu yǒu chātú.
    - Every page of this book has illustrations.
  - 我昨天晚上读(讀)了三十页(頁)。
    - Wǒ zuótiān wǎnshang dúle sānshí yè.
    - I read thirty pages last night.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 頁](@media/glyph9801.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕 → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head; first
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of an animal with a long mouth and horns, often shown with or without hair ( 巛) ->
    - perpetuated as 𩠐 (form with hair) ->
    - streamlined to 首
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts the head of an animal, with prominent features like a long mouth and horns, emphasizing the notion of a 'head' both physically and symbolically as the foremost part.
- **examples:**
  - 他是这(這)个(個)团(團)队(隊)的首领(領)。
    - Tā shì zhège tuánduì de shǒulǐng.
    - He is the head of this team.
  - 这(這)首歌是我最喜欢(歡)的歌曲。
    - Zhè shǒu gē shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de gēqǔ.
    - This song is my favorite track.
  - 他抬起头(頭)，看向远(遠)方的山。
    - Tā tái qǐ tóu, kàn xiàng yuǎnfāng de shān.
    - He raised his head and looked towards the distant mountains.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 首](@media/glyph9996.png)
### 晚上 → 晚 → 免 → 冕 → 頁 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)
### 晚上 → 上
- **definition:** up; above; on
- **pinyin:** shàng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line above another line ->
    - indicates 'up'
  - **interpretation:** The character visually represents a line positioned above another, symbolizing upward direction or the concept of being 'on top.' This simplicity highlights its clear graphical indication of elevation or ascension.
- **examples:**
  - 鸟(鳥)儿(兒)飞(飛)上树(樹)梢。
    - Niǎo'ér fēi shàng shù shāo.
    - The birds fly to the treetops.
  - 他把梯子搭上，爬上屋顶(頂)。
    - Tā bǎ tīzi dā shàng, pá shàng wūdǐng.
    - He set the ladder up and climbed onto the roof.
  - 太阳(陽)从(從)东(東)方升上天边(邊)。
    - Tàiyáng cóng dōngfāng shēng shàng tiānbiān.
    - The sun rises from the east and ascends to the horizon.
- **historical forms:**
