## 数(數)
---
## number
### shù
---
- **traditional:** 數
- **definition:** number
- **pinyin:** shù
- **components:**
  - 婁
    - lóu
    - bundle
  - 攴
    - pū
    - tap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic: 婁 (lóu, "bundle") + semantic: 攴 (pū, "tap") =
    - calculating by tapping or marking numbers ->
    - number; count
  - **interpretation:** The character 数(數) (shù, "number; count") combines 婁 (lóu, "bundle") as a phonetic component with 攴 (pū, "tap") as the semantic component, reflecting the action of physically counting or tallying numbers.
- **examples:**
  - 我会(會)数(數)。
    - Wǒ huì shù.
    - I can count.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)教我数(數)，像一、二、三那样(樣)。
    - Māmā jiào wǒ shù, xiàng yī, èr, sān nàyàng.
    - Mom teaches me how to count, like one, two, three.
  - 这(這)个(個)数(數)很大，使人难(難)以计(計)算。
    - Zhège shù hěn dà, shǐ rén nán yǐ jìsuàn.
    - This number is huge, making it hard to calculate.
### 数(數) → 婁
- **definition:** bundle
- **pinyin:** lóu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 数(數) → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爪](@media/glyph722a.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 角
- **definition:** horn
- **pinyin:** jiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an animal horn
  - **interpretation:** The character 角 (jiǎo, "horn") visually represents the distinctive shape of an animal's horn.
- **examples:**
  - 牛角是一种(種)坚(堅)固的天然武器。
    - niú jiǎo shì yī zhǒng jiān gù de tiān rán wǔ qì。
    - Cow horns are sturdy natural weapons.
  - 鹿角丰(豐)富了森林的传(傳)说(說)，象征(徵)着(著)自由与(與)力量。
    - lù jiǎo fēng fù le sēn lín de chuán shuō, xiàng zhēng zhe zì yóu yǔ lì liàng。
    - Deer antlers enrich the legends of the forest and symbolize freedom and strength.
  - 犀牛角在古代被视(視)作珍贵(貴)药(藥)材。
    - xī niú jiǎo zài gǔ dài bèi shì zuò zhēn guì yào cái。
    - Rhinoceros horns were regarded as precious medicinal materials in ancient times.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 角](@media/glyph89d2.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 数(數) → 婁 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 数(數) → 攴
- **definition:** tap
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 数(數) → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)

## 看一看
---
## take a look
### kàn yī kàn
---
- **definition:** take a look
- **pinyin:** kàn yī kàn
- **components:**
  - 看
    - kàn
    - look; see
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; once
  - 看
    - kàn
    - look; see
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 看 (kàn, "look; see") + 一 (yī, "one; once") + 看 (kàn, "look; see") =
    - take a look
  - **interpretation:** 看 (kàn, "look; see") refers to using one's eyes to observe or inspect. 一 (yī, "one; once") serves to indicate a single action or an attempt, similar to saying 'once' or 'a bit' in English. By having 看 (kàn, "look; see") both before and after 一 (yī, "one"), it emphasizes or softens the action, suggesting a brief or casual glance rather than a thorough examination. It carries the sense of 'taking a moment to see', implying a light or simple action with no deep commitment.
- **examples:**
  - 你可以过(過)来(來)这(這)儿(兒)看一看。
    - Nǐ kěyǐ guòlái zhè'er kàn yī kàn.
    - You can come over here to take a look.
  - 我们(們)去书(書)店看一看，然后(後)再决(決)定。
    - Wǒmen qù shūdiàn kàn yī kàn, ránhòu zài juédìng.
    - Let's go to the bookstore to take a look, then decide.
  - 她想去市场(場)看一看。
    - Tā xiǎng qù shìchǎng kàn yī kàn.
    - She wants to go to the market to take a look.
### 看一看 → 看
- **definition:** look; see
- **pinyin:** kàn
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, "hand") + 目 (mù, "eye") ->
    - hand above eyes to gaze afar ->
    - look
  - **interpretation:** 看(kàn, "look") visually represents the action of shading eyes with one's hand to see more clearly, emphasizing the act of observing or watching.
- **examples:**
  - 你看那只(隻)鸟(鳥)，在枝头(頭)跳跃(躍)。
    - Nǐ kàn nà zhī niǎo, zài zhī tóu tiàoyuè.
    - Look at that bird, it is hopping on the branch.
  - 他看书(書)，仔细(細)研究内(內)容。
    - Tā kàn shū, zǐxì yánjiū nèiróng.
    - He reads the book and carefully examines its contents.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 看](@media/glyph770b.png)
### 看一看 → 看 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 看一看 → 看 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 看一看 → 一
- **definition:** one; once
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)

## 看一下
---
## take a look
### kàn yīxià
---
- **definition:** take a look
- **pinyin:** kàn yīxià
- **components:**
  - 看
    - kàn
    - look
  - 一下
    - yīxià
    - a bit; briefly
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 看 (kàn, "look") + 一下 (yīxià, "a bit; briefly") =
    - combine to form the expression for 'take a brief look'
  - **interpretation:** 看 (kàn, "look") implies directing one's gaze or attention towards something. 一下 (yīxià, "a bit; briefly") indicates a short or brief action. Together, 看一下 expresses the idea of looking or checking something quickly or briefly, capturing the sense of a momentary glance or inspection.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)你看一下。
    - Qǐng nǐ kàn yīxià.
    - Please take a look.
  - 他要过(過)来(來)看看一下，然后(後)决(決)定。
    - Tā yào guòlái kànkàn yīxià, ránhòu juédìng.
    - He will come over to take a look, and then decide.
  - 你可以帮(幫)我看一下这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)吗(嗎)？
    - Nǐ kěyǐ bāng wǒ kàn yīxià zhège wèntí ma?
    - Can you help me take a look at this problem?
### 看一下 → 看

### 看一下 → 一下
- **definition:** a bit; briefly
- **pinyin:** yīxià
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single; whole
  - 下
    - xià
    - down; below; short of; next
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** In this word, 一 (yī, "one") is used to signify a single or brief occurrence, while 下 (xià, "down; below") suggests a short interval. Together, 一下 (yíxià, "a moment") conveys the idea of something happening briefly or temporarily.
  - **interpretation:** The sense 'a moment; a while' emerges because 一 (yī, "one") implies a single or specific instance, and 下 (xià, "down; below") indicates a downward transition or brief action. The combination suggests doing something 'for a single moment' or 'briefly' as if applying an effort or action in a singular, complete manner.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)等一下。
    - Qǐng děng yíxià.
    - Please wait for a moment.
  - 他想休息一下。
    - Tā xiǎng xiūxi yíxià.
    - He wants to rest for a while.
  - 过(過)来(來)一下，我有事情告诉(訴)你。
    - Guòlái yíxià, wǒ yǒu shìqíng gàosù nǐ.
    - Come over for a moment, I have something to tell you.
### 看一下 → 一下 → 一
- **definition:** one; single; whole
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 看一下 → 一下 → 下
- **definition:** down; below; short of; next
- **pinyin:** xià
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - a line below another ->
    - later evolved into 下
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, 'down') is an ideogram showing a line positioned below another line, visually representing 'below' or 'downward'. This layout intuitively depicts the concept of being beneath or beneath another object.
- **examples:**
  - 水从(從)山上流下。
    - Shuǐ cóng shān shàng liú xià.
    - The water flows down from the mountain.
  - 他坐下来(來)看书(書)。
    - Tā zuò xià lái kàn shū.
    - He sits down to read a book.
  - 请(請)把箱子放在地下。
    - Qǐng bǎ xiāngzi fàng zài dìxià.
    - Please put the box down on the ground.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 下](@media/glyph4e0b.png)

## 看看
---
## look
### kànkan
---
- **definition:** look
- **pinyin:** kànkan
- **components:**
  - 看
    - kàn
    - look; watch; read
  - 看
    - kàn
    - look; watch; read
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 看 (kàn, "look") + 看 (kàn, "look") indicates a repeated or brief action, often used to suggest casually looking at something.
  - **interpretation:** The repetition of 看 (kàn, "look") in 看看 (kànkan, "look") conveys a sense of casually or briefly looking at something, not with intense focus but more out of curiosity or to check something quickly.
- **examples:**
  - 你看看书(書)。
    - Nǐ kànkan shū.
    - Take a look at the book.
  - 到公园(園)时(時)，你看看风(風)景。
    - Dào gōngyuán shí, nǐ kànkan fēngjǐng.
    - When you get to the park, take a look at the scenery.
  - 吃饭(飯)前，先看看菜单(單)。
    - Chīfàn qián, xiān kànkan càidān.
    - Before eating, first take a look at the menu.

## 数(數)一下
---
## count it
### shǔ yīxià
---
- **traditional:** 數一下
- **definition:** count it
- **pinyin:** shǔ yīxià
- **components:**
  - 數
    - shǔ
    - count; number; several
  - 一下
    - yīxià
    - a bit; for a moment; briefly
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 數 (shǔ, "count") suggests the act of enumerating or calculating something, while 一下 (yīxià, "a bit; for a moment") refers to doing something quickly or briefly, often for a short duration or an experiment.
  - **interpretation:** 數 (shǔ, "count") specifically refers to the action of counting items or making calculations. 一下 (yīxià, "a bit; for a moment") contributes the sense of immediacy or briefness, implying the counting is done quickly or as a test. Together, the phrase suggests doing a quick count.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)你数(數)一下库(庫)存。
    - Qǐng nǐ shǔ yīxià kùcún.
    - Please count the inventory.
  - 孩子们(們)正在数(數)一下他们(們)的糖果。
    - Háizimen zhèngzài shǔ yīxià tāmen de tángguǒ.
    - The children are counting their candies.
  - 老师(師)让(讓)我们(們)数(數)一下书(書)本的数(數)量。
    - Lǎoshī ràng wǒmen shǔ yīxià shūběn de shùliàng.
    - The teacher asked us to count the number of books.
### 数(數)一下 → 數
- **definition:** count; number; several
- **pinyin:** shǔ
- **components:**
  - 婁
    - lǒu
    - a surname
  - 攴
    - pū
    - tap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 婁 (lǒu) + semantic 攴 (pū, "tap") ->
    - count; number; several
  - **interpretation:** The character 數 combines the phonetic 婁(lǒu) with the semantic 攴 (pū, "tap"), suggesting an action involving counting or enumerating, akin to tapping items or keeping track of numbers. This leads to its meaning of 'count' and 'number'. Over time, the sense extended to 'several,' referring to a count of multiple items.
  - **simplification:** 數 was simplified to 数 by replacing 婁 (lǒu, "a surname") with its simpler variant 娄(婁).
- **examples:**
  - 我开(開)始数(數)星星。
    - Wǒ kāishǐ shǔ xīngxīng.
    - I started counting the stars.
  - 这(這)几(幾)天，我有很多事情要处(處)理。
    - Zhè jǐ tiān, wǒ yǒu hěn duō shìqíng yào chǔlǐ.
    - In the past few days, I have had many things to handle.
  - 数(數)一数(數)，看看我们(們)有多少苹(蘋)果。
    - Shǔ yī shǔ, kàn kàn wǒmen yǒu duōshǎo píngguǒ.
    - Count and see how many apples we have.
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁
- **definition:** a surname
- **pinyin:** lǒu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爪](@media/glyph722a.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁 → 角
- **definition:** horn
- **pinyin:** jiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an animal horn
  - **interpretation:** The character 角 (jiǎo, "horn") visually represents the distinctive shape of an animal's horn.
- **examples:**
  - 牛角是一种(種)坚(堅)固的天然武器。
    - niú jiǎo shì yī zhǒng jiān gù de tiān rán wǔ qì。
    - Cow horns are sturdy natural weapons.
  - 鹿角丰(豐)富了森林的传(傳)说(說)，象征(徵)着(著)自由与(與)力量。
    - lù jiǎo fēng fù le sēn lín de chuán shuō, xiàng zhēng zhe zì yóu yǔ lì liàng。
    - Deer antlers enrich the legends of the forest and symbolize freedom and strength.
  - 犀牛角在古代被视(視)作珍贵(貴)药(藥)材。
    - xī niú jiǎo zài gǔ dài bèi shì zuò zhēn guì yào cái。
    - Rhinoceros horns were regarded as precious medicinal materials in ancient times.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 角](@media/glyph89d2.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 婁 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 攴
- **definition:** tap
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 數 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 一下
- **definition:** a bit; for a moment; briefly
- **pinyin:** yīxià
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single; whole
  - 下
    - xià
    - down; below; short of; next
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** In this word, 一 (yī, "one") is used to signify a single or brief occurrence, while 下 (xià, "down; below") suggests a short interval. Together, 一下 (yíxià, "a moment") conveys the idea of something happening briefly or temporarily.
  - **interpretation:** The sense 'a moment; a while' emerges because 一 (yī, "one") implies a single or specific instance, and 下 (xià, "down; below") indicates a downward transition or brief action. The combination suggests doing something 'for a single moment' or 'briefly' as if applying an effort or action in a singular, complete manner.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)等一下。
    - Qǐng děng yíxià.
    - Please wait for a moment.
  - 他想休息一下。
    - Tā xiǎng xiūxi yíxià.
    - He wants to rest for a while.
  - 过(過)来(來)一下，我有事情告诉(訴)你。
    - Guòlái yíxià, wǒ yǒu shìqíng gàosù nǐ.
    - Come over for a moment, I have something to tell you.
### 数(數)一下 → 一下 → 一
- **definition:** one; single; whole
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 数(數)一下 → 一下 → 下
- **definition:** down; below; short of; next
- **pinyin:** xià
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - a line below another ->
    - later evolved into 下
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, 'down') is an ideogram showing a line positioned below another line, visually representing 'below' or 'downward'. This layout intuitively depicts the concept of being beneath or beneath another object.
- **examples:**
  - 水从(從)山上流下。
    - Shuǐ cóng shān shàng liú xià.
    - The water flows down from the mountain.
  - 他坐下来(來)看书(書)。
    - Tā zuò xià lái kàn shū.
    - He sits down to read a book.
  - 请(請)把箱子放在地下。
    - Qǐng bǎ xiāngzi fàng zài dìxià.
    - Please put the box down on the ground.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 下](@media/glyph4e0b.png)
---
## 数(數)一下
### shǔ yīxià
---
## count it
%%%
## 数(數)一数(數)
---
## count
### shǔ yī shǔ
---
- **traditional:** 數一數
- **definition:** count
- **pinyin:** shǔ yī shǔ
- **components:**
  - 數
    - shǔ
    - count
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single
  - 數
    - shǔ
    - count
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 數 (shǔ, "count") + 一 (yī, "one/single") + 數 (shǔ, "count")
  - **interpretation:** 數 (shǔ, "count") expresses the core action of recounting or numbering. When paired with 一 (yī, "one/single") and repeated as 數 (shǔ), the phrase creates an emphasis on the act of counting, as if to say "count each one attentively." Here, 一 (yī, "one/single") highlights the precision in the act of counting, ensuring attention to each single unit.
- **examples:**
  - 他开(開)始数(數)一数(數)手里(裡)的硬币(幣)。
    - Tā kāishǐ shǔ yī shǔ shǒulǐ de yìngbì.
    - He started to count the coins in his hand.
  - 老师(師)让(讓)我们(們)数(數)一数(數)桌上的书(書)。
    - Lǎoshī ràng wǒmen shǔ yī shǔ zhuō shàng de shū.
    - The teacher asked us to count the books on the table.
  - 请(請)你数(數)一数(數)这(這)些苹(蘋)果，看有多少个(個)。
    - Qǐng nǐ shǔ yī shǔ zhèxiē píngguǒ, kàn yǒu duōshǎo gè.
    - Please count these apples and see how many there are.
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數
- **definition:** count
- **pinyin:** shǔ
- **components:**
  - 婁
    - lǒu
    - a surname
  - 攴
    - pū
    - tap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 婁 (lǒu) + semantic 攴 (pū, "tap") ->
    - count; number; several
  - **interpretation:** The character 數 combines the phonetic 婁(lǒu) with the semantic 攴 (pū, "tap"), suggesting an action involving counting or enumerating, akin to tapping items or keeping track of numbers. This leads to its meaning of 'count' and 'number'. Over time, the sense extended to 'several,' referring to a count of multiple items.
  - **simplification:** 數 was simplified to 数 by replacing 婁 (lǒu, "a surname") with its simpler variant 娄(婁).
- **examples:**
  - 我开(開)始数(數)星星。
    - Wǒ kāishǐ shǔ xīngxīng.
    - I started counting the stars.
  - 这(這)几(幾)天，我有很多事情要处(處)理。
    - Zhè jǐ tiān, wǒ yǒu hěn duō shìqíng yào chǔlǐ.
    - In the past few days, I have had many things to handle.
  - 数(數)一数(數)，看看我们(們)有多少苹(蘋)果。
    - Shǔ yī shǔ, kàn kàn wǒmen yǒu duōshǎo píngguǒ.
    - Count and see how many apples we have.
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 婁
- **definition:** a surname
- **pinyin:** lǒu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.

### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 攴
- **definition:** tap
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 数(數)一数(數) → 數 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)
### 数(數)一数(數) → 一
- **definition:** one; single
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)

## 数(數)一数(數)
### shǔ yī shǔ
---
## count
%%%
## 数(數)数(數)
---
## count
### shǔ shù
---
- **traditional:** 數數
- **definition:** count
- **pinyin:** shǔ shù
- **components:**
  - 數
    - shǔ
    - count; enumerate
  - 數
    - shù
    - number; figure; count
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 數 (shǔ, "count") is the verb for counting in Chinese, often referring to the act of enumerating items or numbers. 數 (shù, "number") is the noun that refers to numbers themselves. This combination highlights the interplay between counting as an action and numbers as a concept.
  - **interpretation:** 數 (shǔ, "count") captures the active process of determining quantity by enumeration. 數 (shù, "number") embodies the result of that process, the abstract concept of numerals. Together, summing up a specific counting activity with its numerical result creates the cohesive action of 'counting numbers' or simply 'count'.
- **examples:**
  - 孩子在学(學)着(著)数(數)数(數)。
    - Háizi zài xuézhe shǔ shù.
    - The child is learning to count.
  - 我们(們)来(來)数(數)数(數)聚会(會)的人数(數)。
    - Wǒmen lái shǔ shù jùhuì de rénshù.
    - Let's count the number of people at the party.
  - 老师(師)让(讓)学(學)生数(數)数(數)，练(練)习(習)加法。
    - Lǎoshī ràng xuéshēng shǔ shù, liànxí jiāfǎ.
    - The teacher asked the students to count and practice addition.
### 数(數)数(數) → 數
- **definition:** count; enumerate
- **pinyin:** shǔ
- **components:**
  - 婁
    - lǒu
    - a surname
  - 攴
    - pū
    - tap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 婁 (lǒu) + semantic 攴 (pū, "tap") ->
    - count; number; several
  - **interpretation:** The character 數 combines the phonetic 婁(lǒu) with the semantic 攴 (pū, "tap"), suggesting an action involving counting or enumerating, akin to tapping items or keeping track of numbers. This leads to its meaning of 'count' and 'number'. Over time, the sense extended to 'several,' referring to a count of multiple items.
  - **simplification:** 數 was simplified to 数 by replacing 婁 (lǒu, "a surname") with its simpler variant 娄(婁).
- **examples:**
  - 我开(開)始数(數)星星。
    - Wǒ kāishǐ shǔ xīngxīng.
    - I started counting the stars.
  - 这(這)几(幾)天，我有很多事情要处(處)理。
    - Zhè jǐ tiān, wǒ yǒu hěn duō shìqíng yào chǔlǐ.
    - In the past few days, I have had many things to handle.
  - 数(數)一数(數)，看看我们(們)有多少苹(蘋)果。
    - Shǔ yī shǔ, kàn kàn wǒmen yǒu duōshǎo píngguǒ.
    - Count and see how many apples we have.
### 数(數)数(數) → 數 → 婁
- **definition:** a surname
- **pinyin:** lǒu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 数(數)数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爪](@media/glyph722a.png)
### 数(數)数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 角
- **definition:** horn
- **pinyin:** jiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an animal horn
  - **interpretation:** The character 角 (jiǎo, "horn") visually represents the distinctive shape of an animal's horn.
- **examples:**
  - 牛角是一种(種)坚(堅)固的天然武器。
    - niú jiǎo shì yī zhǒng jiān gù de tiān rán wǔ qì。
    - Cow horns are sturdy natural weapons.
  - 鹿角丰(豐)富了森林的传(傳)说(說)，象征(徵)着(著)自由与(與)力量。
    - lù jiǎo fēng fù le sēn lín de chuán shuō, xiàng zhēng zhe zì yóu yǔ lì liàng。
    - Deer antlers enrich the legends of the forest and symbolize freedom and strength.
  - 犀牛角在古代被视(視)作珍贵(貴)药(藥)材。
    - xī niú jiǎo zài gǔ dài bèi shì zuò zhēn guì yào cái。
    - Rhinoceros horns were regarded as precious medicinal materials in ancient times.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 角](@media/glyph89d2.png)
### 数(數)数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 数(數)数(數) → 數 → 婁 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)

- **pinyin:** zhōng

This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.

    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.

## 林
---
## a surname
### Lín
---
- **definition:** a surname
- **pinyin:** Lín
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, "tree") + 木 (mù, "tree") =
    - multiple trees ->
    - forest
  - **interpretation:** 林 (lín, "forest") uses the repetition of 木 (mù, "tree") to visually and conceptually represent a forest, which consists of many trees grouped together. This ideogram effectively captures the collective meaning through duplication.
- **examples:**
  - 我走进(進)幽静(靜)的林。
    - Wǒ zǒu jìn yōujìng de lín.
    - I walked into the quiet forest.
  - 孩子们(們)在林中围(圍)成一圈，嬉戏(戲)声(聲)此起彼伏。
    - Háizimen zài lín zhōng wéi chéng yī quān, xīxì shēng cǐ qǐ bǐ fú.
    - The children formed a circle in the forest, and their laughter echoed continuously.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 林](@media/glyph6797.png)
### 林 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)

## 娜
---
## a name
### Nà
---
- **definition:** a name
- **pinyin:** Nà
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 那
    - nà
    - that
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + 那 (nà, "that") =
    - semantic element indicating femininity + phonetic element providing pronunciation ->
    - used as a feminine name component/
  - **interpretation:** 娜 (nà, "a name") combines 女 to indicate a female name or noun, and phonetic 那 to provide the pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 娜老师(師)。
    - Nà lǎoshī。
    - Teacher Na.
  - 我叫娜。
    - Wǒ jiào Nà。
    - My name is Na.
  - 娜在校园(園)中努力学(學)习(習)。
    - Nà zài xiàoyuán zhōng nǔlì xuéxí。
    - Na studies hard on campus.
### 娜 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 娜 → 那
- **definition:** that
- **pinyin:** nà
- **components:**
  - 冄
    - njam
    - to shine
  - 邑
    - yì
    - city
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** phonetic 冄(njam, "to shine") + semantic 邑 (yì, "city")
  - **interpretation:** The character 那(nà, "that") originally served as the name of a state, with 冄 suggesting its sound, while 邑 indicates a place or territory. It was later borrowed to denote the demonstrative 'that', reflecting the concept of something distant or separate like a distinct location or city.
- **examples:**
  - 那个(個)人是我的老师(師)。
    - Nà gè rén shì wǒ de lǎoshī.
    - That person is my teacher.
  - 我想要那本书(書)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng yào nà běn shū.
    - I want that book.
  - 那是一段难(難)忘的经(經)历(歷)。
    - Nà shì yī duàn nánwàng de jīnglì.
    - That was an unforgettable experience.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 那](@media/glyph90a3.png)
### 娜 → 那 → 冄
- **definition:** to shine
- **pinyin:** njam
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hairy object
  - **interpretation:** The character 冄(rǎn, "obscure") is a pictogram representing a hairy object. Its original depiction relates to its long, hanging appearance, resembling strands or tufts, evoking obscurity or indistinctness in its metaphorical sense.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 冄](@media/glyph5184.png)
### 娜 → 那 → 邑
- **definition:** city
- **pinyin:** yì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a walled settlement with an enclosure and a road leading to it ->
    - town or city
  - **interpretation:** 邑 (yì, "town; city") originates from a pictogram representing a place enclosed by walls, characteristic of ancient cities with roads leading into them.
- **examples:**
  - 他游览(覽)了那座邑，感受到了浓(濃)厚的历(歷)史气(氣)息。
    - Tā yóulǎn le nà zuò yì, gǎnshòu dào le nónghòu de lìshǐ qìxī.
    - He toured that town and experienced its rich historical atmosphere.
  - 这(這)个(個)邑依山傍水，生活节(節)奏缓(緩)慢。
    - Zhège yì yī shān bàng shuǐ, shēnghuó jiézòu huǎn màn.
    - This town is nestled by the mountains and rivers, and its pace of life is slow.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 邑](@media/glyph9091.png)

## 换(換)
---
## to exchange
### huàn
---
- **traditional:** 換
- **definition:** to exchange
- **pinyin:** huàn
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 奐
    - huàn
    - abundant
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 手 (shǒu, "hand") + phonetic 奐 (huàn)
  - **interpretation:** The character 换(換) uses the semantic part 手 (shǒu, "hand") to signify an action typically performed by the hand, such as exchanging or swapping. The phonetic 奐 (huàn) provides the pronunciation, and together they indicate the act of using hands to make an exchange.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 換 switched from 手 (shǒu, "hand") to 扌, the simplified hand radical, and retained 奐 (huàn) for phonetic purpose.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)帮(幫)我换(換)桌子。
    - Qǐng bāng wǒ huàn zhuōzi.
    - Please help me exchange the table.
  - 如果你不喜欢(歡)这(這)件衣服，可以去店里(裡)换(換)另一件。
    - Rúguǒ nǐ bù xǐhuān zhè jiàn yīfu, kěyǐ qù diàn lǐ huàn lìng yī jiàn.
    - If you don't like this piece of clothing, you can go to the store to exchange it for another.
  - 我每两(兩)个(個)月换(換)一次手机(機)壳(殼)。
    - Wǒ měi liǎng gè yuè huàn yīcì shǒujī ké.
    - I change my phone case every two months.
### 换(換) → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 换(換) → 奐
- **definition:** abundant
- **pinyin:** huàn
- **components:**
  - 夐
    - xiòng
    - eminent
  - 廾
    - gǒng
    - hands
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 夐 (phonetic, indicating 'eminent') + 廾 (hands, 'numerous') ->
    - 'brilliant', 'abundant'
  - **interpretation:** The character 奐 (huàn, 'eminent; abundant') combines the phonetic element 夐 with the semantic element 廾, representing hands, which implies abundance or copiousness. This idea is further supported by oracle bone scripts where the hands symbolized numerous objects. While it also represented the idea of 'brilliant' due to its ancient context of authority, it was used phonetically in the context of 換 (huàn, 'change'). The ideogrammatic explanation suggests hands opening a yurt to let in sunlight, further linking to 'brilliant'.
  - **simplification:** Simplified to 奂 by removing strokes for ease of writing.
### 换(換) → 奐 → 夐
- **definition:** eminent
- **pinyin:** xiòng
- **components:**
  - 穴
    - xué
    - cave; yurt
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 支
    - zhī
    - to support
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 穴 (xué, 'cave; yurt') with 目 (mù, 'eye') + a hand with a stick like 支 (zhī, 'to support') indicating authority ->
    - concept of 'eminent'
  - **interpretation:** The character 夐 combines the elements of a cave or yurt, an eye, and a hand holding a stick. These components collectively symbolize a figure of authority, representing the idea of 'eminent'. The presence of a hand with a stick suggests control or command, reinforcing the leader or prominent person's status.
### 换(換) → 奐 → 夐 → 穴
- **definition:** cave; yurt
- **pinyin:** xué
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a cave or hole, resembling a small dwelling or opening
  - **interpretation:** The character 穴 (xué, "cave") visually represents a hole or cave with an open entry, suggesting a sheltered space similar to a primitive dwelling or burrow.
- **examples:**
  - 山里(裡)隐(隱)匿着(著)一个(個)深深的穴。
    - Shān lǐ yǐn nì zhe yí gè shēn shēn de xué.
    - A deep cave is hidden in the mountains.
  - 探险(險)家在悬(懸)崖下发(發)现(現)了一个(個)幽静(靜)的穴，据(據)说(說)里(裡)面住着(著)古老的精灵(靈)。
    - Tàn xiǎnjiā zài xuán yá xià fāxiàn le yí gè yōu jìng de xué, jù shuō lǐmiàn zhùzhe gǔlǎo de jīng líng.
    - The explorer discovered a quiet cave beneath the cliff, and it is said that ancient spirits dwell inside.
  - 河岸边(邊)的岩石上有一个(個)小穴。
    - Hé àn biān de yán shí shàng yǒu yí gè xiǎo xué.
    - There is a small cave on the rock by the riverbank.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 穴](@media/glyph7a74.png)
### 换(換) → 奐 → 夐 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 换(換) → 奐 → 夐 → 支
- **definition:** to support
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand holding a drumstick
  - **interpretation:** The character 支 (zhī, 'hand holding drumstick') visually represents a hand grasping a stick-like object, suggesting support or physical action, which aligns with its meanings related to branching or supporting.
- **examples:**
  - 他支鼓槌，敲响(響)大鼓。
    - Tā zhī gǔchuí, qiāo xiǎng dà gǔ.
    - He holds the drumstick and strikes the big drum.
  - 鼓手支着(著)鼓槌，打出动(動)人节(節)奏。
    - Gǔshǒu zhī zhe gǔchuí, dǎ chū dòngrén jiézòu.
    - The drummer holds the drumstick and produces a captivating rhythm.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 支](@media/glyph652f.png)
### 换(換) → 奐 → 廾
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** gǒng
- **components:**
  - 𠂇
    - shǒu
    - left hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - right hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠂇 (left hand) + 又 (right hand) =
    - two hands
  - **interpretation:** The character combines depictions of the left hand 𠂇 and the right hand 又, representing the concept of using both hands together. This combination naturally conveys the meaning of 'two hands.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廾](@media/glyph5efe.png)
### 换(換) → 奐 → 廾 → 𠂇
- **definition:** left hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - again
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 又 (yòu, "again") flipped, representing a left hand.
  - **interpretation:** 𠂇 is a pictogram representing a left hand, visually derived from the character 又 (yòu, "again") by flipping it.
### 换(換) → 奐 → 廾 → 𠂇 → 又
- **definition:** again
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)

## 早上
---
## morning
### zǎoshang
---
- **definition:** morning
- **pinyin:** zǎoshang
- **components:**
  - 早
    - zǎo
    - early
  - 上
    - shàng
    - above; upper; on top
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 早 (zǎo, "early") indicates the early part of the day, while 上 (shàng, "above; upper; on top") suggests the beginning or upper/first segment of the day. Together they indicate the 'morning', the early part that comes before the main part of the day.
  - **interpretation:** 早 (zǎo, "early") signifies the time when activities typically begin. As the sun rises from the horizon, it marks the transition from night to day. 上 (shàng, "above; upper; on top") conveys the upper half of the day after night, delineating the morning as the start or upper section of the daytime sequence.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天早上都去跑步。
    - Wǒ měitiān zǎoshang dōu qù pǎobù.
    - I go jogging every morning.
  - 早上的空气(氣)很清新。
    - Zǎoshang de kōngqì hěn qīngxīn.
    - The morning air is very fresh.
  - 我们(們)计(計)划(劃)在早上出发(發)。
    - Wǒmen jìhuà zài zǎoshang chūfā.
    - We plan to depart in the morning.
### 早上 → 早
- **definition:** early
- **pinyin:** zǎo
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 甲
    - jiǎ
    - first
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - Early pictogram depicts an acorn ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'morning' ->
    - Late bronze inscriptions: semantic 日 (rì, 'sun') + phonetic 棗(枣) (zǎo) ->
    - small seal script: 日(日, 'sun') + 甲(甲, 'first') =
    - when the sun first rises ->
    - 'early'
  - **interpretation:** The character evolved from depicting an acorn to incorporating the image of the sun and the concept of 'first,' symbolizing the sun's rise to indicate 'early.' It's a combination of both semantic elements and phonetic borrowing.
- **examples:**
  - 我今天起床很早。
    - Wǒ jīntiān qǐchuáng hěn zǎo.
    - I woke up very early today.
  - 他早到办(辦)公室，开(開)始了紧(緊)张(張)的会(會)议(議)。
    - Tā zǎo dào bàngōngshì, kāishǐ le jǐnzhāng de huìyì.
    - He arrived at the office early and started a busy meeting.
  - 他喜欢(歡)早睡，早起的习(習)惯(慣)让(讓)他精力充沛。
    - Tā xǐhuān zǎo shuì, zǎo qǐ de xíguàn ràng tā jīnglì chōngpèi.
    - He likes going to bed early, and his habit of getting up early makes him energetic.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 早](@media/glyph65e9.png)
### 早上 → 早 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 早上 → 早 → 甲
- **definition:** first
- **pinyin:** jiǎ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the shape of a suit of armor with overlapping plates
  - **interpretation:** The character 甲 (jiǎ, 'armor') is a pictogram representing a stylized view of a suit of armor consisting of overlapping plates, suggesting protection and covering.
- **examples:**
  - 骑(騎)士穿戴甲，保卫(衛)国(國)家。
    - Qíshì chuāndài jiǎ, bǎowèi guójiā.
    - The knight dons the armor, defending the country.
  - 古代兵士依靠甲，抵御(禦)强(強)敌(敵)。
    - Gǔdài bīngshì yīkào jiǎ, dǐyù qiángdí.
    - Ancient soldiers relied on armor, repelling formidable enemies.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 甲](@media/glyph7532.png)
### 早上 → 上
- **definition:** above; upper; on top
- **pinyin:** shàng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line above another line ->
    - indicates 'up'
  - **interpretation:** The character visually represents a line positioned above another, symbolizing upward direction or the concept of being 'on top.' This simplicity highlights its clear graphical indication of elevation or ascension.
- **examples:**
  - 鸟(鳥)儿(兒)飞(飛)上树(樹)梢。
    - Niǎo'ér fēi shàng shù shāo.
    - The birds fly to the treetops.
  - 他把梯子搭上，爬上屋顶(頂)。
    - Tā bǎ tīzi dā shàng, pá shàng wūdǐng.
    - He set the ladder up and climbed onto the roof.
  - 太阳(陽)从(從)东(東)方升上天边(邊)。
    - Tàiyáng cóng dōngfāng shēng shàng tiānbiān.
    - The sun rises from the east and ascends to the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 上](@media/glyph4e0a.png)

## 早上
### zǎoshang

## 块(塊)
---
## buck; piece
### kuài
---
- **traditional:** 塊
- **definition:** buck; piece
- **pinyin:** kuài
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 鬼
    - guǐ
    - ghost
  - 夬
    - guài
    - decisive
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 土 (tǔ, "earth") + phonetic 鬼 (guǐ, "ghost") ->
    - clod of dirt ->
    - piece
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 土 (tǔ, "earth") to indicate a material aspect with 鬼 (guǐ, "ghost") for its phonetic component, representing a clod or chunk of earth, which extends metaphorically to the meaning of a 'piece' or 'buck'.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 块 replaces the phonetic 鬼 (guǐ, "ghost") with 夬 (guài), which was chosen for its simpler form yet related phonetic value.
- **examples:**
  - 三块(塊)钱(錢)。
    - Sān kuài qián.
    - Three bucks.
  - 这(這)块(塊)蛋糕很好吃。
    - Zhè kuài dàngāo hěn hǎochī.
    - This piece of cake is delicious.
  - 孩子们(們)用五块(塊)木头(頭)，搭建了小屋。
    - Háizimen yòng wǔ kuài mùtou, dājiàn le xiǎowū.
    - The children used five pieces of wood to build a small house.
### 块(塊) → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 土](@media/glyph571f.png)
### 块(塊) → 鬼
- **definition:** ghost
- **pinyin:** guǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling man or figure with an ugly face (甶) + small 厶 (trace of tail) added later
  - **interpretation:** The character 鬼 (guǐ, "demon") visually represents a kneeling figure with a distinctive, mask-like face, evoking the image of a supernatural being or ghost. The addition of a small 厶 suggests a residual tail, enhancing its demon-like appearance. This depiction highlights the character's association with eerie, otherworldly entities.
- **examples:**
  - 深夜独(獨)行时(時)，忽遇鬼影飘(飄)忽。
    - Shēnyè dúxíng shí, hū yù guǐ yǐng piāohū.
    - Walking alone in the deep night, suddenly encountering a fleeting ghostly silhouette.
  - 村里(裡)流传(傳)故事说(說)鬼出没(沒)，人们(們)夜半小心提灯(燈)。
    - Cūn lǐ liúchuán gùshì shuō guǐ chūmò, rénmen yèbàn xiǎoxīn tí dēng.
    - Stories circulate in the village that demons haunt the area, so people cautiously carry lanterns at midnight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 鬼](@media/glyph9b3c.png)
### 块(塊) → 夬
- **definition:** decisive
- **pinyin:** guài
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand wearing an archer's thumb ring
  - **interpretation:** The character 夬 (guài, "decisive") originally depicts a hand wearing an archer's thumb ring, emphasizing the concept of decisiveness or resolution, as this ring is essential for drawing a bowstring.
- **examples:**
  - 他的性格很夬，所以在关键时刻总能做出正确的决(決)定(策)。
    - Tā de xìnggé hěn guài, suǒyǐ zài guānjiàn shíkè zǒng néng zuò chū zhèngquè de juécè.
    - He has a decisive personality, so he can always make the right decisions at critical moments.
  - 在处理危机(機)时(時)，她总是显得异常夬，从未退缩(縮)。
    - Zài chǔlǐ wēijī shí, tā zǒng shì xiǎndé yìcháng guài, cóngwèi tuìsuō.
    - When dealing with crises, she always appears exceptionally decisive and never retreats.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夬](@media/glyph592c.png)

- **examples:**
