## 旅行
---
## to travel
### lǚxíng
---
- **definition:** to travel
- **pinyin:** lǚxíng
- **components:**
  - 旅
    - lǚ
    - trip; journey; travel
  - 行
    - xíng
    - to go; to walk; behavior; conduct
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 旅 (lǚ, "trip") refers to a journey or expedition. 行 (xíng, "to go; to walk") involves the action of moving or proceeding. Together, 旅行 (lǚxíng) literally means "to go on a trip," corresponding directly to the meaning "to travel."
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)旅行。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān lǚxíng.
    - I like to travel.
  - 我们(們)计(計)划(劃)下个(個)月去旅行。
    - Wǒmen jìhuà xià gè yuè qù lǚxíng.
    - We are planning to travel next month.
  - 他想去欧(歐)洲旅行，体(體)验(驗)不同的文化。
    - Tā xiǎng qù Ōuzhōu lǚxíng, tǐyàn bùtóng de wénhuà.
    - He wants to travel to Europe to experience different cultures.
### 旅行 → 旅
- **definition:** trip; journey; travel
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **components:**
  - 㫃
    - bì
    - flag
  - 从(從)
    - cóng
    - two people
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 㫃 ("flag") + 从 ("two people") =
    - flag indicating journey with companions ->
    - brigade ->
    - travel
  - **interpretation:** The character combines a flag, symbolizing guidance or direction, with two people, indicating a journey or movement undertaken together, thus forming the concept of traveling in a group.
- **examples:**
  - 我准(準)备(備)踏上旅程，寻(尋)找失落的记(記)忆(憶)。
    - wǒ zhǔnbèi tà shàng lǚchéng ， xún zhǎo shī luò de jìyì。
    - I am ready to set off on a journey, searching for lost memories.
  - 她喜爱(愛)旅途中发(發)现(現)未知的美丽(麗)。
    - tā xǐ'ài lǚtú zhōng fāxiàn wèi zhī de měilì。
    - She loves discovering unknown beauty during her journey.
  - 兄弟们(們)相聚在旅途，分享各自的故事。
    - xiōngdìmen xiāng jù zài lǚtú ， fēnxiǎng gèzì de gùshì。
    - Brothers gather on the journey, sharing their stories.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 旅](@media/glyph65c5.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 㫃
- **definition:** flag
- **pinyin:** bì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a flag on a pole with a decoration on top ->
    - stylized as 方(㫃)
  - **interpretation:** The character 㫃 originally depicted a flag on a pole, complete with a decorative element on top. Over time, it was stylized into its current form with the flag and pole disconnected and the image abstracted as 方(㫃). Although it shares visual similarities with characters like 朝 (cháo, "morning"), it is unrelated to them in meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 撤下军(軍)㫃。
    - Chèxià jūn bì.
    - Take down the military flag.
  - 他站在城楼(樓)上挥(揮)动(動)㫃。
    - Tā zhàn zài chénglóu shàng huīdòng bì.
    - He waved the flag on the city gate tower.
  - 大风(風)把祭典上的㫃吹得猎(獵)猎(獵)作响(響)。
    - Dàfēng bǎ jìdiǎn shàng de bì chuī dé liè liè zuò xiǎng.
    - The strong wind made the flag at the ceremony flutter noisily.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 㫃](@media/glyph3ac3.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從)
- **traditional:** 從
- **definition:** two people
- **pinyin:** cóng
- **components:**
  - 辵
    - chuò
    - walk; movement
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 辵 ('walk; movement') + phonetic 从 (sound) ->
    - follow
  - **interpretation:** 從 (cóng, 'to follow') combines the idea of 'walking' or 'movement' from 辵 (chuò, 'walk; movement') with the sound symbolized by 从 (cóng, 'follow'), capturing the concept of moving along a path under guidance or direction.
  - **simplification:** 从 is a variant form directly used as the simplified form, adopting the earlier, less complex writing as the standard.
- **examples:**
  - 你需要从(從)这(這)里(裡)开(開)始。
    - Nǐ xūyào cóng zhèlǐ kāishǐ.
    - You need to start from here.
  - 她从(從)小就喜欢(歡)画(畫)画(畫)。
    - Tā cóngxiǎo jiù xǐhuān huàhuà.
    - She has liked drawing since she was a child.
  - 所有东(東)西都从(從)他的袋子里(裡)掉出来(來)了。
    - Suǒyǒu dōngxī dōu cóng tā de dàizi lǐ diào chūláile.
    - Everything fell out of his bag.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 从](@media/glyph4ece.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵
- **definition:** walk; movement
- **pinyin:** chuò
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - walk
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 彳 (chì, "walk") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop") ->
    - 𣥆 ->
    - stylized as 龰 ->
    - 辵
  - **interpretation:** The character 辵 combines 彳 (chì, "walk"), which represents movement, with 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop"), suggesting the concept of stepping or traveling forward. This character represents the idea of movement, particularly the action of walking or traveling, as originally depicted by the more conservative form 𣥆. Over time, the bottom component has been stylized as 龰, forming the current representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他辵在乡(鄉)间(間)的小路上。
    - Tā chuò zài xiāngjiān de xiǎolù shàng.
    - He walks on the rural path.
  - 晨光洒(灑)满(滿)大地，他辵出门(門)开(開)始旅程。
    - Chén guāng sǎ mǎn dàdì, tā chuò chūmén kāishǐ lǚchéng.
    - As the morning light fills the earth, he sets out to begin his journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辵](@media/glyph8fb5.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵 → 彳
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** chì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a foot or person walking
  - **interpretation:** 彳(chì, 'walking') visually represents steps or a person moving, suggesting the idea of walking or movement. Despite a simplified history from characters like 行(xíng, 'walk'), its pictographic heritage directly connects with the notion of stepping or proceeding.
- **examples:**
  - 他喜欢(歡)在河边(邊)慢慢地走。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài hé biān mànmàn de zǒu.
    - He likes to walk slowly by the river.
  - 我们(們)每天退出喧嚣(囂)，享受安静(靜)的散步。
    - Wǒmen měitiān tuìchū xuānxiāo, xiǎngshòu ānjìng de sànbù.
    - We withdraw from the hustle and bustle every day to enjoy a quiet walk.
  - 他常常独(獨)自彳亍于(於)公园(園)小径(徑)。
    - Tā chángcháng dúzì chìchù yú gōngyuán xiǎojìng.
    - He often walks alone on the park trails.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 彳](@media/glyph5f73.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 旅行 → 旅 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 旅行 → 行
- **definition:** to go; to walk; behavior; conduct
- **pinyin:** xíng
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - step
  - 亍
    - chù
    - step
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a symmetric depiction of a street intersection; simplified asymmetrically ->
    - 彳 (chì, "step") + 亍 (chù, "step")
  - **interpretation:** The character 行(xíng) visually represented a street intersection, with two symmetrical parts symbolizing the act of going or walking along paths. Despite its current breakdown into separate elements, it was originally a unified pictogram rather than a compound.
- **examples:**
  - 我行往学(學)校。
    - Wǒ xíng wǎng xuéxiào.
    - I go to school.
  - 他行于(於)青山之间(間)，徒步旅行至古城。
    - Tā xíng yú qīngshān zhī jiān, túbù lǚxíng zhì gǔchéng.
    - He walks among the green mountains and hikes to the ancient city.
  - 他们(們)行在林间(間)小路上。
    - Tāmen xíng zài línjiān xiǎolù shàng.
    - They walk on the forest trail.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 行](@media/glyph884c.png)
### 旅行 → 行 → 彳
- **definition:** step
- **pinyin:** chì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a foot or person walking
  - **interpretation:** 彳(chì, 'walking') visually represents steps or a person moving, suggesting the idea of walking or movement. Despite a simplified history from characters like 行(xíng, 'walk'), its pictographic heritage directly connects with the notion of stepping or proceeding.
- **examples:**
  - 他喜欢(歡)在河边(邊)慢慢地走。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài hé biān mànmàn de zǒu.
    - He likes to walk slowly by the river.
  - 我们(們)每天退出喧嚣(囂)，享受安静(靜)的散步。
    - Wǒmen měitiān tuìchū xuānxiāo, xiǎngshòu ānjìng de sànbù.
    - We withdraw from the hustle and bustle every day to enjoy a quiet walk.
  - 他常常独(獨)自彳亍于(於)公园(園)小径(徑)。
    - Tā chángcháng dúzì chìchù yú gōngyuán xiǎojìng.
    - He often walks alone on the park trails.

### 旅行 → 行 → 亍
- **definition:** step
- **pinyin:** chù
- **components:**
  - 行
    - háng
    - walk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Derived from 行 (háng, 'walk') ->
    - right component of 行 ->
    - represents stepping
  - **interpretation:** 亍 (chù, 'step') retains a visual resemblance to 行 (háng, 'walk'), particularly the right side, symbolizing a step or small movement.
- **historical forms:**

## 玩
---
## to have fun; to play
### wán
---
- **definition:** to have fun; to play
- **pinyin:** wán
- **components:**
  - 玉
    - yù
    - jade
  - 元
    - yuán
    - origin
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 玉 (yù, "jade") + 元 (yuán, "origin") =
    - jade toys (ancient) ->
    - playing, having fun
  - **interpretation:** The character 玩(wán) associates the idea of valuable jade 玉 with 元, reflecting the historical use of jade objects in play or as toys, symbolizing amusement or leisure.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)去玩吧。
    - Wǒmen qù wán ba.
    - Let's go have fun.
  - 孩子们(們)在公园(園)玩游(遊)戏(戲)。
    - Háizimen zài gōngyuán wán yóuxì.
    - The children play games in the park.
  - 周(週)末到了，我们(們)全家一起玩。
    - Zhōumò dàole, wǒmen quánjiā yīqǐ wán.
    - The weekend has arrived, and our whole family plays together.
### 玩 → 玉
- **definition:** jade
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a picture of a cong (琮), a sort of ritual jade totem ->
    - dot added to differentiate from 王 (wáng, "king") ->
    - final form 玉 (yù, "jade")
  - **interpretation:** The character represents a picture of a jade cong, emphasizing its role in rituals and its cultural significance. The image eventually included a distinguishing dot to ensure clarity from similar characters like 王, underscoring the value jade held as a material in ancient contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 她收到了一个漂亮的玉手镯(鐲)。
    - Tā shōu dào le yī gè piàoliang de yù shǒuzhuó.
    - She received a beautiful jade bracelet.
  - 皇帝的王冠上镶(鑲)嵌着(著)闪(閃)耀的玉石。
    - Huángdì de wángguān shàng xiāngqiànzhe shǎnyào de yùshí.
    - The emperor's crown was inlaid with shining jade stones.
  - 古代的玉器常常被视(視)为(為)珍贵(貴)的艺(藝)术(術)品。
    - Gǔdài de yùqì chángcháng bèi shìwéi zhēnguì de yìshùpǐn.
    - Ancient jade artifacts are often regarded as precious works of art.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 玉](@media/glyph7389.png)
### 玩 → 元
- **definition:** origin
- **pinyin:** yuán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a human head above a horizontal line, symbolizing the origin or the head of something
  - **interpretation:** 元 (yuán, 'origin') represents the head, which is often considered the starting point or leader, aligning with the concept of 'origin'. This setup also connects metaphorically to beginnings or first principles.
- **examples:**
  - 万(萬)物之元来(來)自于(於)混沌。
    - Wànwù zhī yuán láizì yú húndùn.
    - The origin of all things comes from chaos.
  - 道家的理念追寻(尋)心灵(靈)的元。
    - Dàojiā de lǐniàn zhuīxún xīnlíng de yuán.
    - Taoist philosophy seeks the origin of the soul.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 元](@media/glyph5143.png)
---
## 玩
### wán

## 住
---
## to live
### zhù
---
- **definition:** to live
- **pinyin:** zhù
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 主
    - zhǔ
    - master
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亻(亻, "person") as semantic + 主(主, "master") as phonetic ->
    - to live
  - **interpretation:** The character 住 (zhù, "to live") combines the semantic component 亻 (rén, "person") with the phonetic component 主 (zhǔ, "master"). The person radical indicates the action done by a person, specifically residing or living in a place, while 主 provides the sound. This combination suggests a person staying or residing, reinforcing the concept of dwelling or living.
- **examples:**
  - 我住在北京。
    - Wǒ zhù zài Běijīng.
    - I live in Beijing.
  - 他们(們)住在山上，每天都能看到美丽(麗)的日出。
    - Tāmen zhù zài shān shàng, měitiān dōu néng kàn dào měilì de rìchū.
    - They live on the mountain and can see the beautiful sunrise every day.
  - 他曾经(經)住在英国(國)，后(後)来(來)搬到了日本。
    - Tā céngjīng zhù zài Yīngguó, hòulái bān dào le Rìběn.
    - He used to live in the UK, then moved to Japan.
### 住 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座城市里(裡)住着(著)很多优(優)秀的人。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.
    - There are many outstanding people living in this city.
  - 每个(個)人都有梦(夢)想。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 住 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 住 → 主
- **definition:** master
- **pinyin:** zhǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a torch with a flame on top, symbolizing guidance or leadership
  - **interpretation:** The character 主 (zhǔ, "master") represents a torch with a flame, symbolizing a guiding or leading figure, akin to a master or lord providing direction.
- **examples:**
  - 他是我们(們)家的主。
    - Tā shì wǒmen jiā de zhǔ.
    - He is the master of our family.
  - 僧侣(侶)虔诚(誠)祷(禱)告主。
    - Sēnglǚ qiánchéng dǎogào zhǔ.
    - The monks devoutly prayed to the Lord.
  - 臣子忠心辅(輔)佐主。
    - Chénzi zhōngxīn fǔzuǒ zhǔ.
    - The ministers loyally assist their master.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 主](@media/glyph4e3b.png)

## 介绍(紹)
---
## to introduce
### jièshào
---
- **traditional:** 介紹
- **definition:** to introduce
- **pinyin:** jièshào
- **components:**
  - 介
    - jiè
    - to mediate; intermediate
  - 绍(紹)
    - shào
    - to continue; to connect
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 介 (jiè, "to mediate; intermediate") + 绍(紹) (shào, "to continue; to connect") =
    - action of mediating and connecting ->
    - introducing
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 介 (jiè, "to mediate; intermediate") and 绍(紹) (shào, "to continue; to connect") represents the idea of serving as an intermediary to connect people or ideas, which is the essence of introducing someone or something.
- **examples:**
  - 我介绍(紹)一下。
    - Wǒ jièshào yīxià.
    - Let me introduce (someone).
  - 我介绍(紹)我的朋友，你就听(聽)他的。
    - Wǒ jièshào wǒ de péngyǒu, nǐ jiù tīng tā de.
    - I introduce my friend, then you can listen to him.
  - 老师(師)给(給)我们(們)介绍(紹)历(歷)史，让(讓)我们(們)了解过(過)去。
    - Lǎoshī gěi wǒmen jièshào lìshǐ, ràng wǒmen liǎojiě guòqù.
    - The teacher introduces history to us, letting us understand the past.
### 介绍(紹) → 介
- **definition:** to mediate; intermediate
- **pinyin:** jiè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person standing between two lines or boundaries
  - **interpretation:** The character 介 (jiè, 'to derive an idea from') represents the concept of being in-between or acting as a mediator. It conceptually fits the idea of deriving by positioning oneself between different ideas or entities.
- **examples:**
  - 他从(從)古代诗(詩)词(詞)中介出艺(藝)术(術)灵(靈)感。
    - Tā cóng gǔdài shīcí zhōng jiè chū yìshù línggǎn.
    - He derives artistic inspiration from ancient poems.
  - 科学(學)家阅(閱)读(讀)文献(獻)时(時)介出创(創)新思想，工程师(師)从(從)实(實)验(驗)结(結)果中介出改进(進)方案。
    - Kēxuéjiā yuèdú wénxiàn shí jiè chū chuàngxīn sīxiǎng, gōngchéngshī cóng shíyàn jiéguǒ zhōng jiè chū gǎijìn fāng'àn.
    - Scientists derive innovative ideas when reading literature, and engineers derive improvement plans from experimental results.
  - 研究者从(從)历(歷)史资(資)料中介出重要信(資)息(訊)。
    - Yánjiū zhě cóng lìshǐ zīliào zhōng jiè chū zhòngyào xìnxī.
    - Researchers derive key information from historical data.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 介](@media/glyph4ecb.png)
### 介绍(紹) → 绍(紹)
- **traditional:** 紹
- **definition:** to continue; to connect
- **pinyin:** shào
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk
  - 召
    - zhào
    - to summon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (mì, "silk") + 召 (zhào, "to summon") =
    - threading through like summoning ->
    - to continue or connect
  - **interpretation:** The character 紹 (shào, "to continue") combines 糸 (mì, "silk") representing continuity or connection through threads, with 召 (zhào, "to summon") as the phonetic element, suggesting the idea of threading or extending threads to maintain continuity.
  - **simplification:** The simplified form 绍(紹) uses the more familiar 召 for its phonetic component in place of the more intricate 紹 radical and phonetic, retaining overall readability.
- **examples:**
  - 他绍(紹)古人的智慧。
    - Tā shào gǔrén de zhìhuì.
    - He continues the wisdom of the ancients.
  - 博物馆(館)展示文物，绍(紹)起千年文化。
    - Bówùguǎn zhǎnshì wénwù, shào qǐ qiānnián wénhuà.
    - The museum exhibits cultural relics, connecting a millennium of culture.
### 介绍(紹) → 绍(紹) → 糸
- **definition:** silk
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 糸](@media/glyph7cf8.png)
### 介绍(紹) → 绍(紹) → 召
- **definition:** to summon
- **pinyin:** zhào
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - original hands over a wine vessel ->
    - phonetic 刀 (dāo) + semantic 口 (kǒu, 'mouth') ->
    - summon
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 召 depicted hands over a wine vessel, linked to the practice of serving wine to guests. The character evolved by adding a phonetic component 刀 (dāo) and a semantic component 口 (kǒu, 'mouth'). The mouth element implies calling out, and the knife contributes the zhào sound. The meaning extended to 'summoning' due to both calling out and the attentiveness required in serving. The concept of welcoming and calling guests informs its modern sense of summoning or calling.
- **examples:**
  - 国(國)王召集大臣们(們)商讨(討)对(對)策。
    - Guówáng zhàojí dàchénmen shāngtǎo duìcè.
    - The king summoned the ministers to discuss strategies.
  - 他被召回故乡(鄉)接受新的任务(務)。
    - Tā bèi zhào huí gùxiāng jiēshòu xīn de rènwù.
    - He was called back to his hometown to accept a new assignment.
  - 战(戰)争(爭)爆发(發)后(後)，军(軍)队(隊)迅速召集士兵。
    - Zhànzhēng bàofā hòu, jūnduì xùnsù zhàojí shìbīng.
    - After the outbreak of war, the army quickly summoned soldiers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 召](@media/glyph53ec.png)
### 介绍(紹) → 绍(紹) → 召 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 刀](@media/glyph5200.png)
### 介绍(紹) → 绍(紹) → 召 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)

### jièshào

## 下午
---
## afternoon
### xiàwǔ
---
- **definition:** afternoon
- **pinyin:** xiàwǔ
- **components:**
  - 下
    - xià
    - below; under; next time
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - noon; midday
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 下 (xià, "below") + 午 (wǔ, "noon") =
    - the period after noon
  - **interpretation:** 下 (xià, "below") indicates a position after or below in sequence, and 午 (wǔ, "noon") refers to the middle of the day. Thus, in 上午, their combination suggests the 'afternoon,' being the time below or after noon.
- **examples:**
  - 下午，我和朋友去看电(電)影。
    - Xiàwǔ, wǒ hé péngyǒu qù kàn diànyǐng.
    - In the afternoon, my friend and I go to watch a movie.
  - 每天的下午，他都去公园(園)散步。
    - Měitiān de xiàwǔ, tā dōu qù gōngyuán sànbù.
    - Every afternoon, he goes to the park for a walk.
  - 我们(們)将(將)在下午开(開)会(會)。
    - Wǒmen jiāng zài xiàwǔ kāihuì.
    - We will have a meeting in the afternoon.
### 下午 → 下
- **definition:** below; under; next time
- **pinyin:** xià
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - a line below another ->
    - later evolved into 下
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, 'down') is an ideogram showing a line positioned below another line, visually representing 'below' or 'downward'. This layout intuitively depicts the concept of being beneath or beneath another object.
- **examples:**
  - 水从(從)山上流下。
    - Shuǐ cóng shān shàng liú xià.
    - The water flows down from the mountain.
  - 他坐下来(來)看书(書)。
    - Tā zuò xià lái kàn shū.
    - He sits down to read a book.
  - 请(請)把箱子放在地下。
    - Qǐng bǎ xiāngzi fàng zài dìxià.
    - Please put the box down on the ground.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 下](@media/glyph4e0b.png)
### 下午 → 午
- **definition:** noon; midday
- **pinyin:** wǔ
- **components:**
  - 杵
    - chǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: Depicts a pestle (modern 杵 (chǔ, "pestle")) ->
    - original meaning unrelated to time concepts
  - **interpretation:** 午 (wǔ, "noon") originally depicted a pestle, but over time it was borrowed for usage in the context of time. Despite its current association with noon, its visual origin is agricultural, related to pounding or grinding.
- **examples:**
  - 中午时(時)分，阳(陽)光灿(燦)烂(爛)。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, yángguāng cànlàn.
    - At noon, the sunlight is brilliant.
  - 我在午休中，享受宁(寧)静(靜)。
    - Wǒ zài wǔxiū zhōng, xiǎngshòu níngjìng.
    - I enjoy tranquility during my noon break.
  - 午餐后(後)，公园(園)里(裡)热(熱)闹(鬧)非凡。
    - Wǔcān hòu, gōngyuán lǐ rènào fēifán.
    - After lunch, the park is bustling.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 午](@media/glyph5348.png)
### 下午 → 午 → 杵
- **definition:** pestle
- **pinyin:** chǔ
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 午 (wǔ, "pestle") ->
    - a wooden pestle
  - **interpretation:** Combines 木 (mù, "wood"), which signifies that the object is made of wood, with 午 (wǔ, "pestle") serving as the phonetic component to suggest the word's pronunciation. The character effectively depicts a pestle made from wood, as was traditionally used.
- **examples:**
  - 他用杵捣(搗)碎坚(堅)果。
    - Tā yòng chǔ dǎosuì jiānguǒ.
    - He used a pestle to crush the nuts.
  - 这(這)根杵是用来(來)捣(搗)蒜的。
    - Zhè gēn chǔ shì yòng lái dǎo suàn de.
    - This pestle is used for crushing garlic.
  - 传(傳)统(統)上，杵和臼一起使用来(來)制(製)作药(藥)物。
    - Chuántǒng shàng, chǔ hé jiù yìqǐ shǐyòng lái zhìzuò yàowù.
    - Traditionally, a pestle is used with a mortar to make medicine.
### 下午 → 午 → 杵 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
---
## 下午
### xiàwǔ

## 中午
---
## noon
### zhōngwǔ
---
- **definition:** noon
- **pinyin:** zhōngwǔ
- **components:**
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - noon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 中 (zhōng, "middle") + 午 (wǔ, "noon") =
    - middle of noon ->
    - noon
  - **interpretation:** The term 中午 (zhōngwǔ, "noon") combines 中 (zhōng, "middle") and 午 (wǔ, "noon") to describe the middle part of the day, typically around 12 PM when the sun is highest in the sky.
- **examples:**
  - 中午十二点(點)吃饭(飯)。
    - zhōngwǔ shí'èr diǎn chīfàn.
    - I eat lunch at noon.
  - 中午太阳(陽)高悬(懸)，公园(園)里(裡)的人们(們)在休息。
    - zhōngwǔ tàiyáng gāoxuán, gōngyuán lǐ de rénmen zài xiūxí.
    - The midday sun hangs high, and people in the park are resting.
  - 中午时(時)分，是休息时(時)间(間)。
    - zhōngwǔ shífēn, shì xiūxí shíjiān.
    - Noon time is the time for rest.
### 中午 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 中午 → 午
- **definition:** noon
- **pinyin:** wǔ
- **components:**
  - 杵
    - chǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: Depicts a pestle (modern 杵 (chǔ, "pestle")) ->
    - original meaning unrelated to time concepts
  - **interpretation:** 午 (wǔ, "noon") originally depicted a pestle, but over time it was borrowed for usage in the context of time. Despite its current association with noon, its visual origin is agricultural, related to pounding or grinding.
- **examples:**
  - 中午时(時)分，阳(陽)光灿(燦)烂(爛)。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, yángguāng cànlàn.
    - At noon, the sunlight is brilliant.
  - 我在午休中，享受宁(寧)静(靜)。
    - Wǒ zài wǔxiū zhōng, xiǎngshòu níngjìng.
    - I enjoy tranquility during my noon break.
  - 午餐后(後)，公园(園)里(裡)热(熱)闹(鬧)非凡。
    - Wǔcān hòu, gōngyuán lǐ rènào fēifán.
    - After lunch, the park is bustling.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 午](@media/glyph5348.png)
### 中午 → 午 → 杵
- **definition:** pestle
- **pinyin:** chǔ
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 午 (wǔ, "pestle") ->
    - a wooden pestle
  - **interpretation:** Combines 木 (mù, "wood"), which signifies that the object is made of wood, with 午 (wǔ, "pestle") serving as the phonetic component to suggest the word's pronunciation. The character effectively depicts a pestle made from wood, as was traditionally used.
- **examples:**
  - 他用杵捣(搗)碎坚(堅)果。
    - Tā yòng chǔ dǎosuì jiānguǒ.
    - He used a pestle to crush the nuts.
  - 这(這)根杵是用来(來)捣(搗)蒜的。
    - Zhè gēn chǔ shì yòng lái dǎo suàn de.
    - This pestle is used for crushing garlic.
  - 传(傳)统(統)上，杵和臼一起使用来(來)制(製)作药(藥)物。
    - Chuántǒng shàng, chǔ hé jiù yìqǐ shǐyòng lái zhìzuò yàowù.
    - Traditionally, a pestle is used with a mortar to make medicine.
### 中午 → 午 → 杵 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)

## 小时(時)
---
## hour
### xiǎoshí
---
- **traditional:** 小時
- **definition:** hour
- **pinyin:** xiǎoshí
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small; little; young; minor
  - 时(時)
    - shí
    - time; hour; season; o'clock
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 小 (xiǎo, "small") + 时(時) (shí, "time")
  - **interpretation:** The word 小时(時) (xiǎoshí, "hour") combines 小 (xiǎo, "small") and 时(時) (shí, "time") to denote a 'small unit of time,' which is an 'hour.' This formation reflects the partitioning of time into smaller segments within a day.
- **examples:**
  - 我工作八个(個)小时(時)。
    - Wǒ gōngzuò bā gè xiǎoshí.
    - I work eight hours.
  - 电(電)影持续(續)两(兩)个(個)小时(時)。
    - Diànyǐng chíxù liǎng gè xiǎoshí.
    - The movie lasts two hours.
  - 会(會)议(議)开(開)了三个(個)小时(時)。
    - Huìyì kāile sān gè xiǎoshí.
    - The meeting lasted three hours.
### 小时(時) → 小
- **definition:** small; little; young; minor
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小猫(貓)很可爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座小桥(橋)横(橫)跨河流，连(連)接两(兩)岸。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我一小杯水。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 小](@media/glyph5c0f.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時)
- **traditional:** 時
- **definition:** time; hour; season; o'clock
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun; day
  - 寺
    - sì
    - temple
  - 之
    - zhī
    - governing
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, 'sun; day') as semantic + 寺 as phonetic ->
    - associated with time; ancient form 旹 with 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing'), referring to the passing of time ->
    - over time, 寸 (cùn, 'inch') added to form current 時
  - **interpretation:** The character 時 (shí, 'time; season') stems from the interplay between 日 (rì, 'sun; day'), which signifies the passage of time marked by the sun, and 寺 as the phonetic component capturing the sound. The historical forms show an evolution from 旹, merging 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing') to imply governance over time, to its modern form, where 寸 ('inch') likely emphasizes precision or measurement in the concept of time.
  - **simplification:** In 时 (shí), the component 寺 was retained for phonetic purposes, while 日 (rì, 'sun; day') was simplified to resemble 日 with fewer strokes, streamlining the character.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)相识(識)时(時)，天已经(經)暗了。
    - Wǒmen xiāngshí shí, tiān yǐjīng àn le.
    - When we met, the sky was already dark.
  - 在这(這)样(樣)的时(時)刻，我们(們)需要团(團)结(結)。
    - Zài zhèyàng de shíkè, wǒmen xūyào tuánjié.
    - At such a time, we need to unite.
  - 时(時)光流逝，童年的回忆(憶)依然鲜(鮮)活。
    - Shíguāng liúshì, tóngnián de huíyì yīrán xiānhuó.
    - As time passes, childhood memories remain vivid.
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 日
- **definition:** sun; day
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺
- **definition:** temple
- **pinyin:** sì
- **components:**
  - 𡳿
    - zhī
    - to go; footprint
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 𡳿 ->
    - 之; 士 + semantic 又 (hand) ->
    - 寸 in Small Seal Script ->
    - 寺
  - **interpretation:** 寺(sì, 'temple') combines the semantic element 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), originally from 又 (yòu, 'hand'), to imply precision or holding, with the phonetic element that evolved into 士 (shì, 'scholar'). The phonetic component originally represented going or movement but later took on a more abstract form. This combination suggests a place of order and ritual, characteristic of temples.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天早晨去寺庙(廟)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎochén qù sìmiào.
    - He goes to the temple every morning.
  - 寺庙(廟)里(裡)的钟(鐘)声(聲)非常悠扬(揚)。
    - Sìmiào lǐ de zhōngshēng fēicháng yōuyáng.
    - The bell sounds in the temple are very melodious.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了京都的古老寺庙(廟)，觉(覺)得很平静(靜)。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle Jīngdū de gǔlǎo sìmiào, juéde hěn píngjìng.
    - We visited an ancient temple in Kyoto and felt very peaceful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寺](@media/glyph5bfa.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿
- **definition:** to go; footprint
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - the beginning place
  - 之
    - zhī
    - to go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止(“foot”) + 一(“the beginning place”) ->
    - originally 㞢 ->
    - similar to 出 ->
    - evolved as a variant of 之
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡳿 is a variant of 之 (zhī, "to go") and conveys the idea of movement or direction. The original form 㞢 combines 止 (zhǐ, "foot") representing a footprint with 一 (yī, "the beginning place"), symbolizing the commencement of movement or journey, leading to the meaning of 'to go'. Over time, components such as the footprint evolved into different forms, leading to variants such as 𡳿.
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 一
- **definition:** the beginning place
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 之
- **definition:** to go
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; the beginning place
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 ('foot') + 一 ('beginning place') ->
    - originally 㞢 ('to go') ->
    - simplified to a point
  - **interpretation:** The original compound 㞢 depicted a foot 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') stepping on a line 一 (yī, 'one; the beginning place'), indicating the concept of 'to go'. The footprint evolving into a point symbolized direction or movement, ultimately abstracted into 之 (zhī, 'of; possessive particle'), representing directionality or connection, as in 'of'.
- **examples:**
  - 天空之蓝(藍)让(讓)人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Tiānkōng zhī lán ràng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the sky makes people feel relaxed and happy.
  - 树(樹)之影在湖面上摇(搖)曳。
    - Shù zhī yǐng zài húmiàn shàng yáoyè.
    - The shadow of the tree sways on the surface of the lake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 之](@media/glyph4e4b.png)
### 小时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数(數)据(據)都准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)

## hour
